# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Evidence of Higgs boson inclusive production at high transverse momentum decaying to a pair of $b$-quarks with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19369)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文首次报告了在高横动量（p_T > 450 GeV）下希格斯玻色子在b\bar{b}末态中产生的证据，通过单一大半径喷注重建，观测到3.8σ显著性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高横动量（high transverse momentum）区域希格斯玻色子的产生，这对于检验标准模型（Standard Model）预测和理解希格斯玻色子与重夸克的耦合具有重要意义。

Method: 利用ATLAS探测器在大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider）上记录的质子-质子对撞数据，总积分亮度为301 fb⁻¹。采用基于Transformer的喷注识别算法进行背景抑制，并使用专用回归模型提高质量和横动量分辨率。

Result: 在p_T > 450 GeV区域测得希格斯玻色子产额相对于标准模型预测的比值为1.53±0.27(统计误差)⁺⁰·³³₋₀·₂₇(系统误差)±0.17(理论误差)，观测显著性为3.8σ（预期为2.5σ）。三个p_T区间的结果均与标准模型预测兼容。

Conclusion: 首次在高横动量区域观测到希格斯玻色子在b\bar{b}末态中产生的证据，结果与标准模型预测一致，验证了基于Transformer的喷注识别算法和回归模型的有效性。

Abstract: This letter reports on the first evidence of Higgs-boson production at high transverse momentum in the $b\bar{b}$ final state, reconstructed in a single large-radius jet. The results are based on proton proton collision data recorded by the ATLAS detector at the Large Hadron Collider at a centre-of-mass energies of 13 TeV and 13.6 TeV, corresponding to a total integrated luminosity of 301 fb$^{-1}$. The study profits from the large background suppression provided by the use of a new transformer-based algorithm for jet identification and the sharper mass and transverse momentum, $p_{\text{T}}$, resolution from a dedicated regression model. The yield relative to the Standard Model prediction, for Higgs bosons produced at $p_{\text{T}}$ larger than 450 GeV is measured to be $1.53\pm 0.27\text{(stat.)}\ ^{+0.33}_{-0.27}\text{(syst.)}\pm 0.17\text{(theo.)}$ corresponding to an observed (expected) significance of $3.8σ(2.5σ)$ relative to the background-only hypothesis. Results are also obtained in three Higgs boson $p_{\text{T}}$ intervals and found to be compatible with Standard Model predictions.

</details>


### [2] [Measurement of the transverse-momentum fraction of strange hadrons from jet-like correlation structures in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19387)
*ALICE Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: ALICE合作组首次测量了pp碰撞中奇异重子（Λ/Λ̄）和奇异介子（K_S^0）的平均横向动量分数⟨z⟩随横向动量p_T的变化关系，揭示了二者不同的强子化机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过测量奇异重子（Λ和Λ̄）和奇异介子（K_S^0）的平均横向动量分数⟨z⟩随p_T的变化，探究不同奇异强子的强子化机制（hadronization mechanisms）。

Method: 采用新颖方法，通过角关联（angular correlation）定义mini-jets，利用奇异强子与包含性带电强子（inclusive charged hadrons）之间的角关联，并以小角度距离下关联粒子的p_T进行加权，获得⟨z⟩随p_T的分布。

Result: 在测量的p_T范围内，奇异介子（K_S^0）的⟨z⟩呈现平坦趋势，而奇异重子（Λ/Λ̄）则呈现下降趋势，表明二者具有不同的强子化机制。与PYTHIA 8（Monash和Color Rope调谐）及AMPT（string melting）模型的比较显示，这些模型在低和中p_T区域均无法满意描述⟨z⟩分布。

Conclusion: 测量结果揭示了奇异介子和奇异重子具有不同的强子化机制，现有主流蒙特卡洛模型（PYTHIA 8和AMPT）在描述这些分布方面存在不足，为强子化机制的理论发展提供了新的实验约束。

Abstract: The first measurements of the average transverse-momentum fraction ($\langle z \rangle$) as a function of transverse momentum ($p_{\rm T}$) for strange baryons ($Λ$ and $\barΛ$) and strange mesons ($K_{\rm S}^0$), produced in mini-jets defined through angular correlations in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV, are reported by the ALICE Collaboration at the LHC. The observable is obtained using a novel method, where the angular correlation between the strange hadrons and inclusive charged hadrons is weighted by the $p_{\rm T}$ of correlated particles at small angular distance. As a function of strange particles' $p_{\rm T}$, the results reveal a flat trend for strange mesons and a decreasing trend for strange baryons in the measured $p_{\rm T}$ region, indicating distinct hadronization mechanisms for $K_{\rm S}^0$ and $Λ$($\barΛ$). The measurements are compared to Monte Carlo models, namely PYTHIA~8 (with both Monash and Color Rope tunes) and the AMPT (A Multi-Phase Transport) model with string melting. None of these models provides a satisfactory description of the $\langle z \rangle$ distributions at low and intermediate $p_{\rm T}$.

</details>


### [3] [Higgs Self-Coupling Measurement at a Linear Collider at 550 GeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19884)
*Mikael Berggren,Bryan Bliewert,Jenny List,Dimitris Ntounis,Taikan Suehara,Junping Tian,Julie Munch Torndal,Caterina Vernieri*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究基于ILD探测器概念，通过更新模拟分析技术（包括风味标记和运动学重建改进），重新评估了在550 GeV对撞能量下双希格斯产生过程对三线性希格斯自耦合（trilinear Higgs self-coupling）的测量灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 希格斯机制（Higgs mechanism）是标准模型（Standard Model, SM）成功的关键，通过测量希格斯自耦合（Higgs self-coupling）可实验验证该机制。任何与标准模型预测的偏差都可能暗示超出标准模型（beyond the SM）的新物理，并为扩展希格斯模型提供指导。

Method: 研究采用最新的ILD探测器概念模拟，结合快速SGV（Simulation a Grande Vitesse）模拟技术，在包含完整标准模型背景的条件下进行分析。方法整合了风味标记（flavour tagging）和运动学重建（kinematic reconstruction）等先进重建与分析工具的预期改进，并基于2014年的全模拟分析进行外推。

Result: 在550 GeV质心能量下，双希格斯产生（double-Higgs production）的主要模式来自双希格斯辐射（di-Higgs strahlung），WW融合（WW-fusion）贡献较小。该过程在树图水平（tree-level）对三线性希格斯自耦合敏感，研究展示了基于最新ILD预测的最新分析结果。

Conclusion: 通过整合先进的重建与分析工具，并基于更新的模拟技术重新分析，该研究为在电子-正电子对撞机上通过双希格斯产生过程精确测量希格斯自耦合提供了最新的灵敏度预测，这对于验证标准模型和探索新物理至关重要。

Abstract: The Higgs mechanism is essential for the success of the Standard Model (SM) and can be experimentally verified with the determination of the Higgs self-coupling. As the simplest model of a Higgs potential, the SM provides a clear prediction of the Higgs self-coupling in terms of the Higgs boson mass and the vacuum expectation value. Any deviations would indicate physics beyond the SM and help guide extended Higgs models. At large enough centre-of-mass energies, double-Higgs production provides tree-level sensitivity to the trilinear Higgs self-coupling. At 550 GeV the leading production mode in $e^+e^-$ comes from di-Higgs strahlung with a small contribution from $WW$-fusion. The most up-to-date ILD projections are extrapolated based on a full simulation analysis from 2014 by incorporating expected improvements in flavour tagging and kinematic reconstruction for event selection, and are presented in this contribution together with the ongoing re-analysis using fast SGV (Simulation a Grande Vitesse) simulations of the ILD detector concept on a full SM background including the aforementioned state-of-the-art reconstruction and analysis tools.

</details>


### [4] [Measurement of the jet mass in hadronic decays of boosted W bosons at 13 TeV and extraction of the W boson mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19963)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: CMS实验在13 TeV质子-质子对撞中测量了W玻色子衰变为夸克-反夸克对时的喷注质量（jet mass），首次给出了双微分截面作为喷注横向动量和软降质量的函数，并从中提取了W玻色子质量80.83 ± 0.55 GeV，这是强子对撞机全喷注末态中目前最小的不确定度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高动量W玻色子的强子衰变由于洛伦兹助推（Lorentz boost）效应产生高度准直的衰变产物，这些产物被重建为单个大半径喷注。研究这些喷注的质量分布对于理解W玻色子性质及其在强子对撞环境中的产生机制具有重要意义。

Method: 使用CMS实验在LHC收集的138 fb⁻¹积分亮度数据，通过软降算法（soft-drop algorithm）计算喷注质量，该算法抑制导致喷注质量分布展宽的软大角度辐射。利用喷注的特定子结构特征来区分W玻色子喷注与夸克和胶子引发的背景喷注。

Result: 首次展示了W+喷注双微分截面作为喷注横向动量（transverse momentum）和软降质量函数的展开测量结果。从这些分布中提取的W玻色子质量为80.83 ± 0.55 GeV，这是目前强子对撞机全喷注末态中获得的最小不确定度测量结果。

Conclusion: 该研究成功测量了W玻色子喷注质量分布，并通过双微分截面分析精确提取了W玻色子质量，为强子对撞环境中全喷注末态的W玻色子研究提供了重要基准，展示了软降算法在喷注质量测量中的有效性。

Abstract: The jet mass of W bosons decaying to a quark-antiquark pair is measured in W+jets events from proton-proton collisions at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV. The data used were collected by the CMS experiment at the CERN LHC and correspond to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. Hadronic decays of W bosons with high momenta produce strongly collimated decay products due to the large Lorentz boost, and are reconstructed as single large-radius jets. These jets have a characteristic substructure that is exploited to distinguish them from the large background of quark- and gluon-initiated jets. The jet mass is computed using the soft-drop algorithm, which suppresses soft wide-angle radiation that leads to a broadening of the jet mass distribution. For the first time, unfolded measurements are presented of the double-differential W+jets cross section as a function of the jet transverse momentum and soft-drop mass. From these distributions, the W boson mass is obtained, with a value of 80.83 $\pm$ 0.55 GeV, achieving the smallest uncertainty available today from an all-jets final state at a hadron collider.

</details>


### [5] [Search for anomalies in vector-boson fusion production of the Higgs boson in $H(\rightarrow γγ) jj$ events using 164 fb$^{-1}$ of $pp$ collision data collected at $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20087)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文基于ATLAS实验在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上记录的164 fb⁻¹质子-质子碰撞数据，通过矢量玻色子融合（VBF）产生模式和γγjj末态，对希格斯玻色子性质进行了两项研究：一是约束超出标准模型（SM）的CP-odd耦合，二是探测希格斯玻色子与纵向和横向极化W/Z玻色子的耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于利用矢量玻色子融合（vector-boson fusion, VBF）产生模式和γγjj末态，深入探索希格斯玻色子的性质。具体包括：在标准模型有效场论（Standard Model Effective Field Theory, SMEFT）框架内约束超出标准模型的CP-odd耦合，以及探测希格斯玻色子与不同极化状态的矢量玻色子之间的耦合强度。

Method: 研究方法包括：第一项研究采用基于矩阵元（matrix element-based）的最优可观测量（optimal observables），在Warsaw基下约束CP-odd耦合；第二项研究利用角分布（angular distributions）探测希格斯玻色子与纵向和横向极化W/Z玻色子的耦合。通过结合先前在13 TeV、140 fb⁻¹数据样本中的γγjj事件分析结果，并实施新的基于神经网络（neural network-based）的分类算法来最大化灵敏度。

Result: 研究结果显示，通过实施新的神经网络分类算法，相对于先前分析取得了显著改进。所有测量结果均与标准模型预测一致：希格斯玻色子为CP-even，且与纵向和横向极化矢量玻色子的相对耦合强度符合预期。

Conclusion: 结论表明，基于ATLAS实验在√s=13.6 TeV、164 fb⁻¹数据样本中的分析，两项希格斯玻色子性质研究均支持标准模型预测。通过结合先前数据和改进的神经网络算法，显著提升了CP-odd耦合约束的灵敏度，并验证了希格斯玻色子与不同极化矢量玻色子耦合的相对强度。

Abstract: This article details two studies of Higgs boson properties using the vector-boson fusion production mode and the $γγjj$ final state. Both efforts are based on a data sample corresponding to 164 fb$^{-1}$ of $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV proton--proton collisions recorded by the ATLAS experiment at the Large Hadron Collider. The first study employs matrix element-based optimal observables to constrain CP-odd couplings beyond the Standard Model within the Standard Model Effective Field Theory framework, expressed in the Warsaw basis. The second study exploits angular distributions to probe the Higgs boson's couplings to longitudinally and transversely polarised $W$ and $Z$ bosons in the production of the Higgs boson. To maximise the sensitivity, the constraints of the CP-odd couplings are combined with those from a previous analysis performed in $γγjj$ events in a data sample of proton--proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 140 fb$^{-1}$. A significant improvement with respect to the previous analysis is achieved through the implementation of a new neural network-based classification algorithm. All measurements are in agreement with the Standard Model prediction of a CP-even Higgs boson with the expected relative coupling strengths to longitudinally and transversely polarised vector bosons.

</details>


### [6] [Combination of measurements of CP properties of Higgs boson interactions with vector bosons using proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20117)
*The ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: ATLAS实验结合多个希格斯玻色子衰变道（H→ττ、WW*、γγ、ZZ*、WH/H→bb）的测量结果，在标准模型有效场论框架下对CP破坏算子设定约束，未观测到CP破坏证据，相关威尔逊系数限制达到迄今最严格水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过结合ATLAS探测器记录的多个希格斯玻色子衰变通道测量结果，系统检验希格斯玻色子与电弱规范玻色子相互作用的CP性质，并在标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）框架下对CP破坏算子设定约束。

Method: 研究结合了H→ττ、H→WW*、H→γγ、H→ZZ*以及WH/H→bb五个衰变通道的测量结果，使用ATLAS探测器在√s=13 TeV质子-质子对撞中收集的140 fb⁻¹数据，在标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）的华沙基（Warsaw basis）下分析CP破坏算子。

Result: 未观测到CP破坏的证据，对c_{H\tilde{W}}系数的限制比先前个体限制提高了40%以上，首次同时设定了c_{H\tilde{W}}、c_{H\tilde{B}}和c_{H\tilde{W}B}三个系数的约束，这些限制是迄今在SMEFT框架下对相关威尔逊系数（Wilson coefficients）最严格的约束。

Conclusion: 该组合分析显著提升了希格斯玻色子CP性质的测量精度，为标准模型有效场论框架下的CP破坏算子设定了迄今最严格的约束，具有最小的模型依赖性。

Abstract: A combination of measurements of the CP properties of Higgs boson interactions with electroweak gauge bosons is presented, using 140 fb$^{-1}$ of proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV recorded by the ATLAS detector. Results from $H\toττ$, $H\to WW^{*}$, $H\toγγ$, $H\to ZZ^{*}$, and $WH,H\to b\bar{b}$ channels are combined. No evidence of CP violation is observed, and constrains on the CP-violating operators in the SMEFT framework are set in the Warsaw basis. The results from the combination improve by over 40% on previous individual limits on $c_{H\tilde{W}}$ and, for the first time, simultaneous constraints on three coefficients $c_{H\tilde{W}}$, $c_{H\tilde{B}}$, and $c_{H\tilde{W}B}$ are set. This limits are the most stringent constraints to date on the relevant Wilson coefficients in the SMEFT framework with minimum model dependence.

</details>


### [7] [AI Agents Can Already Autonomously Perform Experimental High Energy Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20179)
*Eric A. Moreno,Samuel Bright-Thonney,Andrzej Novak,Dolores Garcia,Philip Harris*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究展示了基于大语言模型（large language model）的AI代理能够自主执行高能物理（high energy physics）分析流程的主要阶段，包括事件选择、背景估计、不确定性量化、统计推断和论文起草，仅需最小化的专家输入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前高能物理（HEP）社区低估了基于大语言模型的AI代理的实际能力，且多数提出的代理工作流程过于局限于特定分析结构。需要展示这些系统在自主执行完整HEP分析方面的真实潜力。

Method: 提出了概念验证框架"Just Furnish Context (JFC)"，该框架整合了自主分析代理、基于文献的知识检索和多代理评审机制。使用ALEPH、DELPHI和CMS的开放数据进行了电弱（electroweak）、QCD和希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）测量的分析演示。

Result: Claude Code成功自动化了典型分析的所有阶段：事件选择、背景估计、不确定性量化、统计推断和论文起草。JFC框架被证明足以规划、执行和记录可信的高能物理分析。

Conclusion: 这些工具旨在减轻分析代码开发的重复性技术负担，使研究人员能够专注于物理洞察、真正新颖的方法开发和严格验证。建议社区重新思考如何培训学生、组织分析工作和分配人类专业知识。

Abstract: Large language model-based AI agents are now able to autonomously execute substantial portions of a high energy physics (HEP) analysis pipeline with minimal expert-curated input. Given access to a HEP dataset, an execution framework, and a corpus of prior experimental literature, we find that Claude Code succeeds in automating all stages of a typical analysis: event selection, background estimation, uncertainty quantification, statistical inference, and paper drafting. We argue that the experimental HEP community is underestimating the current capabilities of these systems, and that most proposed agentic workflows are too narrowly scoped or scaffolded to specific analysis structures. We present a proof-of-concept framework, Just Furnish Context (JFC), that integrates autonomous analysis agents with literature-based knowledge retrieval and multi-agent review, and show that this is sufficient to plan, execute, and document a credible high energy physics analysis. We demonstrate this by conducting analyses on open data from ALEPH, DELPHI, and CMS to perform electroweak, QCD, and Higgs boson measurements. Rather than replacing physicists, these tools promise to offload the repetitive technical burden of analysis code development, freeing researchers to focus on physics insight, truly novel method development, and rigorous validation. Given these developments, we advocate for new strategies for how the community trains students, organizes analysis efforts, and allocates human expertise.

</details>

# math.ST [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [The monotonicity of the Franz-Parisi potential is equivalent with Low-degree MMSE lower bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20070)
*Konstantinos Tsirkas,Leda Wang,Ilias Zadik*

Main category: math.ST

TL;DR: 本文建立了统计物理中的Franz-Parisi势单调性与低阶多项式估计算法能力之间的数学等价关系，为理解统计估计问题的计算复杂性提供了统一的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 统计物理文献通过Franz-Parisi势的局部稳定性和单调性预测算法难度，而数学严谨文献通过低阶多项式估计器的局限性来刻画难度。这两种视角在许多推断模型中预测一致，但长期缺乏精确的数学关系。

Method: 针对高斯加性模型（Gaussian additive models, GAMs）家族，在信噪比λ条件下，证明了低阶多项式的能力与退火Franz-Parisi势的单调性之间的等价关系。

Result: 研究结果表明，在GAMs的低阶猜想前提下，这些模型的多项式时间极限直接由退火FP势的单调性所决定，这与自1990年代以来物理文献的预测在概念上一致。

Conclusion: 该工作为统计物理的Franz-Parisi势方法与数学严谨的低阶多项式方法之间建立了精确的数学联系，统一了两种理解统计估计计算复杂性的不同视角。

Abstract: Over the last decades, two distinct approaches have been instrumental to our understanding of the computational complexity of statistical estimation. The statistical physics literature predicts algorithmic hardness through local stability and monotonicity properties of the Franz--Parisi (FP) potential \cite{franz1995recipes,franz1997phase}, while the mathematically rigorous literature characterizes hardness via the limitations of restricted algorithmic classes, most notably low-degree polynomial estimators \cite{hopkins2017efficient}. For many inference models, these two perspectives yield strikingly consistent predictions, giving rise to a long-standing open problem of establishing a precise mathematical relationship between them. In this work, we show that for estimation problems the power of low-degree polynomials is equivalent to the monotonicity of the annealed FP potential for a broad family of Gaussian additive models (GAMs) with signal-to-noise ratio $λ$. In particular, subject to a low-degree conjecture for GAMs, our results imply that the polynomial-time limits of these models are directly implied by the monotonicity of the annealed FP potential, in conceptual agreement with predictions from the physics literature dating back to the 1990s.

</details>

### [9] [Electrically switchable ferron upconversion in a van der Waals ferroelectric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19394)
*Sujan Subedi,Wuzhang Fang,Fan Fei,Zixin Zhai,Jack P. Rollins,Carter Fox,Alaina Drew,Bing Lv,Yuan Ping,Jun Xiao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究报道了在范德华铁电体NbOI₂中实现了电可调控的非线性铁子（ferron）上转换，通过太赫兹激发3.1 THz铁子驱动相干上转换至7.0 THz光学声子，并利用电场切换实现对铁子动力学和上转换过程的非易失性控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性声子学（nonlinear phononics）为调控晶格激发提供了强大的超快途径，但非谐声子相互作用的动态控制仍然受限，因为这些相互作用通常由平衡晶格固定且缺乏外部可调性。铁电体中的铁子（ferrons）结合了固有的声子非线性和铁电序参数的直接电控制，可能为克服这一限制提供有前景的平台。

Method: 研究采用二维太赫兹光谱（two-dimensional THz spectroscopy）直接解析非对角耦合特征并建立非线性上转换路径，结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和分析建模识别微观起源为立方非谐晶格耦合（cubic anharmonic lattice coupling）。通过原位电场切换（in situ electric-field switching）实现对铁子动力学和上转换过程的非易失性控制。

Result: 实验显示共振太赫兹激发3.1 THz铁子驱动相干上转换至7.0 THz光学声子。跨越矫顽场（coercive fields）的相位反转和迟滞行为表明，铁子介导的非线性声子相互作用强烈依赖于底层铁电序参数。电场切换实现了对铁子动力学和相关上转换过程的非易失性控制。

Conclusion: 该研究将铁子上转换确立为铁电体中非线性声子学的新普适机制，并建立了一个电可编程的相干晶格控制平台，为铁子信息处理（ferronic information processing）和量子声子转导（quantum phononic transduction）开辟了道路。

Abstract: Nonlinear phononics provides a powerful ultrafast route to control lattice excitations, enabling access to hidden quantum orders, phononic computing, and quantum transduction. However, dynamic control of anharmonic phonon interactions remains limited, as these interactions are typically fixed by the equilibrium crystal lattice and lack external tunability. Emergent ferrons in ferroelectrics, which are collective oscillations of the spontaneous electric polarization, may offer a promising platform to overcome this limitation by combining intrinsic phononic nonlinearity with direct electrical control of the ferroelectric order parameter. Here we report electrically controllable nonlinear ferron upconversion in the van der Waals ferroelectric NbOI2. We show that resonant THz excitation of a 3.1 THz ferron drives coherent upconversion to a 7.0 THz optical phonon. Using two-dimensional THz spectroscopy, we directly resolve off-diagonal coupling features and establish the nonlinear upconversion pathway. Supported by first-principles calculations and analytical modeling, we identify the microscopic origin as a cubic anharmonic lattice coupling. Importantly, in situ electric-field switching enables nonvolatile control of both the ferron dynamics and the associated upconversion process. The phase reversal and hysteretic behavior across the coercive fields establish that the ferron-mediated nonlinear phononic interaction is strongly dependent on the underlying ferroelectric order parameter. These results introduce ferron upconversion as a new and universal regime of nonlinear phononics in ferroelectrics and establish an electrically programmable platform for coherent lattice control, paving the way for ferronic information processing and quantum phononic transduction.

</details>


### [10] [Tailoring Emergent Magnetic Moment in La$_{0.7}$Sr$_{0.3}$MnO$_3$-Bi$_2$Te$_3$ Heterostructures via Interfacial Reconstructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19433)
*Damian Brzozowskim,Yu Liu,Øyvind Finnseth,Egil Y. Tokle,Andrew J. Caruana,Christy J. Kinane,Alexander J. Grutter,Dennis G. Meier,Ingrid Hallsteinsen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究报道了在(111)取向La₀.₇Sr₀.₃MnO₃ (LSMO)与(00l)取向Bi₂Te₃ (BT)异质结构中，通过界面重构控制涌现磁行为的现象。界面重构稳定了与底层铁磁LSMO层耦合的次级磁有序相，导致室温下出现非传统的自交叉磁滞回线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索磁性氧化物-拓扑绝缘体异质结构中界面工程对涌现磁耦合和磁态的控制能力。通过调控界面重构，旨在理解并操纵这些异质结构中出现的非传统磁行为。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）制备两种不同界面结构的异质结构（直接沉积BT与引入碲种子层）；2）使用极化中子反射测量（Polarized Neutron Reflectometry）建模分析界面重构区域；3）采用元素特异性X射线吸收光谱（element-specific X-ray absorption spectroscopy）分析锰物种的化学重构。

Result: 研究结果显示：1）直接沉积BT时形成中间界面层，稳定了与底层铁磁LSMO耦合的次级磁有序相；2）异质结构在室温下表现出非传统的自交叉磁滞回线，具有低外加场下净磁化反转特征；3）引入碲种子层产生更尖锐的LSMO-BT界面，同时保留异常磁滞行为并增强饱和磁化强度；4）元素特异性X射线吸收光谱表明涌现磁相源于锰物种的化学重构。

Conclusion: 结论表明，磁性氧化物-拓扑绝缘体异质结构中的界面工程为控制涌现磁耦合和涌现磁态提供了有效途径。界面重构能够稳定次级磁有序相，导致非传统磁行为，这为设计新型磁电子器件奠定了基础。

Abstract: We report emergent magnetic behavior in heterostructures composed of (111)-oriented La$_{0.7}$Sr$_{0.3}$MnO$_3$ (LSMO) and (00$l$)-oriented Bi$_2$Te$_3$ (BT), controlled by interfacial reconstructions. When BT is deposited directly onto LSMO, an intermediate interfacial layer forms between the two materials. Polarized Neutron Reflectometry modeling reveals that this reconstructed region stabilizes a secondary magnetically ordered phase that is coupled to the underlying ferromagnetic LSMO layer. As a consequence, the heterostructures exhibit unconventional self-crossing magnetic hysteresis loops at room temperature, characterized by a reversal of the net magnetization at low applied fields. In contrast, the introduction of a tellurium seed layer results in a sharper LSMO-BT interface, while preserving the anomalous hysteresis behavior and enhancing the saturation magnetization. Element-specific X-ray absorption spectroscopy suggests that the emergent magnetic phase originates from the chemical reconstruction of manganese species. These results demonstrate that interface engineering in magnetic oxide-topological insulator heterostructures provides a pathway to control emergent magnetic coupling and emergent magnetic states in oxide-topological insulator heterostructures.

### [11] [Auxetic Response in Two-Dimensional MXenes with Atomically Defined Perforations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19436)
*Hossein Darban*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过大规模反应分子动力学模拟，揭示了穿孔单层钛基MXene超材料具有可调谐的负泊松比（negative Poisson's ratio）特性，其力学行为可通过穿孔几何结构和表面终止基团进行调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米制造技术的进步使得二维材料能够通过引入工程化孔隙和穿孔进行原子尺度操控，但穿孔二维材料的拉胀力学行为（auxetic mechanical behavior）尚未得到充分关注。本研究旨在探索穿孔单层MXene超材料的力学响应特性。

Method: 采用大规模反应分子动力学模拟（reactive molecular dynamics simulations），并通过实验测量和第一性原理计算进行验证。系统研究了包含矩形穿孔（具有直韧带和正弦曲线韧带）的MXene超材料结构，在不同几何参数和温度条件下进行单轴拉伸和压缩测试，从变形起始到断裂全过程。

Result: MXene超材料表现出可调谐的负泊松比（negative Poisson's ratio），可通过穿孔几何结构和表面终止基团进行控制。原子应力分析揭示了连接点处的交替面内剪切应力诱导韧带发生旋转变形，这种旋转连接机制（rotating-junction mechanism）与原子级薄材料的低弯曲刚度引起的面外偏转相耦合，产生复杂的三维变形。

Conclusion: 穿孔几何结构主导拉胀趋势的定性特征，而本征材料性质决定定量响应。MXene被认为是设计可调谐二维力学超材料的多功能候选材料，研究为几何结构、弯曲刚度和拉胀变形机制之间的相互作用提供了原子尺度见解。

Abstract: Recent advances in nanoscale fabrication enable atomic-scale manipulation of two-dimensional (2D) materials by introducing engineered pores and perforations. This provides new opportunities to tailor functional properties of 2D materials for applications such as selective ion transport, desalination membranes, and molecular filtration. Despite this progress, the auxetic mechanical behavior of perforated 2D materials has received little attention. In this work, large-scale reactive molecular dynamics (MD) simulations, validated against experimental measurements and first-principles calculations, are employed to investigate the mechanical response of perforated monolayer titanium-based MXene metamaterials. Architectures containing rectangular perforations with straight ligaments and sinusoidally curved ligaments are systematically examined under uniaxial tension and compression over a range of geometric parameters and temperatures, from the onset of deformation to fracture. The results demonstrate that MXene metamaterials exhibit a tunable negative Poisson's ratio (NPR), which can be controlled through the perforation geometry and surface termination. Atomistic stress analysis reveals alternating in-plane shear stresses at the junctions that induce rotational deformation of the ligaments. This rotating-junction mechanism is coupled with out-of-plane deflections arising from the low bending rigidity of atomically thin materials, producing complex three-dimensional deformations. Comparison with graphene metamaterials indicates that the perforation geometry governs qualitative auxetic trends, whereas intrinsic material properties determine quantitative responses. These findings identify MXenes as a versatile candidate for the design of tunable 2D mechanical metamaterials and provide atomistic insight into the interplay between geometry, bending rigidity, and auxetic deformation mechanisms.

### [12] [Theoretical investigation of the photovoltaic properties of MgSnN$_{2}$ for multi-junction solar cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19508)
*Issam Mahraj,Mossab Oublal,Andrzej Ptok*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有Pna2₁对称性的正交晶系MgSnN₂化合物，通过DFT和SLME计算发现其作为低成本、无毒光伏材料的潜力。带隙为2.45 eV，2 μm薄膜效率可达13.17%，串联结构可提升至22.42%，阳离子无序可进一步降低带隙。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究正交晶系（orthorhombic）MgSnN₂化合物作为低成本、无毒光伏（photovoltaic, PV）材料的应用潜力，探索其在太阳能电池领域的可行性。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）和光谱限制最大效率（spectroscopic limited maximum efficiency, SLME）计算方法，使用mBJ半局域交换泛函（semilocal exchange functional）分析电子和光学性质。

Result: MgSnN₂带隙为2.45 eV，2 μm薄膜在室温下效率可达13.17%。多结器件（multi-junction device）模拟显示串联配置（tandem configuration）将效率从12.80%（单结）提升至22.42%，阳离子无序（cation disorder）可进一步降低带隙。

Conclusion: MgSnN₂是具有潜力的低成本无毒光伏材料，通过薄膜优化、多结器件设计和阳离子无序调控可显著提升其光伏性能，适合太阳能电池应用。

Abstract: The orthorhombic crystal structure of the MgSnN$_2$ compound with Pna2$_1$ symmetry has been investigated as a low-cost, non-toxic material for photovoltaic (PV) applications using density functional theory (DFT) and spectroscopic limited maximum efficiency (SLME) calculations. A detailed analysis of the electronic and optical properties was performed using the mBJ semilocal exchange functional. The bandgap of MgSnN$_2$ is found to be 2.45 eV. SLME photovoltaic analysis suggests that a thin film of MgSnN$_2$ with a thickness of 2 $μ$m can reach an efficiency of 13.17% at room temperature. This efficiency was further improved through the simulation of a multi-junction device, where the tandem configuration increased the efficiency from 12.80% (single-junction) to 22.42%. Furthermore, introducing cation disorder can further reduce the bandgap, enhancing its suitability for solar cell applications.

### [13] [First principles characterization of spinterfaces between magnetic Cobaltocene molecule and 2D magnets (CrI$_3$, Fe$_3$GeTe$_2$)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19511)
*Nikola Machacova,Biplab Sanyal*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过第一性原理计算分析了钴茂（cobaltocene）单分子磁体与二维磁性材料（CrI₃和Fe₃GeTe₂）界面的磁电性质，发现界面稳定且存在强方向各向异性的磁交换作用，钴茂/CrI₃界面在费米能级呈现100%自旋极化，具有自旋输运应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索单分子磁体钴茂与二维磁性材料（半导体CrI₃和金属Fe₃GeTe₂）形成的自旋极化界面的性质，以理解界面磁交换机制并评估其在自旋电子学（spintronics）应用中的潜力。

Method: 采用基于第一性原理密度泛函理论（first-principles density functional theory）的计算方法，通过吸附能评估界面稳定性，并利用总能量差法和Liechtenstein-Katsnelson-Antropov-Gubanov（LKAG）形式在最大局域化Wannier函数（maximally localized Wannier functions, MLWFs）基础上获取磁交换相互作用参数。

Result: 计算显示异质界面稳定且存在界面电子态杂化（hybridization）；磁交换作用呈现强方向各向异性（directional anisotropy），与轨道杂化性质一致；分子吸附可增强层内交换相互作用，部分参数相比独立情况增加达3倍；钴茂/CrI₃界面在费米能级（Fermi level）呈现100%自旋极化（spin polarization）。

Conclusion: 钴茂与二维磁性材料界面表现出稳定的磁电耦合和强各向异性交换作用，特别是钴茂/CrI₃界面的完全自旋极化为自旋输运（spin-transport）应用提供了有前景的平台。

Abstract: In this paper, we examine the properties of spin-polarized interfaces consisting of single-molecule magnet bis(cyclopentadienyl)cobalt(II) (cobaltocene) and two-dimensional magnetic materials, semiconducting CrI$_3$ and metallic Fe$_3$GeTe$_2$, using first-principles density functional theory based calculations. Our calculated adsorption energies indicate the stability of these hetero-interfaces with the observation of hybridization of electronic states across the interface. Magnetic exchange interaction parameters have been obtained from both total energy differences and the Liechtenstein-Katsnelson-Antropov-Gubanov (LKAG) formalism in the basis of maximally localized Wannier functions (MLWFs). Analysis of these parameters shows a strong directional anisotropy in the magnetic substrate-molecule interaction in agreement with the nature of orbital hybridization. Additionally, possible exchange mechanisms are proposed based on orbital-resolved exchange and hopping parameters. We also show that the molecular adsorption may enhance the intralayer exchange interactions, with some exchange parameters reaching up to a 3-fold increase in magnitude compared to the freestanding case. Finally, we observe a 100 % spin polarization at the Fermi level in the cobaltocene/CrI$_3$ interface, which makes it particularly promising for spin-transport applications.

### [14] [Realizing giant valley polarization effect based on monolayer altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19619)
*Weifeng Xie,Libo Wang,Xiong Xu,Yunliang Yue,Huayan Xia,Longhui He,Hui Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过第一性原理计算和对称性分析，揭示了单层V2Se2O交变磁体（altermagnet）中谷极化效应与磁性原子间净磁矩的关联，提出了两种实现巨大谷极化效应的策略：通过Cr替代构建亚铁磁单层VCrSe2O，以及构建V2Se2O/α-SnO范德华异质结。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稳定且显著的谷极化效应是利用谷自由度（valley degree of freedom）构建谷电子学（valleytronic）器件的关键。本研究旨在探索在单层交变磁体（altermagnet）中实现巨大谷极化效应的有效策略。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和对称性分析（symmetry analysis）方法。研究基于单层V2Se2O交变磁体，通过两种策略调控谷极化：1）用Cr原子替代一个V原子构建亚铁磁单层VCrSe2O；2）构建V2Se2O与α-SnO单层组成的范德华异质结（van der Waals heterostructure）。

Result: 研究发现谷极化效应与磁性原子间的净磁矩（net magnetic moment）相关。在VCrSe2O中，沿a轴或b轴施加单轴应变（uniaxial strain）可显著增强谷极化值，且谷极化与磁性原子间净磁矩呈近线性关系。在异质结中，压缩层间距可增加V原子间净磁矩，将谷极化值提升至近400 meV。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了单层交变磁体中谷极化与磁性原子间净磁矩的关联性。提出的两种策略——构建亚铁磁单层和交变磁体基异质结——为实现巨大谷极化效应提供了理论指导，推动了亚铁磁单层和交变磁体基异质结在谷电子学中的潜在应用。

Abstract: Stable and remarkable valley polarization effect is the key to utilizing valley degree of freedom in valleytronic devices. According to first-principles calculations and symmetry analysis, we reveal that valley polarization effect in monolayer V2Se2O altermagnet is correlated with the net magnetic moment between magnetic V atoms under uniaxial strain, thereby proposing two strategies for achieving giant valley polarization effect. Firstly, substituting one V atom in V2Se2O with Cr to construct a ferrimagnetic monolayer VCrSe2O enhances the net magnetic moment between magnetic atoms, thereby realizing a giant valley polarization effect. Applying uniaxial strain along either the a-axis or b-axis significantly increases the value of valley polarization, which exhibits a nearly linear relationship with the net magnetic moments between the magnetic atoms. Secondly, constructing a van der Waals heterostructure composed of V2Se2O and α-SnO monolayers breaks mirror symmetry, thereby inducing a net magnetic moment, which in turn causes a remarkable valley polarization effect. Compressing the interlayer distance of the heterostructure can increase the net magnetic moment between V atoms, then enhancing the value of valley polarization to nearly 400 meV. This work reveals that valley polarization in monolayer altermagnet is correlated with the net magnetic moment between magnetic atoms. Finally, we propose two strategies to achieve giant valley polarization based on monolayer altermagnets, providing theoretical guidance for the potential applications of ferrimagnetic monolayers and altermagnet-based heterostructures in valleytronics.

</details>


### [15] [Influence of oxygen ion implantation on magnetic microstructure in Pt/Co/Pt multilayers with perpendicular magnetic anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19674)
*Anmol Sharma,Mukul Gupta,Prasanta Karmakar,V. Raghavendra Reddy,Vivek K. Malik,Andrei Gloskovskii,Ranjeet Kumar Brajpuriya,Ajay Gupta,Vishakha Kaushik,Sachin Pathak*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过氧离子注入调控钴/铂多层膜界面，显著提升磁畴壁运动速度，为自旋电子器件性能优化提供新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氧与钴及钴基合金的相互作用对自旋电子学至关重要，因其能增强轨道各向异性和界面Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI），这些特性在磁隧道结（MTJs）数据存储和磁畴壁（DW）运动等应用中具有关键作用。研究旨在理解氧与铁磁（FM）/重金属（HM）界面之间的复杂关系。

Method: 采用特定结构的Pt/Co 1.2/Pt（nm）多层膜，对钴层进行受控氧离子注入。通过面内磁滞回线测量验证各向异性变化，并在低磁场条件下分析Co/Pt多层膜的磁畴壁动力学，重点关注磁畴壁速度、粗糙度振幅和粗糙度指数等关键参数。

Result: 高注入剂量下垂直各向异性消失。氧离子注入后，磁畴壁速度从5 um/s提升至300 um/s，增幅超过50倍。这种改善的根本原因是注入引起的结构和磁性变化，成功降低了阻碍磁畴壁运动的能量势垒。

Conclusion: 研究表明氧离子注入可用于精确调控铁磁界面，有望提升下一代自旋电子器件的功能性，为界面工程提供有效手段。

Abstract: The interaction of oxygen with cobalt and cobalt-based alloys has been a very important topic in the field of spintronics as it leads to enhanced orbital anisotropy and interfacial Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction (DMI), which are crucial in the context of applications such as magnetic tunnel junctions (MTJs) based data storage and domain wall (DW) motion. To understand the complex and interesting relationship between oxygen and ferromagnetic (FM)/heavy metal (HM) interfaces, we studied controlled oxygen ion implantation in a cobalt layer located in a Pt/Co 1.2 /Pt (nm) multilayer with a specific structure. At high implantation fluence, the perpendicular anisotropy was lost, as verified by in-plane hysteresis measurements. Under low magnetic field conditions, the DW dynamics of Co/Pt multilayers were analyzed, highlighting key parameters such as DW velocity, roughness amplitude, and roughness exponent. After O+-ion implantation, the DW velocity increased by more than 50 times, rising from 5 um/s to 300 um/s compared with the as-deposited multilayer. The fundamental cause of this improvement is the structural and magnetic changes brought by the implantation, which successfully lower the energy barriers preventing DW movements. The results show how oxygen implantation can be used to precisely tailor the ferromagnetic interfaces, leading to promised improvements in the functionality of next-generation spintronic devices.

</details>


### [16] [First-principle study of the influence of hydroxyapatite on magnesium surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19823)
*Anthony Veit Berg,Ablai Forster,Tim Hansson,Alexandra J. Jernstedt,Emmy Salminen,Elsebeth Schröder*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 采用密度泛函理论研究羟基磷灰石（HA）在镁（Mg）表面的吸附行为，探究HA涂层和合金化对镁基可降解植入体表面的影响。研究发现钙（Ca）和锌（Zn）掺杂通常能改善HA吸附，但掺杂位置与HA相对构型会影响效果，其中Ca掺杂时原子可能迁移至HA层。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在理解羟基磷灰石（HA）涂层和合金化对镁基可降解植入体（Mg-based biodegradable implants）表面的影响机制。通过理论计算探究HA在纯镁及掺杂镁表面的吸附行为，为优化植入体表面性能提供理论基础。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算羟基磷灰石单层在纯Mg(0001)表面以及稀疏掺杂钙（Ca）或锌（Zn）的Mg(0001)表面的吸附。研究内容包括吸附能（adsorption energies）、结构变化以及电子密度变化分析。

Result: 除少数相对位置外，Zn和Ca掺杂均能改善HA在镁表面的吸附。所有吸附构型均导致表面和HA层发生形变。特别地，在特定吸附构型中，Ca掺杂原子会从镁表面迁移至HA层，同时在镁表面顶层留下空位。电子密度变化图显示，Ca掺杂时电子在掺杂原子及邻近镁原子周围聚集，而Zn掺杂的电子聚集效应较弱。

Conclusion: 掺杂元素的选择以及HA与掺杂位置的相对构型共同影响HA与镁表面的相互作用，进而调控吸附能、原子结构和电子结构。该研究为通过表面工程优化镁基植入体的生物相容性和降解性能提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Hydroxyapatite (HA) on a magnesium (Mg) surface is studied using density functional theory, to help understand the effect of HA coating and alloying in the surfaces of Mg-based biodegradable implants. We determine the adsorption energies and structural changes of a single layer of HA on pure Mg(0001) and on sparsely calcium (Ca) or zinc (Zn) doped Mg(0001) and find that both Zn and Ca doping improves the adsorption, except in a few positions of HA relative to the dopant position. All adsorption configurations, whether with pure or doped Mg surfaces, show deformation of the surface and HA layer. For Ca doping, we found that for a certain adsorption configuration, the dopant Ca atom moves out of the Mg surface and into the HA layer, leaving behind a Mg vacancy in the top layer of the Mg surface. Plots of electron density changes show that electrons accumulate around the Ca dopant and the neighboring Mg atoms, while in Zn doping this is less pronounced. Overall, our results demonstrate that the dopant choice and relative position of HA influence the interaction between HA and Mg-surfaces, and affect both adsorption energies and atomic and electronic structures.

### [17] [DSC curve fingerprints directly encode mechanical properties of aluminum alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19905)
*Lukas Pichlmann,Samuel Studer,Aurel R. Arnoldt,Paul Oberhauser,Johannes A. Österreicher*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究证明差示扫描量热法（DSC）曲线可作为直接预测铝合金力学性能的指纹特征，通过机器学习模型实现了对屈服强度、抗拉强度和均匀伸长率的准确预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 差示扫描量热法（Differential Scanning Calorimetry, DSC）是研究铝合金析出和相变的标准工具，但其与力学性能的关系迄今主要停留在间接层面。本研究旨在探索DSC曲线本身能否作为直接编码力学性能的指纹特征。

Method: 研究选取四种代表性6xxx系列铝合金（Al-Mg-Si），施加不同自然和人工时效处理，随后进行DSC热流测量和拉伸测试。利用热分析图训练机器学习模型，通过五折分组交叉验证预测力学性能，并采用留一合金法评估模型泛化能力。

Result: 最佳模型（Lasso）在预测屈服强度、抗拉强度和均匀伸长率时分别获得0.93、0.86和0.87的R²值，平均绝对误差分别为14.3 MPa、11.1 MPa和1.5%。特征重要性分析显示230-270°C区域（与主要硬化相β''析出相关）对预测精度贡献最大。

Conclusion: 研究确立了DSC作为一种诊断工具，可作为力学性能评估的快速替代方法，实现加速合金筛选、工艺优化以及热分析在数据驱动制造中的集成应用。

Abstract: Differential scanning calorimetry (DSC) is a standard tool for studying precipitation and phase transformations in aluminum alloys, yet its relation to mechanical performance has so far remained mostly indirect. Here, we demonstrate that DSC curves themselves act as fingerprints that directly encode mechanical properties. Four representative 6xxx series alloys (Al-Mg-Si) were subjected to different natural and artificial aging regimens, followed by DSC heat-flow measurements and tensile testing. Machine learning models trained on the thermograms predicted yield strength, ultimate tensile strength, and uniform elongation in five-fold grouped cross-validation, with the best model (Lasso) achieving R^2 values of 0.93, 0.86, and 0.87 and mean absolute errors of 14.3 MPa, 11.1 MPa, and 1.5 percent, respectively. Leave-one-alloy-out evaluation with sparse calibration using anchor samples further demonstrated generalization across alloy chemistries. While direct prediction on unseen alloy data degraded performance substantially, inclusion of as few as one to two anchor conditions from the target alloy recovered predictive accuracy, approaching that of the standard cross-validation. Feature importance analysis revealed that the 230 to 270 C region, associated with precipitation of the primary hardening phase beta'', contributed most strongly to predictive accuracy, providing direct mechanistic validation of the model. These findings establish DSC as a diagnostic tool that can serve as a rapid proxy for mechanical property evaluation, enabling accelerated alloy screening, process optimization, and integration of thermal analysis into data-driven manufacturing.

</details>


### [18] [Physics-aware neural networks enable robust and full atomic structure determination via low-dose atomic electron tomography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19942)
*Yao Zhang,Lanyi Cao,Zhen Sun,Jihan Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种物理感知的两阶段神经网络（PANN），用于在低剂量条件下实现准确的原子电子断层扫描（AET），通过结合物理约束显著提升了原子坐标精度和元素分类性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原子电子断层扫描（AET）在低剂量条件下面临信噪比降低的问题，需要在精度、鲁棒性和通量之间进行权衡，这限制了AET的广泛应用。研究旨在开发一种方法来解决低剂量成像下的准确AET重建挑战。

Method: 提出物理感知的两阶段神经网络（PANN）：第一阶段使用全局-局部3D ResUNet优化初始重建并校正体积中的几何畸变；第二阶段通过3D Zernike矩编码每个已识别原子周围的局部密度，结合原子坐标使用图注意力Transformer进行元素分类。

Result: 在包含42,588个重建体积的数据集上进行基准测试，涵盖多种噪声模型、材料形态和剂量设置。低剂量条件下，PANN显著提升了性能，降低了原子坐标误差并提高了原子恢复率。在不同形态和组成的纳米颗粒实验数据上表现出稳健的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 该方法有望扩展AET的适用性，特别是在研究对电子剂量或化学状态敏感的材料方面，包括卤化物钙钛矿、沸石和量子点等材料体系。

Abstract: Atomic electron tomography (AET) determines the three-dimensional (3D) coordinates and chemical identities of individual atoms from a series of scanning transmission electron microscopy images taken at different tilt angles. However, under the low dose conditions required to mitigate beam damage, the reduced signal-to-noise ratio forces a trade off among accuracy, robustness, and throughput, which ultimately limits the broader application of AET. Here, we introduce a physics aware, two stage neural networks (PANN) that incorporates physical constraints throughout its workflow to achieve accurate AET under low-dose imaging. First, a global local 3D ResUNet refines the initial reconstruction and corrects geometric distortions in the volume. Second, the local density around each identified atom is encoded using 3D Zernike moments. These feature descriptors, along with the atomic coordinates are then processed by a graph attention Transformer to classify the elemental species. We benchmark the PANN workflow using a dataset of 42,588 reconstructed volumes, covering diverse noise models, materials morphologies, and dose settings. Under low dose conditions, PANN significantly improves performance, reducing the atomic coordinates error and leading to an increase in the atomic recovery rate. The framework's performance on experimental lose dose AET data across nanoparticles of varying morphology and composition demonstrate robust generalization. We anticipate this approach will extend the applicability of AET, particularly in investigating materials sensitive to electron dose or chemical state, including halide perovskites, zeolite, and quantum dot.

### [19] [The interplay between thermomigration and stress-driven hydrogen transport in metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20049)
*Daniel J. Long,Edmund Tarleton,Alan C. F. Cocks,Felix Hofmann*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个热力学一致框架，用于分析热迁移（thermomigration）和应力驱动氢传输的竞争与协同效应，通过铁/镍热交换器和锆合金核燃料包壳案例研究，量化了不同机制的主导作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热迁移作为由温度梯度驱动的氢传输机制，可与应力梯度驱动的氢传输竞争。然而，由于对热迁移的机理理解有限且实验数据稀缺，该领域相对研究不足，需要建立更完善的框架来分析这两种传输机制的相互作用。

Method: 开发了一个热力学一致的氢传输框架，包含热迁移的机理模型。该框架通过有效化学势（effective chemical potential）在有限元（finite element）框架中实现，并应用于铁和镍热交换器以及锆合金核燃料包壳的案例研究。

Result: 研究表明，在传热部件中，即使存在显著的热失配应力（thermal incompatibility stresses），热迁移通常主导氢的再分布。然而，在尖锐应力集中器附近，应力驱动传输变得决定性。研究还引入了一种图形方法，可在无需完全耦合模拟的情况下快速识别主导传输机制。

Conclusion: 该研究为评估传热结构部件中的氢再分布和氢脆（hydrogen embrittlement）风险提供了实用指导，强调了热迁移在传热部件中的主导作用，同时识别了应力驱动传输在特定区域的重要性。

Abstract: Thermomigration is the driving force for hydrogen transport due to a temperature gradient. It can compete with hydrogen transport induced by stress gradients. While stress-driven hydrogen migration is well established, thermomigration remains comparatively underexplored, largely due to limited mechanistic understanding and a scarcity of experimental data. In this work, we develop a thermodynamically consistent framework for hydrogen transport, incorporating a mechanistic model for thermomigration. This is implemented within a finite element framework using an effective chemical potential. Using case studies of iron and nickel heat exchangers and zirconium alloy nuclear fuel cladding, we quantify the competing and synergistic effects of thermomigration and stress-driven transport. We show that thermomigration often dominates hydrogen redistribution in heat-carrying components, even in the presence of significant thermal incompatibility stresses. However, stress-driven transport is shown to become decisive near sharp stress concentrators. A graphical method is introduced to rapidly identify the dominant transport mechanism without requiring fully coupled simulations. The results provide practical guidance for assessing hydrogen redistribution and embrittlement risk in heat-carrying structural components.

### [20] [An Analytical Model of Alkali Metal Dendrite Growth in Ceramic Solid Electrolytes based on Griffith's Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20113)
*Ansgar Lowack*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 基于最小功耗原理，推导出固态电池中枝晶生长的临界电流密度与最长界面缺陷长度的3/2次方成正比，并预测其分布遵循威布尔分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究固态电池中陶瓷固态电解质在临界电流密度以上时被枝晶穿透的现象，旨在理解枝晶生长的物理机制并建立定量模型。

Method: 基于最小功耗原理（principle of minimal power dissipation），比较机械开裂能与电流绕行枝晶的焦耳热损耗，建立枝晶生长的能量平衡判据。

Result: 推导出临界电流密度J_crit与最长界面缺陷长度c_max的3/2次方成正比关系，并预测不同样品间J_crit的散射遵循威布尔分布（Weibull-distribution）。

Conclusion: 固态电池中枝晶生长的临界电流密度由界面缺陷的统计特性决定，其分布规律类似于陶瓷材料的拉伸强度分布，为固态电池的设计和可靠性评估提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In solid-state batteries, ceramic solid electrolytes are penetrated by dendrites when plating above a critical current density $J_\mathrm{crit}$. A dendrite will propagate by metal deposition at a pre-existing dendrite tip if the mechanical energy required to crack the ceramic open is less than the electrical energy (Joule heating) wasted by forcing the current to detour around the dendrite to the flat electrode surface. Based on this principle of minimal power dissipation, a dependence of $J_\mathrm{crit}\propto c_\mathrm{max}^{3/2}$ is derived. $c_\mathrm{max}$ is the length of the longest preexisting, sufficiently thin interfacial defect. Consequentially, scattering of $J_\mathrm{crit}$ between samples must follow a Weibull-distribution, similar to the tensile strength of ceramic components.

</details>


### [21] [Transformer-based prediction of two-dimensional material electronic properties under elastic strain engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20141)
*Haoran Ma,Yuchen Zheng,Leining Zhang,Xiaofei Chen,Dan Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 应变工程（strain engineering）是调控二维材料电子性质的有效途径，但使用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）探索多维应变空间时，由于法向和剪切应变分量之间的非线性耦合，计算成本过高。

Method: 引入基于Transformer的多目标代理模型框架，通过注意力权重分析（attention-weight analysis）保持模型的可解释性，实现DFT级别的带隙预测精度。

Result: 模型达到0.0103 eV的平均绝对误差，注意力图一致识别出剪切应变（shear strain）作为影响带隙和声子稳定性的相互作用中心，这一洞察是传统特征重要性指标难以捕捉的。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了基于注意力的架构作为多性质预测的物理可解释代理模型，为加速材料信息学中的深度弹性应变工程（deep elastic strain engineering）提供了通用策略。

Abstract: Strain engineering provides a powerful route for tuning the electronic properties of two-dimensional (2D) materials, but exploring the full multidimensional strain space with density functional theory (DFT) is computationally prohibitive due to the nonlinear coupling between normal and shear components. In this work, we introduce a Transformer-based, multi-target surrogate model framework that achieves DFT-level bandgap prediction accuracy, reaching a mean absolute error of 0.0103 eV while retaining full interpretability through attention-weight analysis. The learned self-attention map consistently identifies shear strain as the interaction center that influences both bandgap and phonon stability, an insight not readily captured by classical feature-importance metrics. This work establishes attention-based architectures as physically interpretable surrogate models for multi-property prediction, offering a generalizable strategy for accelerating deep elastic strain engineering in materials informatics.

### [22] [When Cubic Is Not Isotropic: Phonon-Exciton Decoupling in CuInSnS$_4$ Single Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20159)
*Lara Kim Linke,Yvonne Tomm,Xinyun Liu,Galina Gurieva,Daniel M. Tobbens,Pardis Adams,Michel Calame,Ryan W. Crisp,Jessica Boland,Sean Kavanagh,Susan Schorr,Mirjana Dimitrievska*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 立方结构CuInSnS₄单晶中的本征阳离子无序导致局部对称性破缺，显著影响激子性质但保持声子对称性平均化，揭示了声子-激子解耦现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原子尺度无序可在平均结构为立方的晶体中产生隐藏的光学各向异性。研究旨在探索CuInSnS₄单晶中由本征In/Sn阳离子无序引起的局部对称性破缺环境如何以不同方式影响振动和激子性质。

Method: 结合偏振和温度依赖的拉曼光谱（polarization- and temperature-dependent Raman spectroscopy）、红外近场显微镜（infrared near-field microscopy）、稳态和时间分辨光致发光（steady-state and time-resolved photoluminescence）以及第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）。

Result: 声子在纳米尺度上保持对称性平均化和局部均匀性，而光致发光显示低能带尾发射具有明显的偏振各向异性，遵循明确的角对称性。这表明激子态对局部对称性破缺具有强烈敏感性。

Conclusion: 本征无序可在保持振动相干性和介电均匀性的同时局域化激子，揭示了声子-激子解耦现象。这为偏振敏感光源、各向异性光电探测器和基于激子的光学功能器件开辟了新机遇，即使在名义上的立方多元半导体中也是如此。

Abstract: Atomic-scale disorder can create hidden optical anisotropy even in crystals that are structurally cubic on average. Here, we show that CuInSnS$_4$ single crystals host locally symmetry-broken environments arising from intrinsic In/Sn cation disorder, which affect vibrational and excitonic properties in markedly different ways. Combining polarization- and temperature-dependent Raman spectroscopy, infrared near-field microscopy, steady-state and time-resolved photoluminescence, and first-principles calculations, we find that phonons remain largely symmetry-averaged and locally homogeneous on the nanoscale. In contrast, photoluminescence reveals a lower-energy band-tail emission with pronounced polarization anisotropy following a well-defined angular symmetry, highlighting the strong sensitivity of excitonic states to local symmetry breaking. This phonon-exciton decoupling reveals that intrinsic disorder can localize excitons while preserving vibrational coherence and dielectric homogeneity, thereby opening new opportunities for polarization-sensitive light sources, anisotropic photodetectors, and exciton-based optical functionalities even in nominally cubic multinary semiconductors.

### [23] [Symmetry-protected Interface Modes Bifurcated from Double Dirac Cones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19442)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用离散版本的层势框架（discrete version of the layer-potential framework）进行严格数学证明，该方法为分析界面模式提供了理论基础。

Result: 严格证明了界面模式的存在性，确定了界面模式的确切数量，并证明了这些模式在保持反射对称性（reflection symmetry）的扰动下受到对称性保护（symmetry-protected）。

Abstract: We rigorously prove the existence of interface modes in a sharp interface model, which bifurcate from the double Dirac cone as a consequence of the band inversion induced by super-symmetry breaking. The exact number of interface modes are determined. The proof is based on a discrete version of the layer-potential framework. Moreover, we prove that such interface modes are symmetry-protected against perturbations that respect the reflection symmetry.

### [24] [Disordered Ground States of Ergodic Quantum Spin Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19475)
*Eric B. Roon,Jeffrey H. Schenker*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文填补了无序量子自旋系统（disordered quantum spin systems）研究的空白，证明了在满足统计平移不变性的随机局域相互作用下，系统在热力学极限下总是存在具有相同对称性的无序基态（disordered ground states）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献中关于满足统计平移不变性的无序量子自旋系统存在研究空白。作者旨在填补这一空白，证明此类系统在热力学极限下总是存在具有相同对称性的无序基态。

Method: 使用无序版本的Lieb-Robinson界（disordered version of the Lieb-Robinson bounds），该界在温和条件下几乎必然成立。同时形式化了C*-代数（C*-algebra）上随机态的概念，并证明了向量测度文献中未记录的弱-*版本的Riesz-Markov-Kakutani定理。

Result: 证明了满足统计平移不变性的随机局域相互作用系统在热力学极限下总是存在具有相同对称性的无序基态。作为这一存在性的结果，证明了与体动力学相关的GNS哈密顿量（GNS Hamiltonian）的谱相对于无序是确定性的。

Conclusion: 该研究填补了无序量子自旋系统文献中的重要空白，建立了无序基态的存在性定理，并揭示了GNS哈密顿量谱的确定性特征，为无序量子系统的理论研究提供了新的数学工具和结果。

Abstract: In this letter, we fill a hole in the existing literature about disordered quantum spin systems generated by a random local interaction $\{\mathfrak{h}(Z)\}_{Z\Subset \mathbb{Z}^ν}$ satisfying a statistical version of translation invariance. We show such systems always have disordered ground states in the thermodynamic limit with the same symmetry. A key tool we use is a disordered version of the Lieb-Robinson bounds, which hold almost surely under mild conditions on $\mathfrak{h}$. Along the way, we formalize the notion of a random state on a $C^*$-algebra and prove a weak-$\ast$ version of the Riesz-Markov-Kakutani theorem, which seems not to have been recorded in the vector measures literature. As a consequence of the existence of the aforementioned disordered ground states, we show that the spectrum of the GNS Hamiltonain associated to the bulk dynamics is deterministic with respect to the disorder.

</details>


### [25] [Homotopy lattice gauge fields 1: The fields and their properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19525)
*Juan Orendain,Ivan Sanchez,José A. Zapata*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文引入同伦格点规范场（HLGFs），这是一种基于离散化底空间的规范场版本，通过高阶平行传输概念扩展了格点上沿路径的常规平行传输，使其包含高维路径信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是发展一种基于离散化底空间的规范场理论，通过引入高阶平行传输概念来丰富传统格点规范理论。这种框架旨在解决高维同伦中的局部到全局问题，并为量子场论提供更精细的场空间描述。

Method: 方法基于同伦格点规范场（homotopy lattice gauge fields, HLGFs）概念，采用高阶平行传输（higher parallel transport）来扩展传统格点规范理论。该框架应用了为解决高维同伦局部到全局问题而发展的非阿贝尔代数拓扑（nonabelian algebraic topology）框架。

Result: 结果表明，在二维或三维底空间上的同伦格点规范场能够确定底流形上的主丛（principal bundle）。该数据还为二维底空间上的拓扑荷（topological charge）提供了计算公式。框架为量子场论提供了场空间作为研究舞台，并展示了如何细化标准格点规范理论（standard lattice gauge theory）。

Conclusion: 同伦格点规范场框架成功地将高阶平行传输概念引入格点规范理论，为解决高维同伦问题提供了代数拓扑工具。该框架不仅能够确定主丛结构，还为拓扑荷计算提供了新方法，为量子场论研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We introduce homotopy lattice gauge fields (HLGFs), a version of gauge fields over a discretized base, based on a notion of higher parallel transport that enriches the usual parallel transport along paths on a lattice to also consider higher dimensional paths.
  Higher dimensional data keeps information about the parallel transport along homotopies of curves. With this data, a HLGF on a base space of dimension two or three determines a principal bundle over the base manifold. This data is also responsible for our formulas for the topological charge on two-dimensional bases.
  Our framework is an application of a nonabelian algebraic topology framework developed to solve the local to global problem in higher dimensional homotopy.
  No previous knowledge of higher category theory is assumed.
  The second part will be devoted to the space of fields as an arena for doing Quantum Field Theory, and to give the first examples of how our framework refines standard lattice gauge theory.

</details>

### [26] [Matrix Product States for Modulated Topological Phases: Crystalline Equivalence Principle and Lieb-Schultz-Mattis Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19381)
*Shang-Qiang Ning,Hiromi Ebisu,Ho Tat Lam*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文研究了受调制对称性（modulated symmetries）与空间对称性共同保护的一维拓扑相分类，建立了与内部对称性保护拓扑相的对应关系，并推导了相关的Lieb-Schultz-Mattis定理约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 调制对称性是在空间上非均匀作用的内部对称性，当与空间对称性结合时形成半直积群结构。研究这类对称性保护的拓扑相分类对于理解晶体对称性在拓扑物态中的作用具有重要意义。

Method: 使用矩阵乘积态（matrix product states）方法对一维空间中受调制对称性与空间对称性共同保护的拓扑相进行分类。通过Lyndon-Hochschild-Serre谱序列的矩阵乘积态推导，建立了调制对称性保护拓扑相与内部对称性保护拓扑相之间的显式对应关系。

Result: 研究发现调制对称性保护拓扑相由$H^{2}(G,U(1)_s)$分类，符合晶体等价原理（crystalline equivalence principle）。该分类证明了调制对称性的Lieb-Schultz-Mattis定理，禁止对称短程纠缠基态存在，并建立了SPT-LSM约束强制SPT基态具有非平凡纠缠。

Conclusion: 研究建立了调制对称性保护拓扑相的完整分类框架，验证了晶体等价原理在一维情况下的适用性。该分类方法可进一步应用于非可逆Kramers-Wannier反射对称性的LSM型约束分析，为理解空间对称性在拓扑物态中的作用提供了系统工具。

Abstract: Modulated symmetries are internal symmetries that act in a spatially non-uniform manner. Consequently, when a modulated symmetry $G_{\text{int}}$ is combined with a spatial symmetry $G_{\text{sp}}$, the total symmetry group takes the form of a semidirect product $G=G_{\text{int}}\rtimes G_{\text{sp}}$. Using matrix product states, we classify topological phases protected by modulated symmetries together with spatial symmetries in one spatial dimension. We show that these modulated symmetry-protected topological (SPT) phases are classified by $H^{2}(G,U(1)_s)$, in agreement with the crystalline equivalence principle, which states that SPT phases protected by symmetries involving spatial elements are in one-to-one correspondence with internal SPT phases protected by the same symmetries, viewed as acting internally. Furthermore, we provide a matrix product state derivation of the Lyndon-Hochschild-Serre spectral sequence for the corresponding internal SPT phases, which enables us to construct an explicit correspondence between modulated SPT phases and internal SPT phases. As applications of this classification, we prove a Lieb-Schultz-Mattis (LSM) theorem for modulated symmetries that forbids the existence of symmetric short-ranged entangled ground state, as well as an SPT-LSM constraint that enforces nontrivial entanglement in the SPT ground state. Finally, we use the classification to establish a similar LSM-type constraints for non-invertible Kramers-Wannier reflection symmetries.

</details>


### [27] [Non-collinear ferromagnetism in the Kondo lattice Ce$_5$CoGe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19592)
*Jinyu Wu,Jiawen Zhang,Toni Shiroka,Shams Sohel Islam,Mingyi Wang,Yongjun Zhang,Devashibhai T. Adroja,Yu Liu,Huiqiu Yuan,Michael Smidman*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: Ce$_5$CoGe$_2$在常压下呈现非共线铁磁结构，其四个不等价Ce位点具有不同磁矩，这种结构由交换相互作用、晶体电场、近藤效应和DM相互作用竞争驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究常压磁性态，为理解Ce$_5$CoGe$_2$在压力下磁序被抑制后出现超导性的机制提供基础。

Method: 采用磁化率、热容、粉末中子衍射和μ子自旋弛豫（μSR）测量，结合点电荷模型计算晶体电场（crystalline-electric field, CEF）基态。

Result: 中子衍射揭示非共线铁磁结构，四个不等价Ce位点磁矩不同；CEF计算支持位点间磁矩差异，并表明磁矩在不同方向有显著分量；Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya（DM）相互作用分析显示多数Ce-Ce键具有非零DM矢量。

Conclusion: 非共线铁磁性可能由位点间磁交换相互作用、CEF驱动的单离子各向异性、近藤效应（Kondo effect）和DM相互作用的竞争所驱动。

Abstract: The dense Kondo lattice Ce$_5$CoGe$_2$ exhibits superconductivity once the magnetic ordering is suppressed by pressure. Here the ambient pressure magnetic state is investigated via magnetization, heat capacity, powder neutron diffraction, and muon spin relaxation ($μ$SR) measurements. Neutron diffraction results reveal a noncollinear ferromagnetic structure, where the four inequivalent Ce sites exhibit different magnetic moments. Point-charge model calculations of the crystalline-electric field (CEF) ground states corroborate different moments between the sites, and suggest sizeable components of the moments along different directions, consistent with the non-collinear structure. Analysis of the Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya (DM) interaction for the bonds connecting Ce atoms demonstrates that most of these bonds exhibit a nonzero DM vector, suggesting that competition between intersite magnetic exchange interactions, CEF driven single-ion anisotropy, the Kondo effect and the DM interaction may drive the non-collinear ferromagnetism.

</details>


### [28] [Continuous crossover between high-pressure ice phases VII and X driven by monopole screening: a model study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19620)
*Sena Watanabe,Yukitoshi Motome,Haruki Watanabe*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过经典自旋模型和蒙特卡洛模拟，揭示了高压冰VII和冰X之间的转变是连续交叉而非热力学相变，而冰VIII的破坏则是一级相变，这源于氢键网络的拓扑脆弱性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质子无序的冰VII相与超高压非分子冰X相具有相同的宏观晶体对称性（空间群Pn3m），这引发了一个基本热力学问题：它们是具有奇异性的不同相，还是通过连续交叉绝热连接？

Method: 采用烧绿石晶格上的有效经典自旋-1 Blume-Capel模型，通过蒙特卡洛模拟研究高压冰VII、X以及VIII的有限温度相图。

Result: 模拟显示，冰VII和冰X对应态之间的转变缺乏热力学奇异性，表现为比热和磁化率中与S^z=0占据相关的非发散且不重合的峰，这归因于氢键网络的拓扑脆弱性。

Conclusion: 冰VII和冰X之间的连续交叉行为源于点状单极子激发的热增殖诱导的德拜-休克尔屏蔽，而质子有序的冰VIII相破坏涉及自发对称性破缺，保持一级相变特征。

Abstract: The proton-disordered molecular phase of water ice (ice-VII) and its ultrahigh-pressure non-molecular phase (ice-X) share identical macroscopic crystal symmetry (space group $Pn\bar{3}m$). This raises a fundamental thermodynamic question: are they distinct phases separated by a singularity, or are they adiabatically connected via a continuous crossover? To resolve this paradox, we investigate the finite-temperature phase diagram of high-pressure ices VII and X, as well as VIII, the proton-ordered phase that emerges at lower temperatures, using an effective classical spin-$1$ Blume-Capel model on the pyrochlore lattice. Through Monte Carlo simulations, we demonstrate that within this model, the transformation between the states corresponding to ice-VII and ice-X lacks a thermodynamic singularity, as characterized by non-divergent and non-coinciding peaks in the specific heat and susceptibility associated with the $S^z=0$ occupation. We attribute this continuous crossover behavior to the topological fragility of the hydrogen-bond network: the thermal proliferation of point-like monopole excitations (violations of the ice rules) induces Debye-Hückel screening of the emergent gauge field, destroying the topological Coulomb phase at any finite temperature. In contrast, the destruction of the proton-ordered ice-VIII phase involves spontaneous symmetry breaking and remains a first-order phase transition. Our findings provide a microscopic rationale that reconciles the macroscopic crystallographic symmetries of dense ice with its underlying topological properties.

</details>


### [29] [Magnetic anisotropy from interligand hopping in strongly correlated insulators: application to the magnon spectrum of CrI$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19630)
*Evgenii Barts,Paolo Barone,Maxim Mostovoy*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种计算多轨道莫特绝缘体中自旋轨道耦合诱导的各向异性交换相互作用的有效方法，并将其应用于单层CrI₃，揭示了长程跳跃产生的单离子各向异性对磁有序和磁子能带拓扑的稳定作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）在配体离子较强时，能够产生复杂的磁态如自旋液体、斯格明子晶体和拓扑磁子激发。研究旨在理解多轨道莫特绝缘体（multi-orbital Mott insulators）中由配体SOC介导的各向异性交换相互作用（anisotropic exchange interactions）及其对磁性的影响。

Method: 提出了一种计算任意自旋间距交换相互作用的有效方法。该方法考虑了配体上的SOC导致的伴随自旋翻转和配体空穴轨道态涨落的电子跳跃（electron hopping），以及配体间跳跃（hopping between ligands）介导的更远距离自旋相互作用。

Result: 将方法应用于单层CrI₃，获得了最近邻和次近邻Cr自旋间的各向异性相互作用，以及由长程跳跃（long-range hopping）诱导的单离子各向异性（single-ion anisotropy）。磁各向异性稳定了长程铁磁序，并在狄拉克点（Dirac points）处打开了磁子能隙（magnon gap），定义了非平凡的磁子能带拓扑（magnon band topology）。

Conclusion: 基于第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）的哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）参数，所得谱与实验观测到的体相CrI₃自旋波色散（spin-wave dispersion）吻合良好，但计算的狄拉克能隙远小于实验值，表明理论模型与实验观测间存在差异。

Abstract: Spin-orbit coupling (SOC) gives rise to complex magnetic states such as spin liquids, skyrmion crystals, and topological spin-wave excitations. We consider exchange interactions in multi-orbital Mott insulators where SOC is strong on ligand ions. SOC on the ligands enables electron hopping accompanied by spin flips and fluctuations in the orbital state of the ligand hole. These processes generate anisotropic exchange interactions and greatly increase the number of possible exchange paths. The number grows further with the inclusion of hopping between ligands, which mediates interactions between more distant spins. We propose an effective method to calculate exchange interactions at arbitrary separations between spins. Applying it to monolayer CrI$_3$, we obtain anisotropic interactions between nearest-neighbor and next-nearest-neighbor Cr spins, as well as single-ion anisotropy induced by long-range hopping. In this material, magnetic anisotropy stabilizes long-range ferromagnetic order and opens a magnon gap at the Dirac points, which defines a nontrivial magnon band topology. Using Hubbard model parameters from first-principles calculations, the resulting spectrum agrees well with the spin-wave dispersion observed experimentally in bulk CrI$_3$, except that the calculated Dirac gap is much smaller.

</details>


### [30] [Coherent canted ferrimagnetism and higher-order anisotropy in the nodal-line magnetic semiconductor Mn3Si2Te6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19673)
*Chang-woo Cho,Beomtak Kang,Ildo Choi,Jitae Gwak,Jisung Lee,Seung-Young Park,Seyoung Kwon,Sungkyun Park,Joonyoung Choi,Younjung Jo,Benjamin A. Piot,Jun Sung Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过热力学扭矩磁强计和电子自旋共振光谱，重构了Mn3Si2Te6中控制磁化旋转的磁各向异性能，揭示了其低温基态为相干倾斜亚铁磁体，并由高阶磁各向异性项稳定，为理解其巨大角磁阻现象提供了微观磁学基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Mn3Si2Te6作为范德华材料中的节线半导体，展现出巨大角磁阻现象，其电阻随磁场方向旋转发生数量级变化。然而，驱动自旋取向的微观磁势能机制仍不清楚，需要揭示磁各向异性如何控制磁化旋转，从而解释尖锐角输运特征的起源。

Method: 研究结合热力学扭矩磁强计（thermodynamic torque magnetometry）和电子自旋共振光谱（electron spin resonance spectroscopy）技术，重构了Mn3Si2Te6的磁各向异性能。通过分析竞争的二阶（K1）、四阶（K2）和六阶（K3）磁各向异性项，建立了磁场角度θ_H与磁化角度θ_M之间的非线性关系。

Result: 研究发现低温基态为相干倾斜亚铁磁体（coherent canted ferrimagnet），由竞争的二阶和四阶磁各向异性稳定。关键的六阶项提供了近平面刚度，维持了高场下的倾斜构型。利用获得的各向异性参数，研究重新参数化了巨大角磁阻（CAMR），将其表达为磁化角度θ_M的函数。

Conclusion: 该工作为Mn3Si2Te6中尖锐角输运特征的出现提供了具体的磁学基础，表明磁各向异性能的精确重构对于理解磁序与电子拓扑相互作用至关重要，特别是高阶各向异性项在维持倾斜磁结构和产生极端磁响应中的关键作用。

Abstract: The interplay between magnetic order and electronic topology in van der Waals materials enables extreme responses to external stimuli. The nodal-line semiconductor Mn3Si2Te6 exemplifies this, exhibiting colossal angular magnetoresistance (CAMR) where resistivity changes by orders of magnitude upon rotating the magnetic field. While this phenomenon implies a profound coupling between spin orientation and charge transport, the microscopic magnetic potentials driving spin orientations remain elusive. Here, we combine thermodynamic torque magnetometry and electron spin resonance spectroscopy to reconstruct the magnetic anisotropy energy that controls magnetization rotation in Mn3Si2Te6. We show that low-temperature ground state is a coherent canted ferrimagnet stabilized by competing second- (K1) and fourth-order (K2) magnetic anisotropy. Crucially, torque requires a substantial symmetry-allowed sixth-order term (K3), which provides near-plane stiffness and sustains canting at high fields. Using the resulting anisotropy parameters, we compute the non-linear relation between field angle θ_H and magnetization angle θ_M and reparameterize CAMR in terms of θ_M, providing a concrete magnetic basis for how sharp angular transport features can emerge near the in-plane configuration.

</details>


### [31] [Spin subdiffusion in perturbed infinite-U Hubbard chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19743)
*Jakub Rękas,Marcin Mierzejewski,Zala Lenarčič,Peter Prelovšek*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了$t$-模型（Hubbard模型在$U \to \infty$极限下的表示）中的自旋动力学，该模型在保持希尔伯特空间碎片化（Hilbert space fragmentation）的同时破坏可积性，展示了从弹道输运到反常扩散再到亚扩散（subdiffusion）的多种输运行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: $t$-模型作为强关联电子系统的基本模型之一，在一维链上具有可积性，其电荷动力学对应自由无自旋费米子。然而自旋序列被冻结，导致希尔伯特空间碎片化和非平凡的自旋动力学，这需要深入研究。

Method: 研究考虑了可积模型和受扰模型，其中扰动在保持碎片化的同时破坏可积性。通过分析这些模型，展示了不同类型的自旋动力学行为。

Result: 研究显示，在可积情况下自旋动力学呈现从弹道输运（ballistic transport）到反常扩散（anomalous diffusion）的行为；在受扰情况下则呈现从扩散（diffusion）到亚扩散（subdiffusion）的行为。在所有情况下，由于碎片化，自旋输运都由电荷输运介导，并具有特定的磁化依赖性。

Conclusion: 碎片化导致受扰模型在巨正则平均（grandcanonical average）下出现亚扩散，其机制与无序（disordered）或偶极守恒（dipole-conserving）模型中的亚扩散机制不同。这表明碎片化在强关联系统中创造了独特的输运现象。

Abstract: The $t$-model represents the Hubbard model in the limit $U \to \infty$ and is one of the basic models of strongly correlated electrons. On a one-dimensional chain, the model is integrable, and the charge dynamics corresponds to that of free spinless fermions. However, the sequence of spins is frozen, leading to the Hilbert space fragmentation and nontrivial spin dynamics. We consider integrable and perturbed models with perturbations that break integrability while preserving fragmentation, and show that they exhibit various types of spin dynamics, from ballistic transport to anomalous diffusion in the integrable case, and from diffusion to subdiffusion in the perturbed case. Due to fragmentation, in all cases considered, spin transport is mediated by charge transport, with a particular magnetization dependence, most notably leading to subdiffusion in the grandcanonical average of the perturbed model, with a mechanism distinct from subdiffusion in disordered or dipole-conserving models.

</details>


### [32] [Quantum Fisher Information as a Probe of Critical Scaling in Frustrated Magnets: Signatures from Kagome Quantum Spin Liquid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19951)
*Zhengbang Zhou,Chengkang Zhou,Menghan Song,Yong Baek Kim,Zi Yang Meng*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过量子费希尔信息（QFI）分析量子磁体中的多体纠缠，揭示了量子费希尔信息能够区分传统朗道范式下的量子临界点与具有分数化和规范结构的非常规量子临界点，并在kagome晶格量子自旋液体模型中验证了这一能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子费希尔信息（Quantum Fisher information, QFI）作为多体量子纠缠的度量，可从量子磁体的非弹性中子散射数据中获取。本研究旨在验证QFI能否有效区分传统朗道范式下的量子临界点（quantum critical point, QCP）与具有分数化和涌现规范结构的非常规量子临界点。

Method: 研究采用大规模量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo, QMC）模拟和精确对角化方法，计算了具有XY和团簇伊辛相互作用的kagome晶格量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid, QSL）模型中的QFI。对于铁磁XY相互作用，使用QMC获取QFI；对于反铁磁XY相互作用，则通过精确对角化研究QFI的热力学和动力学性质。

Result: 当XY相互作用为铁磁性时，QMC获得的QFI显示出较大的反常维度，这是从铁磁相到ℤ₂ QSL相变的(2+1)d XY*普适类的特征指纹。对于反铁磁XY相互作用，通过QFI、真实多体负性等纠缠探针以及能谱和结构因子分析，表明存在向可能不同的QSL相的转变。

Conclusion: 这些结果不仅证明了QFI在识别QSL态和非常规QCP方面的多功能性，还为未来受挫磁体的理论和实验研究提供了有用的指导。QFI能够有效区分传统与非常规量子临界点，并揭示量子相变的普适类特征。

Abstract: Quantum Fisher information (QFI) is a measure of multipartite quantum entanglement that can be obtained from inelastic neutron scattering data on quantum magnets. In this work, we demonstrate that the QFI can distinguish an unconventional quantum critical point (QCP) with fractionalization and emergent gauge structure from conventional ones within the Landau paradigm. We compute the QFI, via large-scale quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) simulations and exact diagonalization, in a kagome lattice quantum spin liquid (QSL) model with an XY and a cluster-Ising interactions. When the XY interaction is ferromagetic, the QFI obtained by QMC reveals a large anomalous dimension, which is a fingerprint of the (2+1)d XY$^\ast$ universality class for the transition from the ferromagnetic phase to the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ QSL. The investigation of thermal and dynamical properties of QFI is further extended to the case of antiferromagnetic XY interaction via exact diagonalization. In this regime, a transition to a possibly distinct QSL phase is suggested via both entanglement-based probes, such as QFI and genuine multipartite negativity, and analyses of the energy spectrum and structure factors. These results not only demonstrate the versatility of QFI in identifying QSL states and unconventional QCPs but also provide useful guidance for future theoretical and experimental studies of frustrated magnets.

</details>

### [33] [Harnessing Non-Boltzmann Steady States in Lanthanide Nanocrystals for Mid-Infrared Optoelectronics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19644)
*Xinyang Yu,Yin Huang,Karin Yamamura,Chenyi Wang,Lei Ding,Mehran Kianinia,Yang Yu,Jiyun Kim,Baolei Liu,Xiaoxue Xu,Otto Cranwell Schaeper,Yue Bian,Lan Fu,Guochen Bao,Qian Peter Su,Fan Wang,Igor Aharonovich,Chaohao Chen*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究展示了一种基于镧系元素纳米晶体的新型中红外探测方法，通过非玻尔兹曼稳态实现超低功率、高灵敏度的中红外到可见光/近红外转换，可用于室温中红外成像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将中红外（MIR）辐射转换为可见光或近红外波长对于成像和传感至关重要，但实现灵敏、低功耗且可扩展的检测仍然具有挑战性。传统镧系元素纳米晶体通常受玻尔兹曼统计限制，将粒子数分布与晶格温度绑定，从而限制了信号对比度。

Method: 研究中红外辐射重新平衡耗散弛豫途径，驱动镧系元素发射体进入非玻尔兹曼稳态（non-Boltzmann steady state），实现对粒子数分布的非热控制。利用这一机制实现比率计量响应，该响应本质上与泵浦功率无关。

Result: 在6.8至8.6微米波长范围内实现了相对于中红外功率的线性中红外检测。比率计量响应可在10微瓦的超低激发功率下工作，比传统方法低几个数量级。使用标准硅光电探测器实现了室温中红外成像，检测极限接近4纳瓦/微米²。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了镧系元素纳米粒子作为纳米光子系统中高效中红外转换和传感平台的地位，通过非玻尔兹曼稳态机制突破了传统热平衡限制，实现了超低功率的室温中红外检测与成像。

Abstract: Converting mid-infrared (MIR) radiation to visible or near-infrared wavelengths is essential for imaging and sensing, yet achieving sensitive, low-power, and scalable detection remains challenging. Lanthanide nanocrystals provide an alternative through ratiometric luminescence but are typically constrained by Boltzmann statistics, which tie population distributions to lattice temperature and limit signal contrast. Here we show that MIR irradiation rebalances dissipative relaxation pathways, driving lanthanide emitters into a non-Boltzmann steady state that enables non-thermal control of population distributions. This allows emission behaviors inaccessible under thermal equilibrium. We exploit this regime to achieve linear MIR detection with respect to MIR power across 6.8 to 8.6 micrometers. The ratiometric response is intrinsically independent of the pump power, enabling operation at an ultralow excitation power of 10 uW, several orders of magnitude lower than conventional approaches. Using standard silicon photodetectors, we then demonstrate room-temperature MIR imaging with detection limits approaching 4 nW um-2. Our results establish lanthanide nanoparticles as an efficient platform for MIR conversion and sensing in nanophotonic systems.

</details>


### [34] [Anisotropic propagation of GHz surface and bulk acoustic waves in gallium arsenide studied by random scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19860)
*T. A. Steenbergen,M. M. Wohlfarth,P. E. Veefkind,M. Fisicaro,W. Löffler*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解晶体中复杂的各向异性声学传播对于优化表面和体声波器件性能至关重要。研究旨在通过理论和实验方法探究(001)切割砷化镓中GHz声学模式的各向异性和耦合特性。

Method: 首先数值计算表面和体模式的角相关相速度（angle-dependent phase velocities），并提供可适应不同材料系统的代码。通过叉指换能器（interdigital transducer）激发表面模式验证理论模型，利用声波随机散射实现全向声学传播。使用扫描光学干涉仪（scanning optical interferometer）测量复杂声场，并通过傅里叶域分析（Fourier domain analysis）提取表面和体模式的角相关速度。

Result: 成功实现了对(001)切割砷化镓中GHz声学模式各向异性特性的理论计算和实验验证。开发了可适应不同材料系统的计算代码，并通过扫描光学干涉测量技术精确提取了表面和体声学模式的角相关传播速度。

Conclusion: 该方法可用于通过研究表面和体模式的损耗来优化GHz范围的经典和量子声学器件（classical and quantum acoustic devices）。研究为理解复杂晶体中的声学传播特性提供了有效的理论和实验框架。

Abstract: Understanding the complex anisotropic acoustic propagation in crystals is crucial for optimizing the performance of surface and bulk acoustic wave devices. Here, we investigate the anisotropy and coupling of GHz acoustic modes in (001)-cut gallium arsenide through theory and experiment. We first numerically calculate the angle-dependent phase velocities for surface and bulk modes, and we provide a code which can easily be adapted to different material systems. We validate our theoretical model experimentally by exciting surface modes with an interdigital transducer, and achieve omnidirectional acoustic propagation through random scattering of the acoustic waves. We measure the complex acoustic field with a scanning optical interferometer, and extract the angle-dependent velocities of surface and bulk modes using Fourier domain analysis. Our method could be used for the optimization of GHz-range classical and quantum acoustic devices, by studying losses of surface and bulk modes.

### [35] [Non-Hermitian skin effect in a two-dimensional Lieb photonic crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19932)
*Zhi-Kang Xiong,Tianlei Wen,Y. Liu,Hai Lin,Bin Zhou*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Lieb晶格的非厄米耦合紧束缚模型（tight-binding model），通过复折射率（complex refractive indices）模拟非厄米耦合。在具有倾斜边界的光子晶体平板中构造几何依赖的趋肤模式，并通过全波模拟（full wave simulation）进行验证。

Result: 在特定本征态中识别出非平凡谱缠绕数（spectral winding number），该数转化为具有倾斜边界的光子晶体平板中的几何依赖趋肤模式。全波模拟验证了几何趋肤效应的边界依赖性。

Conclusion: 该工作强调了几何趋肤效应的边界依赖性，并通过先进拓扑超材料平台为经典波系统提供了易于实现的非厄米趋肤效应具体原型设计。

Abstract: In this contribution paper, we construct a two-dimensional non-Hermitian (NH) photonic crystal (PhC) to prototype its NH skin effect for experimental proposal. Based on the tight-binding model for Lieb lattice with NH coupling, a nontrivial spectral winding number is pinpointed for certain eigenstates, which translates to geometry-dependent skin modes in a PhC slab with tilt boundaries. For ease of implementation, complex refractive indices are employed for the Lieb unit cell of PhC to emulate the NH coupling. Validated by full wave simulation, our work under scores the boundary dependence of the geometric skin effect, and provides a concrete prototype design of NH skin effect easily implemented in classical wave systems by state-of-the-art of topological metamaterial platforms.

Method: 采用综述研究方法，系统总结了多种非贵金属纳米颗粒中局域表面等离子体共振的研究。涵盖了铝、锑、铋、铬、铜、镓、铟、铅、镁、钼、镍、钾、硒、钠、碲、锡、钛、钨和锌等20种金属。

Conclusion: 该综述系统比较了非贵金属的等离子体特性，为读者简要介绍了这些金属在等离子体应用中的潜力，为非贵金属在表面增强拉曼光谱等特定应用中的选择提供了参考依据。

Abstract: Localized surface plasmon resonances are self-sustained, collective oscillations of free electrons in metallic nanostructures. They have a wide range of applications. The most common plasmonic metals are noble metals, such as gold and silver. However, there are applications, such as surface-enhanced Raman spectroscopy, in which using non-noble metals is advantageous. This review summarizes the investigation of localized surface plasmons in non-noble metal nanoparticles, providing an overview of the plasmonic properties of non-noble metals. Our summary therefore compares the plasmonic properties of non-noble metals and briefly introduces their potential to the readers.

### [37] [Structure and Classification of Matrix Product Quantum Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19866)
*Giorgio Stucchi,J. Ignacio Cirac,Rahul Trivedi,Georgios Styliaris*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了矩阵乘积量子信道（MPQC）框架，用于描述一维张量网络中的完全正定保迹映射。研究表明，具有局部纯化性质的平移不变信道仅产生短程关联，且所有此类信道属于单一相态。扩展框架还展示了某些能产生长程纠缠的信道可通过两轮测量和前馈在常数深度内确定性地实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在开发矩阵乘积量子信道（Matrix Product Quantum Channels, MPQCs）的框架，这是一种用于描述完全正定保迹映射的一维张量网络表示。研究聚焦于具有局部纯化性质的平移不变信道，以理解其相关性质和实现能力。

Method: 采用张量网络方法，构建矩阵乘积量子信道框架，特别关注由单一重复张量生成的平移不变信道。通过分析其纯化等距映射的实现方式，证明这些信道可通过常数深度的砖墙量子电路实现。同时将框架扩展到能产生长程纠缠的平移不变信道类别。

Result: 研究发现，具有局部纯化性质的平移不变信道的纯化等距映射总可通过常数深度砖墙量子电路实现，表明此类信道仅产生短程关联。与幺正情形不同，所有局部纯化信道属于单一相态，可连续相互变形。扩展框架显示，某些能产生长程纠缠的信道可通过两轮测量和前馈在常数深度内确定性地实现。

Conclusion: 矩阵乘积量子信道框架为分析一维量子信道提供了有力工具。局部纯化信道仅产生短程关联且属于单一相态，而扩展框架表明更广泛的信道类别仍可在常数深度内实现，这为量子信息处理中的信道设计和实现提供了重要理论指导。

Abstract: We develop a framework for Matrix Product Quantum Channels (MPQCs), a one-dimensional tensor-network description of completely positive, trace-preserving maps. We focus on translation-invariant channels, generated by a single repeated tensor, that admit a local purification. We show that their purifying isometry can always be implemented by a constant-depth brickwork quantum circuit, implying that such channels generate only short-range correlations. In contrast to the unitary setting, where one-dimensional quantum cellular automata (in one-to-one correspondence with matrix product unitaries) carry a nontrivial index, we prove that all locally purified channels belong to a single phase, that is, they can be continuously deformed into one another. We then extend the framework to a broader class of translation-invariant channels capable of generating long-range entanglement and show that these remain deterministically implementable in constant depth using two rounds of measurements and feedforward.

</details>


### [38] [Bright oxygen- and vacancy-derived spin-singlet diamond color centers with metastable spin triplets: OV$^{2+}$ and VOV$^{2+}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20073)
*John Mark P. Martirez*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 通过嵌入多组态量子力学理论，本研究确定了ST1金刚石色心为V_CO_CV_C^{2+}缺陷结构，解决了其十余年未解的结构问题。该缺陷具有自旋单重态基态和亚稳态自旋三重态，计算激发能与实验零声子线高度吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ST1金刚石色心（ST1 diamond color center）的实验特征表明其涉及氧原子取代（O_C）和碳空位（V_C），具有自旋单重态基态和亚稳态自旋三重态，但其具体结构已十余年未被解析。

Method: 采用嵌入多组态量子力学理论（embedded multiconfigurational quantum mechanical theory），研究O_C-V_C衍生的金刚石缺陷，包括0和+2电荷态的耦合O_CV_C，以及沿[110]轴被V_C包围的O_C（V_CO_CV_C）。

Result: 发现O_CV_C^{2+}（C_{3v}对称性）和V_CO_CV_C^{2+}（C_{2v}对称性）均具有自旋单重态基态（1^1A_1）和亚稳态自旋三重态。确定ST1为V_CO_CV_C^{2+}缺陷，其第一（1^1B_2）和第二（2^1A_1）亮自旋单重态激发态的垂直激发能与ST1实验零声子线（2.2-2.3 eV）高度匹配。

Conclusion: ST1金刚石色心的结构被确定为V_CO_CV_C^{2+}缺陷。两个氧孤对电子（O lone pairs）有利于形成V_CO_CV_C而非O_CV_C，这与氮孤对电子（N lone pair）促进N_CV_C中心形成的机制相似。

Abstract: The ST1 diamond color center was experimentally demonstrated to involve a substitutional oxygen atom (O$_C$) and carbon vacancy (V$_C$), has a spin singlet ground-state, and a metastable electron spin ancilla: a triplet. ST1's structure was left unsolved for more than a decade. With embedded multiconfigurational quantum mechanical theory, we investigate O$_C$-V$_C$-derived diamond defects, specifically both 0 and +2-charged coupled O$_C$V$_C$, and O$_C$ surrounded by V$_C$s along the [110] axis (V$_C$O$_C$V$_C$). We found both O$_C$V$_{C}^{2+}$ (C$_{3v}$) and V$_C$O$_C$V$_{C}^{2+}$ (C$_{2v}$) to have a spin-singlet ground state (1$^1$A$_1$) and metastable spin triplets. We demonstrate ST1 to be V$_C$O$_C$V$_{C}^{2+}$. The calculated vertical excitation energies of V$_C$O$_C$V$_{C}^{2+}$'s first (1$^1$B$_2$) and second (2$^1$A$_1$) bright spin-singlet excited states closely match ST1's experimental zero phonon line (2.2-2.3 eV). O$_C$V$_{C}^{2+}$ ($^1$E) absorbs much higher (2.8 eV). The two O lone pairs favor V$_C$O$_C$V$_C$ over O$_C$V$_C$, in a similar manner as the single N lone pair favors formation of N$_C$V$_C$ centers.

</details>
