### [39] [The classification problem for unitary R-Matrices with two eigenvalues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20158)
*Gandalf Lechner*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 该论文对具有恰好两个不同特征值的任意有限维酉R矩阵进行分类，考虑其辫群表示特征给出的自然等价关系。除一个在大于2的偶数维中可能存在或不存在的类别外，获得了完整的分类定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在解决对具有恰好两个不同特征值的任意有限维酉R矩阵（unitary R-matrices）进行分类的问题。这一分类问题在辫群（braid group）表示理论中具有重要意义，因为R矩阵是构造辫群表示的关键代数结构。

Method: 研究方法基于考虑辫群表示特征（characters of braid group representations）给出的自然等价关系。通过这种等价关系对R矩阵进行分类，将具有相同辫群表示特征的R矩阵视为等价。

Result: 研究获得了几乎完整的分类定理，除一个在大于2的偶数维中可能存在或不存在的类别外，所有满足条件的酉R矩阵都被分类。这表明具有两个不同特征值的酉R矩阵结构受到严格限制。

Conclusion: 论文成功描述了具有恰好两个不同特征值的任意有限维酉R矩阵的分类问题，并在考虑辫群表示特征等价关系下获得了接近完整的分类结果。唯一的未确定情况涉及一个在大于2的偶数维中可能存在或不存在的类别。

Abstract: The problem of classifying all unitary R-matrices of arbitrary finite dimension that have precisely two distinct eigenvalues is described, working up to a natural equivalence relation given by the characters of their braid group representations. Up to one class that might or might not exist in even dimension larger than two, a full classification theorem is obtained.

</details>

### [40] [Tailoring Corner States and Exceptional Points in Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19378)
*Xiao-Ming Zhao,Cui-Xian Guo,Xin-Ran Ma,Xiao-Ran Wang,Su-Peng Kou*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets）具有净磁化强度为零但受晶体对称性强制的动量依赖自旋劈裂特性。本研究旨在探索耗散二维交变磁体中的非厄米效应，以揭示其与传统反铁磁体不同的拓扑性质。

Method: 采用非厄米拓扑理论分析对称性兼容耗散诱导的虚交错交换场（imaginary staggered exchange field）。通过手征趋肤效应（chiral skin effect）框架描述混合趋肤-拓扑模式，并利用转移矩阵方法（transfer matrix method）解析证明边界子晶格终止对角落态的控制机制。

Result: 在拓扑非平凡相中，交变磁体的d波各向异性驱动了混合趋肤-拓扑模式；在无能隙相中，阐明了异常点（exceptional points）的产生和湮灭动力学。边界子晶格终止确定性地控制角落态，且由于对称性约束和手征态的鲁棒性，这些发现在所有拓扑交变磁体中普遍成立。

Conclusion: 建立了控制拓扑角态的一般框架，为设计具有定制非厄米特性的磁性材料提供了新策略。对称性约束确保了这些发现在所有拓扑交变磁体中的普适性，为非厄米拓扑磁学研究开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Altermagnets (AMs) exhibit vanishing net magnetization but strong momentum-dependent spin splitting enforced by crystal symmetry. Here, we explore the non-Hermitian effects in dissipative two-dimensional AMs. We show that symmetry-compliant dissipation naturally induces an imaginary staggered exchange field, driving a NH topological phase transition absent in conventional antiferromagnets. In the topologically nontrivial phase, hybrid skin-topological modes driven by altermagnetic d-wave anisotropy emerge, as captured by the chiral skin effect framework. In the gapless phase, we elucidate the creation and annihilation dynamics of exceptional points. Crucially, we analytically prove via the transfer matrix method that corner states are deterministically controlled by the boundary sublattice termination. Owing to the symmetry constraints and the robustness of chiral states, these findings hold universally across all topological AMs. A general framework is established for controlling topological corner states, offering a new strategy for designing magnetic materials with tailored non-Hermitian properties.

</details>

Abstract: Memory is a foundational concept across disciplines, from neurobiology and electronics to artificial intelligence and quantum gravity. In materials, memory effects typically arise from ferroic orders, such as ferroelectricity and ferromagnetism, where information is stored in charge or spin degrees of freedom. Here, we report a surprising discovery of a nonvolatile superlattice memory effect in monolayer TaIrTe4, a dual quantum spin Hall insulator, where information is encoded through sharply contrasting lattice periodicities. In particular, in a pristine monolayer, we observe the spontaneous emergence of a long-period superlattice that can be programmed ON and OFF in a nonvolatile manner by electrostatic tuning of low-energy electronic states. This switching toggles the system between two structural configurations with unit cell areas differing by nearly two orders of magnitude. Mechanistically, our results reveal two independent and distinct instabilities, one in the lattice and the other in the QSH electrons, which are coupled, leading to electrostatic control of lattice configurations with nonvolatile memory. Combined with the QSH topology, this stability offers a promising route to nonvolatile memory control of topological flat bands and their filling enabled quantum states. Our preliminary data indeed show the emergence of new insulating states at fractional superlattice fillings, which can be clearly switched ON and OFF together with the superlattice.

In our approach, the exchange splitting in the ferromagnetic materials and the spin-orbit coupling (SOC) of the Dresselhaus and Rashba types in the semiconductors are included, allowing control of the wave vector associated with the spin states.
  The tunnel magnetoresistance (TMR) is calculated at low temperature as a function of the semiconductor thickness, parameterized with respect to the crystallographic axis that favors the magnetization direction in the ferromagnetic electrodes, within the Landauer--Büttiker formalism in the single-channel regime. The results show that the TMR reaches its maximum value independently of the relative orientation between the magnetization vector and the crystallographic direction. The most efficient configuration corresponds to Fe_{90}Cr_{10}/GaSb/Fe_{90}Cr_{10}, with a TMR value of 83.60%. Furthermore, the Dresselhaus SOC contributes more significantly to the TMR than the Rashba SOC. Finally, the TMR varies when the electrodes L_j are permuted, due to differences in their Fermi energies. The energy renormalization of tightly bound excitons is analyzed through the exchange interaction between the electron (or hole) component of the exciton and resident carriers that share the same spin and valley quantum numbers. Our theory explains the weak energy shift of excitonic resonances despite the strong energy renormalization of resident carriers. ### [46] [Helicity-Selective Phonon Absorption and Phonon-Induced Spin Torque from Interfacial Spin-Lattice Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19686)

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了在反演对称性破缺的磁性异质结构中，Rashba效应导致的界面自旋-晶格耦合（interfacial spin-lattice coupling）机制，该机制不依赖晶格变形梯度，使得面内声波能够对磁化施加自旋力矩（spin torque），为高效声子驱动磁器件开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究反演对称性破缺的磁性异质结构中，由Rashba效应产生的界面自旋-晶格耦合的动态后果。这种界面耦合在自旋与晶格之间的角动量转换中扮演着关键但常被忽视的角色。

Method: 研究方法包括：将界面自旋-晶格耦合用磁化强度和晶格位移的圆形变量（circular variables）表达，从而揭示出不依赖晶格变形梯度的直接界面诱导螺旋性-螺旋性耦合（helicity-helicity coupling）。

Result: 研究结果表明，该界面耦合导致螺旋性依赖的声子吸收（helicity-dependent phonon absorption），使得面内声波能够对磁化施加自旋力矩，这种效应在薄磁性薄膜中占主导地位。

Conclusion: 该研究强调了反演不对称界面在自旋与晶格角动量转换中的关键作用，为通过界面工程实现高效声子驱动磁器件（phonon-driven magnetic devices）开辟了可能性。

Abstract: In magnetic heterostructures with broken inversion symmetry, the Rashba effect gives rise to a gradient-free interaction between magnons and phonons, which we term interfacial spin-lattice coupling. Here, we investigate the dynamic consequences of this interfacial coupling in ferromagnetic heterostructures. By expressing the interaction in terms of circular variables for magnetization and lattice displacement, we reveal a direct interface-induced helicity-helicity coupling hat does not rely on lattice deformation gradients. Consequently, it leads to helicity-dependent phonon absorption, enabling in-plane acoustic waves to exert a spin torque on the magnetization, which becomes dominant in thin magnetic films. Our findings highlight the crucial, yet overlooked, role of inversion-asymmetric interfaces in angular-momentum conversion between spin and lattice, opening up possibilities for efficient phonon-driven magnetic devices that are enabled by interface engineering.

### [47] [Commensurate moiré superlattices in anisotropically strained twisted bilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19694)
*Ayan Mondal,Bheema Lingam Chittari*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了各向异性应变如何重组扭曲双层石墨烯中相称的莫尔超晶格和电子结构，揭示了两种不同的相称几何结构及其对魔角物理现象持续性的解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于实验观察：在角度无序和异质应变条件下，魔角现象学（magic angle phenomenology）仍保持稳健性。这促使研究者探索各向异性应变如何超越原始扭转角极限，控制相称莫尔物理。

Method: 通过构建由顶部石墨烯层施加的一般各向异性应变生成的精确相称莫尔超晶胞（commensurate moiré supercells），在固定有效莫尔变形下，特别关注±6.008°扭转角，分析不同几何结构。

Result: 研究发现两种不同且对称性不等价的相称几何结构：倾斜二维莫尔超晶格（tilted two dimensional moiré superlattices）和准一维条纹状图案（quasi one dimensional stripe like patterns）。各向异性应变通过减少莫尔布里渊区（moiré Brillouin zone）中的狄拉克点数量，定性重塑了低能带结构。

Conclusion: 各向异性应变是超越原始扭转角极限、控制相称莫尔物理的统一几何机制。倾斜二维结构解释了魔角物理在有限畸变窗口内的持续性，而准一维莫尔图案则表现出维度约简和霍夫施塔特蝴蝶分裂（Hofstadter butterfly splitting）。

Abstract: We investigate how anisotropic strain reorganizes commensurate moiré superlattices and electronic structure in twisted bilayer graphene across a finite range of twist angles. Motivated by experiments demonstrating robust magic angle phenomenology under angular disorder and heterostrain, we construct exact commensurate moiré supercells generated by general anisotropic strain applied to the top graphene layer. At fixed effective moiré deformation, with particular focus on the $\pm 6.008^\circ$ twist angle, we uncover two distinct and symmetry inequivalent commensurate geometries: tilted two dimensional moiré superlattices and quasi one dimensional stripe like patterns. Anisotropic strain qualitatively reshapes the low energy band structure by reducing the number of Dirac points in the moiré Brillouin zone, leading to sharply different electronic and magnetic field responses in these regimes. Strikingly, tilted two dimensional structures near pristine angles preserve bandwidths and AA region localization comparable to the unstrained case, providing a natural explanation for the persistence of magic angle physics over a finite distortion window, whereas quasi one dimensional moiré patterns exhibit dimensional reduction and immediate Hofstadter butterfly splitting at infinitesimal magnetic fields. Our results identify anisotropic strain as a unifying geometric mechanism controlling commensurate moiré physics beyond the pristine twist angle limit.

### [48] [Flying qubits Surfing on Plasmons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19720)
*D. C. Glattli,P. Roulleau*

TL;DR: 该文提出了一种统一理论，将石墨烯等低维导体中飞行的量子比特（flying qubits）的单电子动力学与集体等离子体激元（plasmonic）模式相结合，为GHz/THz频率下的量子输运提供了新框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯等低维导体中飞行的量子比特（flying qubits）的快速发展将量子电子学推向了超快领域，传统输运理论不再适用。现有理论框架要么描述费米子单粒子动力学，要么描述玻色子等离子体激元（plasmonic）模式，未能将两者统一。

Method: 从规范不变（gauge-invariant）的散射方法出发，构建了动力学量子输运的统一理论。该理论表明，时间依赖的单电子激发会自洽地产生传播的内部势，其行为类似于集体等离子体激元（plasmonic）模式。

Result: 电子以费米速度传播的同时，在自诱导的等离子体波上"冲浪"，该波的速度通过库仑相互作用和屏蔽效应被重整化（renormalized）。该动力学平均场（dynamical mean-field）框架能在单一描述中捕捉光子辅助输运、电荷弛豫和边缘磁等离子体激元（edge magnetoplasmon）动力学。

Conclusion: 通过统一单电子和等离子体激元（plasmonic）图像，该结果为GHz/THz频率下石墨烯中飞行的量子比特（flying qubits）实验的解释和控制提供了及时的理论基础。

Abstract: The rapid emergence of flying qubits in graphene and other low-dimensional conductors is pushing quantum electronics into an ultrafast regime where conventional transport theories no longer apply. In these systems, single-electron wave packets propagate coherently over micrometer scales while interacting with collective charge excitations on comparable time scales. Yet existing theoretical frameworks describe either fermionic single-particle dynamics or bosonic plasmonic modes, without reconciling the two. Here we introduce a unified theory of dynamical quantum transport that bridges this long-standing divide. Starting from a gauge-invariant scattering approach, we show how a time-dependent single-electron excitation self-consistently generates a propagating internal potential that behaves as a collective plasmonic mode. Electrons propagate at the Fermi velocity while simultaneously 'surfing' on this self-induced plasmon wave, whose velocity is renormalized by Coulomb interactions and screening. This dynamical mean-field framework captures photon-assisted transport, charge relaxation, and edge magnetoplasmon dynamics within a single description and remains valid far beyond the low-frequency limit. By unifying single-electron and plasmonic pictures, our results provide a timely foundation for the interpretation and control of flying-qubit experiments in graphene at gigahertz/terahertz frequencies.

</details>


### [49] [Twist-Tuned Magnonic Nanocavity Mode in a Trilayer Moiré Superlattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19729)
*Tianyu Yang,Gianluca Gubbiotti,Marco Madami,Haiming Yu,Jilei Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

Motivation: 莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）概念近期被引入磁振子学（magnonics）领域，为纳米尺度磁振子器件中的自旋波（spin wave）传播和局域化提供了前所未有的调控能力。本研究旨在探索三层磁性莫尔超晶格结构中纳米腔的特性，以拓展未来莫尔磁振子器件的设计途径。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法研究由反点阵列（antidot lattices）构成的三层磁性莫尔超晶格结构。通过调控中间层的扭转角度，分析磁振子能带结构（magnonic band structure）的可调谐性，重点关注特征平带（flat bands）及其对应的纳米腔模式形成。

Result: 在3度最优扭转角下，平带频率激发产生线宽为175纳米的纳米腔模式。与双层结构不同，三层磁振子莫尔超晶格在外层形成反相位纳米腔模式（antiphase nanocavity modes），而中间层无纳米腔形成。纳米腔模式的开关和分布可通过调控中间层扭转角实现，并伴随强烈的磁振子强度局域化。

Conclusion: 三层磁振子莫尔结构在可调谐性方面具有显著优势，为未来莫尔磁振子器件的设计开辟了新途径。通过调控中间层扭转角可有效控制纳米腔模式的开关和分布，实现自旋波的高效局域化。

Abstract: The concept of moiré superlattices has recently been introduced into the field of magnonics, enabling unprecedented control over spin-wave propagation and confinement in nanoscale magnonic devices. In this work, we report a numerical investigation on the nanocavity in a trilayer magnetic moiré superlattice structure consisting of antidot lattices. By tuning the middle layer twist angle, high tunability of the magnonic band structure can be achieved with characteristic flat bands and the corresponding nanocavity mode formation in outer layers. At an optimal twist angle of 3 deg, excitation at the flat band frequency yields nanocavity mode with linewidth of 175 nm. In contrast to its bilayer counterpart, the trilayer magnonic moiré superlattice exhibits antiphase nanocavity modes in the outer layers while showing no nanocavity formation in the middle layer. Our study indicates that the switching and distribution of the nanocavity modes can be governed by tuning the middle layer twist angle with a strong magnon intensity confinement. The trilayer magnonic moiré structure holds a distinct advantage in tunability, which opens up new avenues for the design of future moiré magnonic devices.

### [50] [Magnon-Driven Anomalous Hall Effect in Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19737)
*Zheng Liu,Yang Gao,Qian Niu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索反铁磁体中手性磁振子与手性电子运动之间的直接相互作用，这为通过磁振子探测手性并控制电子手性提供了新途径。

Method: 采用密度矩阵微扰理论（density-matrix perturbation theory）和对称性分析（symmetry analysis），并构建了一个具有CrSb反铁磁体相同对称性的最小晶格模型（minimal lattice model）进行验证。

Result: 结果表明，霍尔电导率完全由奈尔序进动（Néel-order precession）的手性决定，与平衡奈尔序产生的反常霍尔效应形成鲜明对比。该效应具有不同的对称性要求，即使在后者被对称性禁止的情况下也能存在。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了手性磁振子与手性电子运动之间的直接相互作用，为探测磁振子手性和通过磁振子控制电子手性开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We propose a magnon-driven anomalous Hall effect in altermagnets, arising from the coupling between coherently excited chiral magnons and chiral electronic motion. Using density-matrix perturbation theory and symmetry analysis, we show that the resulting Hall conductivity is solely determined by the chiralithy of the Néel-order precession, in sharp contrast to the anomalous Hall effect from the equilibrium Néel order. It then has distinct symmetry requirements from the latter and can exist even when the latter is forbidden by symmetry. The magnon-driven anomalous Hall effect is exemplified in a minimal lattice model with the same symmetry of the altermagnet CrSb, which hosts no static anomalous Hall effect. Our results reveal a direct interplay between chiral magnons and chiral electronic motion, paving the way of probing magnon chirality and to control electronic chirality through magnons.

### [51] [Increasing valley splitting in Si/SiGe by practically achievable heterostructure profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19769)
*Lukas Cvitkovich,Peter Stano,Dominique Bougeard,Yann-Michel Niquet,Daniel Loss*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种增强硅基自旋量子比特中谷分裂（valley splitting）的新方法，通过将谷间耦合重新解释为在含锗原子晶面上的点状杂质背散射，并利用多个散射体的相长干涉来显著提升谷分裂能量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅基自旋量子比特受限于导带谷简并（valley degeneracy），在纳米器件中界面和合金无序虽能解除简并，但产生的谷分裂（valley splitting）通常很小（约100 μeV）。现有解决方案要么依赖难以控制的界面原子细节，要么要求超出当前异质结外延技术水平的异质结构剖面。

Method: 研究重新审视了非平凡锗（Ge）剖面引起的谷分裂，提出将谷间耦合（intervalley coupling）视为在含锗原子晶面上的点状杂质背散射（backscattering）的新视角。该方法强调通过多个散射体的相长干涉（constructive interference）来增强背散射振幅，从而提升谷分裂，而不要求异质结构生长方向上的锗含量具有特定周期性。

Result: 研究通过紧束缚模拟（tight-binding simulations）和物理解释提供了数值证据，表明即使没有特定周期性（包括难以实现的2π/(2k₀)周期），也能显著增加谷分裂。研究设计了在当前分子束外延（MBE）生长技术能力范围内的剖面，可将谷分裂提升至超过1 meV的尺度。

Conclusion: 该研究为克服硅基量子比特的谷问题提供了新思路，通过重新理解谷间耦合的物理机制并利用相长干涉效应，提出了在现有外延技术条件下可实现的、能显著增强谷分裂的异质结构设计方案。

Abstract: Silicon spin qubits are marred by the valley degeneracy of the conduction band. In a nanodevice, the degeneracy is lifted by interfaces and alloy disorder, but the arising valley splitting is small, of order 100 $μ$eV in Si/SiGe quantum wells. Substantial efforts were invested both in theory and experiments to overcome the valley issue. Unfortunately, the existing recipes either rely on atomistic details of the interface that are beyond experimental control, or demand heterostructure profiles beyond current state-of-the-art heterostructure epitaxy. We revisit the valley splitting induced by non-trivial Ge profiles and advocate a novel view of the intervalley coupling as a backscattering on point-like impurities realized by crystal planes containing Ge atoms. This perspective reveals that enhancing the backscattering amplitude, which sets the valley splitting, requires constructive interference of multiple scatterers. % We arrive at a remarkable prediction, that the Ge content along the heterostructure growth direction does not have to have any specific periodicity, including the practically unreachable $2π/(2k_0)$ period, to significantly increase the valley splitting. This statement is corroborated with numerical evidence from tight-binding simulations and intuitive physical interpretations. We devise profiles that seem within the capabilities of current MBE growth techniques and boost the valley splitting beyond the 1\,meV scale.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，激子谷相干性（exciton valley coherence）的生成需要线性偏振光作为外部相干驱动，而圆偏振光无法诱导相干性。本研究旨在探索通过激发场偏振特性控制不同激子物种相干性的新机制。

Method: 研究开发了一个统一的微观开放量子系统框架（open-quantum-system framework），采用包含亮-暗激子相互作用（bright-dark exciton interactions）的五能级模型，分析单层WSe2中激子行为。通过连续调节激发场偏振椭圆度（polarization ellipticity）实现相干状态间的可控转变。

Result: 线性偏振激发产生亮相干性（bright coherence），而圆偏振激发产生暗相干性（dark coherence）。磁场对暗相干性具有双重优势：面外磁场抑制相干衰减，面内磁场实现光学读取。这些效应在定量现实的场强下得以实现。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了通过椭圆度驱动相干转移访问隐藏暗态的新机制，为未来量子控制中利用亮-暗谷相干转变开辟了新途径。偏振椭圆度提供了对不同激子物种相干性的选择性控制工具。

Abstract: The generation of exciton valley coherence typically requires linearly polarized (LP) light as an external coherent drive, whereas circularly polarized (CP) light fails to induce coherence. Here, we develop a unified, microscopically-grounded open-quantum-system framework within a five-level model incorporating bright-dark exciton interactions in monolayer WSe2, and demonstrate that the polarization ellipticity of the excitation field provides selective control over distinct exciton species contributing to valley coherence. Specifically, LP and CP excitations generate bright and dark coherence, respectively, with continuous ellipticity tuning enabling controlled transitions between these states. We further reveal dual magnetic advantages for manipulating dark coherence even in the absence of initial coherence: (i) an out-of-plane magnetic field suppresses coherence decay and (ii) an in-plane field enables its optical readout, with quantitatively realistic field strengths. These findings provide a powerful mechanism for accessing hidden dark states via ellipticity-driven coherence transfer, and establish a new pathway for harnessing bright-dark valley-coherence transitions in future quantum control.

### [53] [Anatomy of the modern theory of orbital magnetism from first-principles: term-by-term analysis in the gauge-covariant formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19875)
*Hojun Lee,Insu Baek,Mirco Sastges,Yuriy Mokrousov,Hyun-Woo Lee,Dongwook Go*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过基于贝里相（Berry phase）的现代理论，深入分析了不同材料类别（d过渡金属、sp金属、过渡金属二硫化物）中的轨道磁性，揭示了能带结构特征的微观本质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于深入理解轨道磁性的微观机制，特别是基于贝里相（Berry phase）的现代理论在不同材料体系中的应用。该研究旨在阐明电子轨道的化学性质与能带结构效应之间的相互作用。

Method: 采用Lopez等人提出的规范协变（gauge-covariant）表述的现代理论，该理论能够在任意选择的万尼尔函数（Wannier functions）规范下以可控方式计算轨道磁性，并将总贡献作为规范不变（gauge-invariant）的可测量量。该方法一致地捕获了万尼尔基的异常位置、速度和轨道角动量的贡献，以及哈密顿量的贡献。

Result: 对于d过渡金属，原子中心近似（atom-centered approximation）捕获了现代理论给出的总贡献的大部分，这归因于d电子的局域化性质。然而，5d金属比3d金属表现出更大的偏差，因为5d电子比3d电子更离域。sp金属在两种方法间表现出强烈偏差，其中sp电子的大动能起重要作用。在1H-MoS2中，由于直接带隙中价带和导带的相干杂化，谷轨道矩（valley orbital moment）远超过d电子的原子极限。

Conclusion: 该工作以一致的方式阐明了电子轨道化学性质与能带结构效应之间的相互作用，并强调了贝里相（Berry phase）在轨道磁性中的作用。结果表明，轨道电子学（orbitronics）超越了控制原子轨道，通过利用贝里相可以显著增强轨道磁性。

Abstract: We present an in-depth analysis of the orbital magnetism by means of the so-called modern theory based on the Berry phase across distinct classes of materials-d transition metals, sp metals, and transition metal dichalcogenides-highlighting the microscopic nature of band structure characteristics. We adopt a gauge-covariant formulation of the modern theory proposed in [Lopez et al. Phys. Rev. B 85, 014435 (2012)], which enables the calculation of orbital magnetism in a controlled manner in any chosen gauge of Wannier functions and gives the total contribution as a gauge-invariant measurable. This captures consistently the contributions due to the anomalous position, velocity, and orbital angular momentum of Wannier basis, as well as the contributions due to Hamiltonian such that their sum is gauge-invariant. For d transition metals, we find that the atom-centered approximation captures the majority of the total contribution given by modern theory, which we attribute to localized nature of d electrons. However, 5d metals tend to exhibit larger deviation between the two methods than 3d metals do, as 5d electrons are more delocalized than 3d electrons. On the other hand, sp metals exhibit a strong deviation between the two methods, where large kinetic energy of sp electrons is important. Finally, in 1H-MoS2, we find that the valley orbital moment far exceeds the atomic limit of d electrons due to coherent hybridization between valence and conduction bands in direct band gaps. Our work elucidates the interplay of the chemical nature of electronic orbitals and the effect of band structures in a consistent manner and highlights the role of Berry phase in orbital magnetism. The results suggest a promising direction of orbitronics beyond controlling atomic orbitals, in which the orbital magnetism can be greatly enhanced by exploiting Berry phase.

The optical excitation leads to the creation of Wannier exciton populations, adding new quasi-elastic processes beyond the conventional electronic features to the x-ray scattering spectra. Abstract: In this work, we demonstrate interfacial charge transfer-driven transport enhancement in few-layer graphene monolayer MoS2 vertical heterostructure field-effect transistor. Raman scattering and Raman intensity mapping results confirm the successful stacking of FL graphene on ML MoS2. Pronounced photoluminescence (PL) quenching of MoS2 and spectral redshift in the heterostructure suggest efficient interlayer charge transfer and strong electronic coupling at the vdW interface. Electrical measurements show enhanced drain current, field-effect mobility, and conductivity in Gr-MoS2 device compared to pristine MoS2 transistor with Ag contacts. The energy band considerations under equilibrium and gate bias conditions suggest improved Fermi-level alignment and reduced effective Schottky barrier effects at the graphene-MoS2 interface, enabling efficient carrier injection. Temperature-dependent transport (300-400 K) reveals phonon-dominated mobility and conductivity degradation in both devices; however, the heterostructure exhibits significantly suppressed performance degradation. The mobility enhancement factor increases from ~1.6 at 300 K to ~4.0 at 400 K, accompanied by a corresponding improvement in conductivity stability, demonstrating superior thermal robustness for the Gr-MoS2 heterostructure. The power-law analysis indicates that transport in pristine MoS2 is influenced by both intrinsic phonon scattering and additional thermally activated extrinsic processes such as contact and interfacial effects, whereas the weaker temperature dependence in the Gr-MoS2 device reflects moderated extrinsic contributions and transport behaviour approaching a predominantly phonon-limited regime. These findings demonstrate graphene contact engineering as a viable pathway toward improved performance and thermally stable two-dimensional semiconductor electronics.

### [56] [Reply to: Comment on "Electric conductivity of graphene: Kubo model versus a nonlocal quantum field theory model"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19982)
*Pablo Rodriguez-Lopez,Jian-Sheng Wang,Mauro Antezza*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析评论中的误解点，逐一澄清原论文中从Kubo公式推导Luttinger公式的正确性，并说明模型适用范围的限制。

Result: 确认Phys. Rev. B 111, 115428 (2025)的模型正确预测了无外电场时电流为零的物理要求，反驳了电介质常数存在双极点的说法，并修正了原文中的排版错误。

Conclusion: Phys. Rev. B 111, 115428 (2025)中的所有结果都是完全有效和正确的，与已建立的文献一致，评论中的担忧源于对原文的误解或模型适用范围的不当扩展。

Abstract: In the Comment by Bordag et al. (arXiv:2506.10792), concerns are raised regarding the validity of the results presented in Phys. Rev. B 111, 115428 (2025) (arXiv:2403.02279), where the theoretical descriptions of the electric conductivity of graphene obtained from the Kubo formula and from quantum field theory via the polarization tensor are compared. In this Reply, we show that these concerns arise from misinterpretations of Phys. Rev. B 111, 115428 (2025), in which the results are either inaccurately represented or applied outside the domain of validity of the model. We address the comments concerning the derivation of the Luttinger formula for the electric conductivity from the Kubo formula and clarify why the results of Phys. Rev. B 111, 115428 (2025) cannot be arbitrarily extended to make claims on the gauge invariance. We further demonstrate that our findings are fully consistent with the established and widely accepted literature cited in the Comment. We confirm that the model for electric conductivity discussed in Phys. Rev. B 111, 115428 (2025) correctly predicts a vanishing electric current in the absence of an external electric field, as physically required, and in contrast with the model advocated by the Authors of the Comment. We also show that the electric permittivity does not exhibit a double pole in $ω$, contrary to the claim made in the Comment. Finally, we emphasize that the inclusion of losses is a standard and well-established approach in the study of transport properties of materials, including graphene, and we take the opportunity to correct a few minor typographical errors in Phys. Rev. B 111, 115428 (2025). We show and maintain that all results derived in Phys. Rev. B 111, 115428 (2025) are fully valid and correct.

</details>


### [57] [Domain walls in a dipole-coupled transverse magnetic island chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20018)
*G. M. Wysin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文研究了横向磁纳米岛一维链中的非线性哈密顿运动方程，分析了连接不同均匀静态态的静态畴壁（domain walls）解。研究发现畴壁在特定参数下会形成反铁磁序，这些多样的畴壁结构可能在探测器和开关技术中具有应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究横向磁纳米岛一维链中畴壁（domain walls）的形成机制和特性，旨在理解连接不同均匀静态态的静态畴壁解。该系统包含偶极相互作用、各向异性和外加磁场等多种物理效应，畴壁的多样性可能对参数敏感的探测器和开关技术具有应用价值。

Method: 采用宏观自旋模型（macro-spin model），包含岛间偶极相互作用（dipole interactions）、单轴和易面各向异性（uniaxial and easy-plane anisotropies）以及外加磁场的奥斯特能量（Oersted energy）。通过数值能量弛豫方案（numerical energy relaxation scheme）寻找一般畴壁结构，并使用标量φ⁴理论（scalar φ⁴ theory）描述倾斜态间的畴壁。

Result: 研究发现畴壁最容易在简并均匀态对之间形成，这些态由局部磁化描述为倾斜态（oblique）、y-平行态（y-parallel）和y-交替态（y-alternating）。在某些各向异性和磁场参数下，最近邻偶极相互作用驱动畴壁内部形成反铁磁序（antiferromagnetic order）。倾斜态间的畴壁能用标量φ⁴理论很好地描述。

Conclusion: 该模型呈现了多种畴壁结构，这些结构对参数变化敏感，可能在探测器和开关技术中得到应用。畴壁内部的反铁磁序现象揭示了偶极相互作用在特定参数条件下的重要影响。

Abstract: I analyze the nonlinear Hamiltonian equations of motion for a one-dimensional chain of transverse magnetic nano-islands, seeking solutions for different types of static domain-walls (DWs) connecting uniform static states. The system of elongated magnetic islands oriented transverse ($y$-direction) to the chain direction ($x$-direction) experiences an applied magnetic field transverse to the chain. The macro-spin model includes dipole interactions between islands, their uniaxial and easy-plane anisotropies, and Oersted energy of the applied field. DWs can form most easily between pairs of degenerate uniform states, described by their local magnetizations as oblique, $y$-parallel, and $y$-alternating. The DWs between oblique states are well-described with scalar $\varphi^4$ theory. General DW structures are found via a numerical energy relaxation scheme. At some anisotropy and field parameters, nearest-neighbor dipole interactions drive antiferromagnetic order inside the DW itself. The variety of DWs present in the model might be exploited for their sensitivity to parameter changes in detectors or switching technology.

</details>


### [58] [Micromagnetic Modeling of Surface Acoustic Wave Driven Dynamics: Interplay of Strain, Magnetorotation, and Magnetic Anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20106)
*Florian Millo,Pauline Rovillain,Massimiliano Marangolo,Daniel Stoeffler*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用微磁分析（micromagnetic analysis），完全实现了SAW磁声激发场（magnetoacoustic excitation field），包含所有应变（strain）和晶格旋转（lattice-rotation）项，并考虑具有弱面内单轴各向异性（weak in-plane uniaxial anisotropy）的CoFeB薄膜。

Result: 研究发现各向异性取向（anisotropy orientation）可作为调节平行共振相互作用（parallel resonant interaction）的调控旋钮（knob），为SAW-SW有效耦合提供了条件分析。

Conclusion: 该工作为磁化薄膜中的SAW-SW耦合提供了统一且实用的理论框架，特别强调了各向异性取向在调控平行共振相互作用中的关键作用。

Abstract: We study the coupling mechanism of surface acoustic waves (SAW) with spin waves (SW) using micromagnetic analysis. The SAW magnetoacoustic excitation field is fully implemented, i.e., all strain and lattice-rotation terms are included. A realistic CoFeB film with a weak in-plane uniaxial anisotropy is considered. We investigate the conditions for efficient SAW--SW coupling, with particular emphasis on the case where the SAW propagates parallel to the external magnetic field, a configuration of special interest for magnonic applications. Remarkably, we find that the anisotropy orientation serves as a knob to tune the parallel resonant interaction. Overall, this work provides a unified and practical picture of SAW--SW coupling in thin magnetized films.

### [59] [Understanding Bell locality tests at colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19389)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用贝尔型不等式（Bell-like inequalities）方法，针对μ子对（μ^+ μ^-）和τ子对（τ^+ τ^-）进行检验。

Result: 在满足特定温和假设的前提下，局域隐变量理论可通过μ子和τ子对的贝尔型不等式被证伪。

Conclusion: 满足一组温和假设的局域隐变量理论变得可检验，并可通过μ子和τ子对的贝尔型不等式进行证伪。

Abstract: For decades, it has been known that local hidden variable theories cannot be disproved by collider experiments involving decaying particles. However, if these theories satisfy a small set of mild assumptions, they become testable. In particular, they can be disproved using Bell-like inequalities for $μ^+ μ^-$ and $τ^+ τ^-$ pairs.

### [60] [Global Analyses of Generalized Parton Distributions with Diverse PDF Inputs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19432)
*The MMGPDs Collaboration,Fatemeh Irani,Muhammad Goharipour,K. Azizi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过六次全局分析，探讨了部分子分布函数（PDFs）对零斜度广义部分子分布（GPDs）提取的关键影响，发现使用NNPDF40 PDFs在次领头阶（NLO）下能最佳描述实验数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究部分子分布函数（parton distribution functions, PDFs）在高能物理中的关键作用，特别是其对零斜度（zero skewness）条件下广义部分子分布（generalized parton distributions, GPDs）提取的影响。

Method: 研究采用六次全局分析（global analyses），使用不同现代PDF集（NNPDF40、CT18、MSHT20）在三个特定因子化尺度（μ=2、1.3、1 GeV）和不同微扰阶次下提取GPDs。分析纳入了广泛的弹性电子散射数据，以在动量转移平方t的宽区间内约束GPDs。

Result: 分析显示，使用NNPDF40 PDFs在次领头阶（next-to-leading order, NLO）下能获得对实验数据的最佳总体描述，对PDF输入的选择具有中等敏感性（尤其在低t区域）。微扰阶次的依赖性相对温和，表明提取过程具有稳定性。不同GPD集在较大|t|值时变得更加一致，且下夸克（down-quark）GPDs比上夸克（up-quark）GPDs受到更大抑制。

Conclusion: 研究提取的六套GPD集（在不同尺度和微扰阶次下可用）为未来理论和唯象研究提供了宝贵资源，为探索质子内部结构的研究人员提供了灵活性。分析揭示了PDF选择对GPD提取的重要性，特别是在低动量转移区域。

Abstract: This paper investigates the crucial role of parton distribution functions (PDFs) in high-energy physics, particularly their impact on the extraction of generalized parton distributions (GPDs) at zero skewness. To this aim, we perform six global analyses of GPDs using different modern PDF sets (\texttt{NNPDF40}, \texttt{CT18}, and \texttt{MSHT20}) at three specific factorization scales ($ μ= 2 $, $ 1.3 $, and $ 1 $ GeV) and different perturbative orders. A wide range of elastic electron scattering data is included in the analysis to constrain GPDs in a broad interval in the momentum transfer squared $ t $. The analyses reveal that the best overall description of experimental data is achieved using \texttt{NNPDF40} PDFs at the next-to-leading order (NLO), with moderate sensitivity to the choice of PDF input, especially in the region of low $ t $. The dependence on the perturbative order is relatively mild, indicating stability in the extraction procedure. We also show that different GPD sets become more consistent at larger $ |t| $ values, with down-quark GPDs experiencing greater suppression than up-quark GPDs. The six extracted GPD sets, available at different scales and perturbative orders, provide valuable resources for future theoretical and phenomenological studies, offering flexibility for researchers in exploring the proton's internal structure.

### [61] [Global $Λ$ hyperon polarization in low-energy heavy ion collisions -- a scenario without vorticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19581)
*Feng Liu,Zhoudunming Tu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究首次建立了重离子碰撞中Λ超子整体极化（global polarization）与未极化强子碰撞中横向极化（transverse polarization）之间的定量联系，提出通过定向流（directed flow）驱动的Λ产生平面与反应平面（reaction plane）的对齐机制，可以将横向极化转化为可测量的整体极化信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重离子碰撞中Λ超子的整体极化现象已被确认为源于旋转夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）产生的大涡度（vorticity）。然而，未极化强子碰撞中观测到的横向Λ极化现象已存在近五十年，其物理机制仍是未解之谜。尽管这两种现象具有显著相似性，但通常被认为源于不同的物理起源。

Method: 研究提出通过定向流（directed flow）驱动的Λ产生平面与反应平面（reaction plane）的对齐机制，将横向极化转化为整体极化信号。采用Au+Au碰撞在$\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}} = 3$ GeV条件下的现实蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）进行验证。

Result: 模拟结果表明，该机制能够产生显著的整体极化信号，约占STAR合作组报告幅度的$23\%\pm6\%$。这首次为这两种现象建立了定量联系。

Conclusion: 该研究首次建立了重离子碰撞中Λ整体极化与未极化碰撞系统中长期观测的横向极化之间的直接定量联系。这一发现对低能重离子碰撞中Λ整体极化测量的解释具有重要意义。

Abstract: Since its discovery, global polarization of the $Λ$ hyperon in heavy-ion collisions has been firmly established and is widely attributed to the large vorticity generated in the rotating quark-gluon plasma. In contrast, nearly fifty years after the first observation of unexpectedly large transverse $Λ$ polarization in unpolarized hadron collisions, its underlying mechanism remains an open and long-standing puzzle, despite being observed across a broad range of collision systems. Although these two phenomena exhibit notable similarities, they are generally regarded as arising from distinct physical origins. In this work, we propose a direct connection between $Λ$ global polarization in heavy-ion collisions and the long-standing transverse polarization observed in unpolarized collision systems. We demonstrate that the alignment between the $Λ$ production plane and the reaction plane, driven by directed flow, can transfer transverse polarization into the measured global polarization signal. Realistic Monte Carlo simulations of Au+Au collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}} = 3$ GeV indicate that this mechanism can generate a sizable global polarization, accounting for approximately $23\%\pm6\%$ of the magnitude reported by the STAR Collaboration. Our results establish, for the first time, a quantitative link between these two well-known phenomena and have important implications for the interpretation of $Λ$ global polarization measurements in low-energy heavy-ion collisions.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用QCD求和规则（QCD sum rule）方法，使用三种不同类型的插值流（interpolating currents）来计算所考虑态的质量和流耦合常数（current coupling constants）。研究的态具有自旋宇称量子数$J^{P}=\frac{1}{2}^{-}$和夸克成分$QQQ'Q\bar{Q'}$、$QQQ'Q'\bar{Q}$及$Q'Q'QQ\bar{Q}$。

Abstract: Recent progress in experimental facilities, together with larger data samples and more refined analysis strategies has enabled the observation of many exotic hadronic states, adding new members to the hadron spectrum. Each newly reported signal encourages further experimental searches and simultaneously motivates theoretical studies aimed at uncovering additional nonconventional states. Motivated by this perspective and by the increasing interest in systems containing multiple heavy quarks, we present a spectroscopic study of fully heavy pentaquark candidates with spin-parity quantum numbers $J^{P}=\frac{1}{2}^{-}$ and quark contents $QQQ'Q\bar{Q'}$, $QQQ'Q'\bar{Q}$, and $Q'Q'QQ\bar{Q}$, where $Q(Q')$ represents either $c(b)$ or $b(c)$ quarks. We employ the QCD sum rule approach with three different types of interpolating currents to obtain the corresponding masses and current coupling constants of the considered states. The following masses for the states containing three $c$ and two $b$ quarks are predicted: $m_{(3c2b)}=14479.30\pm75.06~\mathrm{MeV}$ using the current $J_1$, $\tilde{m}_{(3c2b)}=14276.80\pm76.29~\mathrm{MeV}$ using $J_2$, and $\bar{m}_{(3c2b)}=14276.80\pm76.29~\mathrm{MeV}$ using $J_3$. The corresponding predictions for the states containing three $b$ and two $c$ quarks are as $m_{(3b2c)}=17458.90\pm130.11~\mathrm{MeV}$ with $J_1$, $\tilde{m}_{(3b2c)}=17202.70\pm132.37~\mathrm{MeV}$ with $J_2$, and $\bar{m}_{(3b2c)}=17250.80\pm131.98~\mathrm{MeV}$ with $J_3$, respectively. In addition, we provide the corresponding current coupling constants, which can serve as useful inputs for analyses of decay properties and interaction mechanisms of these fully heavy pentaquark candidates.

Abstract: Upcoming and present reactor neutrino experiments represent an appealing tool to probe fundamental properties in the neutrino sector. *Carsten van de Bruck,C. P. Burgess,Adam Smith*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真空能动态弛豫机制为解决宇宙学常数问题提供了具体途径，但弛豫过程不仅影响真空能，还会对低能物理的其他方面产生后果。研究旨在探索这种弛豫机制如何影响低能物理，特别是宇宙学中的轻标量场行为。

Method: 采用最近提出的'yoga'弛豫模型作为明确框架，分析弛豫如何相对于弛豫子（relaxon）质量设定的特征时间尺度，差异性地抑制'慢'物理过程。研究特别重新审视了QCD轴子在此背景下的行为。

Result: 弛豫机制抑制轴子的真空势能，重塑其在宇宙学时间尺度上的行为，但不影响快速高能过程。这导致轴子的质量-耦合关系偏离标准QCD带，进入已被观测约束排除的参数区域。对于QCD动机参数，真空轴子势能的抑制使QCD物质诱导势能即使在宇宙学和日常物质密度下也能占主导，可能使轴子偏离CP守恒最小值。

Conclusion: 在真空能弛豫框架内，传统的QCD轴子不太可能以其标准形式保持可行性。弛豫机制对轴子行为的显著改变使其参数进入已被观测排除的区域。

Abstract: Mechanisms that dynamically relax the vacuum energy offer a concrete way to approach the cosmological constant problem, but because relaxation is not confined to the vacuum energy alone it can have consequences for the rest of low-energy physics. We explore this issue using the recently proposed 'yoga' relaxation models as an explicit framework and show how relaxation differentially suppresses 'slow' physics relative to a characteristic timescale set by the mass of the relaxon. It therefore need not alter e.g. Higgs & collider physics but can dramatically change how light scalar fields participate in cosmology. We revisit the QCD axion in this setting and show that the suppression of the axion's vacuum potential reshapes its behaviour on cosmological timescales while leaving fast, high-energy processes unaffected. The result is to alter the axion mass-coupling relation away from the standard QCD band, driving it into a regime already ruled out by observational constraints. In particular, suppression of the vacuum axion potential allows the QCD matter-induced potential to dominate even for matter densities relevant to cosmology and everyday matter, potentially driving the axion away from the CP-conserving minimum for QCD-motivated parameters. We conclude that conventional QCD axions are unlikely to remain viable in their standard form within vacuum-energy relaxation frameworks.

</details>

### [65] [Deciphering Molecular Charge Anisotropy: the Case of Antibody Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19366)
*Fabrizio Camerin,Susana Marin-Aguilar,Anna Stradner,Peter Schurtenberger,Emanuela Zaccarelli*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种多尺度框架，通过胶体启发的粗粒化建模与神经网络辅助优化，将分子水平静电学与集体性质直接关联，用于解码和控制蛋白质溶液中异质电荷分布的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静电相互作用（electrostatic interactions）对带电（生物）物质的结构、稳定性和动力学具有根本性影响，但异质性和各向异性电荷分布对蛋白质溶液行为的影响仍不清楚。研究旨在解码和控制复杂生物分子中电荷驱动的相互作用。

Method: 引入了一种通用的多尺度框架（multiscale framework），结合胶体启发的粗粒化建模（colloid-inspired coarse-grained modeling）与神经网络辅助优化（neural network-assisted optimization）。采用单克隆抗体（monoclonal antibodies）作为模型系统，通过逆向设计方法（inverse design approach）识别能够可靠再现实验结构因子的电荷模式。

Result: 该逆向设计方法能够在广泛的蛋白质浓度范围内可靠地再现实验结构因子、渗透压缩性和集体扩散系数。数据分析进一步揭示了局部电荷斑块（localized charge patches）的特定物理特征和空间排列如何显著影响溶液结构。

Conclusion: 这种可转移的策略为解码和控制复杂生物分子及更广泛的异质带电软物质系统（heterogeneously-charged soft matter systems）中的电荷驱动相互作用提供了预测途径，对蛋白质配方和生物材料工程具有直接相关性。

Abstract: Electrostatic interactions fundamentally govern the structure, stability, and dynamics of charged (bio)matter, yet the impact of heterogeneous and anisotropic charge distributions on the behavior of protein solutions remains elusive. Here, we introduce a versatile multiscale framework that directly connects molecular-level electrostatics to collective properties via a colloid-inspired coarse-grained modeling combined with neural network-assisted optimization. Using monoclonal antibodies as model system, our inverse design approach identifies charge patterns capable of reliably reproducing experimental structure factors, osmotic compressibility and collective diffusion coefficients in a wide region of protein concentrations. Close inspection of our data further uncovers how specific physical features and spatial arrangements of localized charge patches significantly influence the solution structure. This transferable strategy provides a predictive pathway to decode and control charge-driven interactions in complex biomolecules and, more generally, in heterogeneously-charged soft matter systems, with immediate relevance to protein formulation and biomaterials engineering.

### [66] [The effect of interactions on elastic cavitation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19603)
*Ali Saeedi,S Chockalingam,Mrityunjay Kothari*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究分析了空穴（cavitation）在软材料中的失效机制，特别关注了空穴与刚性界面及邻近空穴之间的相互作用对空穴压力阈值的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空穴是软材料和生物材料中常见的失效成核机制。经典理论给出了孤立空穴的空穴压力为2.5μ，但实际应用中空穴阈值受到与附近界面和其他空穴相互作用的影响。这些相互作用效应在多材料系统、增材制造结构以及泡沫、多孔固体等有限孔隙材料中尤为重要。

Method: 研究通过理论分析表征了两种相互作用对空穴压力的影响：一是空穴与附近刚性界面的相互作用，二是空穴与邻近相同空穴之间的相互作用。分析基于不可压缩neo-Hookean固体模型，考虑了初始空穴-界面距离和初始空穴间距离的变化。

Result: 对于刚性界面附近的空穴，空穴压力随初始空穴-界面距离减小而增加，从远处空穴的体值2.5μ开始，当空穴接近界面边界时趋近于界面处缺陷的空穴压力值（约3.5μ）。对于相互作用的空穴，空穴压力对初始空穴间距离d呈现非单调依赖性：远处空穴趋近于体值2.5μ，在d≈5.7R（R为初始空穴半径）时达到最大值约2.8μ。

Conclusion: 空穴与界面及邻近空穴的相互作用显著影响空穴压力阈值。刚性界面使空穴压力增加，而空穴间相互作用导致非单调变化，在特定距离处达到最大阈值。这些发现对于理解多材料系统和有限孔隙材料中的失效机制具有重要意义。

Abstract: Cavitation refers to the sudden, unstable expansion of a defect or cavity within a material in response to applied loads, when the loads reach a critical threshold. It is widely recognized as a common failure nucleation mechanism in soft and biological materials. For an isolated cavity in the bulk of an incompressible neo-Hookean solid loaded by remote hydrostatic tension, the classical cavitation pressure is well established as $2.5 μ$, where $μ$ is the shear modulus. However, in realistic settings the cavitation threshold is influenced by interaction of the cavity with nearby interfaces and other cavities. Interface interaction effects are particularly relevant in multi-material systems and additively manufactured structures, where defects frequently occur near material boundaries. Meanwhile, cavity-cavity interactions become important in materials exhibiting finite porosity, such as foams, porous solids, and phase-separating polymers.
  Here, we characterize the effect of interactions on cavitation pressure for (i) a nearby rigid interface and (ii) a neighboring identical cavity. For cavities near a rigid interface, our analysis shows that the cavitation pressure increases as the initial cavity-interface distance decreases, starting from the bulk value for a distant cavity and approaching the cavitation pressure value for a defect situated at an interface ($\approx3.5μ$) as the cavity approaches the interface boundary. In contrast, interacting cavities exhibit a non-monotonic dependence of the cavitation pressure on the initial inter-cavity distance $d$: the threshold approaches the bulk value of $2.5μ$ for distant cavities and reaches a maximum of $\sim2.8μ$ at $d\sim5.7R$, where $R$ is the initial cavity radius.

</details>


### [67] [Discontinuous change of viscosity in a sheared granular gas with velocity-dependent restitution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19605)
*Makoto R. Kikuchi,Yuria Kobayashi,Satoshi Takada*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 研究具有速度依赖恢复系数（velocity-dependent restitution coefficient）的剪切颗粒气体流变学，发现剪切粘度随剪切速率呈现S形依赖关系，并在低剪切和高剪切区域间出现不连续变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究剪切颗粒气体的流变特性，特别关注恢复系数随碰撞速度变化时对系统粘度的非线性影响。

Method: 采用动力学理论（kinetic theory）推导剪切粘度，分析恢复系数在两种值之间切换时系统的流变行为。

Result: 剪切粘度随剪切速率呈现S形依赖关系（S-shaped dependence），在低剪切和高剪切区域间出现不连续变化，两个区域均表现出Bagnold型标度（Bagnold-type scaling）。

Conclusion: 该现象与Wyart-Cates致密悬浮液场景相似，但当前转变完全源于动力学效应，无需摩擦接触或阻塞（jamming）机制。

Abstract: We investigate the rheology of a sheared granular gas composed of hard spheres with a velocity-dependent restitution coefficient. Using kinetic theory, we derive the shear viscosity and show that it exhibits an S-shaped dependence on the shear rate when the restitution coefficient switches between two values depending on the collision velocity. As a result, a discontinuous change of viscosity emerges between low- and high-shear regimes, both characterized by Bagnold-type scaling. While the phenomenology resembles the Wyart-Cates scenario for dense suspensions, the present transition arises purely from kinetic effects without frictional contacts or jamming.

</details>


### [68] [Effects of Divalent Cations on Diffusion Dynamics of Biological Water Confined between Lipid Membranes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19719)
*Minho Lee,Jinwon Park,Ji-Hyun Kim,Minhaeng Cho,Jaeyoung Sung*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过分子动力学模拟和广义输运方程，揭示了钙离子（Ca²⁺）和镁离子（Mg²⁺）对脂质膜间纳米受限生物水（biological water）传输动力学的不同影响：Ca²⁺浓度增加使水扩散系数单调上升，而Mg²⁺则呈现非单调依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物水（biological water）是含有单价和双价离子的离子溶液，但双价离子对生物水动力学的影响尚不明确。本研究旨在探究钙离子（Ca²⁺）和镁离子（Mg²⁺）浓度如何影响脂质膜间纳米受限水分子的传输动力学。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）和生物水的广义输运方程（generalized transport equation for biological water），研究钙离子和镁离子浓度对脂质膜间纳米受限水分子传输动力学的影响。

Result: 研究发现生物水的扩散系数随Ca²⁺浓度单调增加，但对Mg²⁺浓度呈现基本相反的非单调依赖关系。水分子位移分布偏离高斯分布的程度也表现出对Mg²⁺和Ca²⁺浓度的不同依赖性。这些差异源于双价离子的不同水合半径（hydration radii）及其对生物水界面结构和动力学的不同影响。

Conclusion: 水分子横向位移分布向高斯分布的弛豫由扩散系数涨落的时间相关函数决定，其弛豫时间随盐浓度增加而增加。横向扩散系数涨落的主要来源是水分子在纵向的热运动，沿该方向水分子周围的微观环境（包括脂质膜官能团和离子浓度）发生剧烈变化。

Abstract: Biological water is an ionic solution containing both monovalent and divalent ions. However, the effects of divalent ions on the dynamics of biological water remain largely unknown. Here, we investigate how the transport dynamics of water molecules nanoconfined between lipid membranes depends on the concentration of calcium (Ca2+) and magnesium (Mg2+) ions by using molecular dynamics simulations and the generalized transport equation for biological water. We find that the diffusion coefficient of biological water monotonically increases with Ca2+ ion concentration but exhibits a largely opposite, non-monotonic dependence on Mg2+ concentration. The deviation of the water molecules' displacement distribution from the Gaussian also shows distinct dependence on the concentrations of Mg2+ and Ca2+. These contrasting behaviors originate from the different hydration radii of these divalent ions and their distinct effects on the interfacial structure and dynamics of biological water. The relaxation of the lateral displacement distribution of water molecules toward a Gaussian is determined by the time-correlation function of diffusion coefficient fluctuations, whose relaxation time increases with salt concentrations. The primary source of the lateral diffusion coefficient fluctuation is thermal motion of water molecules in the longitudinal direction, along which microscopic environments surrounding a water molecule, including the functional groups of lipid membrane and ion concentrations, drastically change.

</details>


### [69] [Modelling the passive and active response of skeletal muscles within the adapted Voigt representation framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19723)
*Sara Galasso,Giulio G. Giusteri*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种骨骼肌被动与主动响应的本构模型，采用非线性柯西弹性框架下的Voigt表示，通过双材料模型分离纤维与细胞外基质贡献，成功预测了不同纤维方向的非线性应力响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在开发一种能够描述骨骼肌被动和主动响应的本构模型，以改进传统方法，增强材料函数的力学可解释性，并深入理解收缩纤维与细胞外基质的不同作用。

Method: 模型基于非线性柯西弹性（nonlinear Cauchy elasticity）框架，采用Voigt表示法描述应变和应力张量，提出双材料模型（two-material model）进行应力贡献的加法分解，其中仅一个分量依赖于激活参数。

Result: 被动行为本构模型成功预测了不同纤维方向相对取向下的非线性应力响应，揭示了细胞外基质的主导作用；激活模型通过沿纤维主动应变的弹塑性演化，很好地捕捉了等长应力响应。

Conclusion: 该模型框架能够以直接方式从实验数据中识别非平凡的应力-应变关系，增强了对组织响应材料函数的力学解释，为理解收缩纤维与细胞外基质的独特作用提供了新见解。

Abstract: We present a constitutive model for the passive and active response of skeletal muscles. At variance with more classical approaches, the model is developed exploiting adapted Voigt representations of strain and stress tensors within the context of nonlinear Cauchy elasticity. This framework allows us to identify non-trivial stress-strain relations in a rather direct way from experimental data, enhancing the mechanical interpretability of the material functions that describe the tissue response and obtaining additional insight on the distinct role of the contractile fibres and of the surrounding extracellular matrix. We propose a two-material model, with an additive splitting of the stress contributions, in which only one component depends on an activation parameter. The constitutive model for the passive behaviour satisfactorily predicts the nonlinear stress response to elongation at different relative orientations with respect to the fibre direction and highlights the dominant role of the extracellular matrix. The activation model, essentially determined by the mechanics of the contractile fibres, captures well the isometric stress response through the prescription of an elasto-plastic evolution of the along-fibre active strain.

</details>


### [70] [Amorphous Silicates -- Time-Current Superposition and the Dynamics of Plastic Flow in the Glassy State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19816)
*Matthieu Bourguignon,Gustavo A. Rosales-Sosa,Yoshinari Kato,Sergio Sao-Joao,Morgan Rusinowicz,Guillaume Kermouche,Etienne Barthel*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 电子辐照（electron irradiation）能够实现对硅酸盐玻璃（silicate glasses）塑性流动动力学的定量控制，即使在远低于玻璃化转变温度（glass transition temperature）的条件下。通过应力松弛实验（stress-relaxation experiments），研究者发现了时间-电流等效性（time-current equivalence），从而能够重构本征塑性流动曲线并定量评估网络连通性和温度的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论框架在描述玻璃态（glassy state）塑性流动动力学方面存在不足，特别是在远低于玻璃化转变温度条件下的行为。研究者旨在通过电子辐照技术实现对塑性流动的定量控制，以深入理解网络连通性（network connectivity）和温度对玻璃塑性行为的影响。

Method: 采用电子辐照技术结合应力松弛实验（stress-relaxation experiments），在环境温度到接近玻璃化转变温度（near-glass-transition temperatures）的范围内进行研究。通过时间-电流等效性（time-current equivalence）方法，实现了在五个数量级应变率（strain rate）范围内对稳态塑性流动（steady-state plastic flow）的直接观测。

Result: 实验发现了时间-电流等效性（time-current equivalence），使得能够重构本征塑性流动曲线（intrinsic plastic-flow curve）。温度依赖性的观测结果与现有理论框架存在显著差异，揭示了当前模型在描述玻璃态塑性流动动力学方面的局限性。

Conclusion: 电子辐照技术为定量控制硅酸盐玻璃（silicate glasses）的塑性流动动力学提供了有效手段。观测到的温度依赖性（temperature dependence）与现有理论框架的差异，突显了需要建立更全面的玻璃态塑性流动动力学模型（comprehensive model of plastic flow dynamics in the glassy state）。

Abstract: Electron irradiation enables quantitative control over the plastic flow dynamics of silicate glasses, even far below the glass transition temperature. Through stress-relaxation experiments spanning ambient to near-glass-transition temperatures, we uncover a time-current equivalence that grants direct access to steady-state plastic flow over five decades in strain rate. This equivalence allows reconstruction of the intrinsic plastic-flow curve and quantitative assessment of the roles of network connectivity and temperature. Notably, the observed temperature dependence reveals a striking discrepancy with existing theoretical frameworks, highlighting the need for a comprehensive model of plastic flow dynamics in the glassy state.

</details>


### [71] [Symmetric mixtures in slit-like pores with selective walls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20023)
*A. Patrykiejew*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 对称混合物在高负几何和能量非加性条件下体相不分离，但在选择性狭缝孔中会发生相分离，孔壁选择性影响填充过程，存在阈值决定填充方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究对称混合物（symmetric mixtures）在受限环境中的相行为，特别是当混合物具有高负几何和能量非加性（high negative geometric and energetic non-additivity）时，体相中不发生相分离，但在选择性孔壁（selective walls）的狭缝孔（slit pores）中会出现相分离现象。

Method: 通过分析混合物组分与孔壁之间的相互作用能差异（difference of the interaction energies），研究其对孔填充（pore filling）过程的影响，重点关注阈值（threshold value）的存在及其对相变路径的决定作用。

Result: 当混合物组分与孔壁的相互作用能差异低于阈值时，发生从稀相（dilute phase）到混合液体（mixed liquid）的凝聚（condensation）；当差异超过阈值时，孔填充分两步进行：首先从稀相凝聚成分离液体（demixed liquid），然后形成混合液体。

Conclusion: 对称混合物的非加性（non-additivity）以及组分与孔壁相互作用能的差异共同决定了受限环境中的相行为，孔壁选择性能够诱导体相中不存在的相分离现象，且填充机制受相互作用能差异阈值的调控。

Abstract: Symmetric mixtures characterized by high negative geometric and energetic non-additivity do not exhibit phase separation in the bulk. However, the phase separation occurs when such mixtures are confined in slit pores with selective walls. It is demonstrated that the wall selectivity affects the pore filling. When the difference of the interaction energies between the mixture components and pore walls is lower than a certain threshold value, condensation occurs between a dilute phase and the mixed liquid. When this difference exceeds the threshold value, the pore filling may occur in two steps. The first is the condensation of a dilute phase into the demixed liquid, and the second step leads to the formation of the mixed liquid. We have elucidated the changes in the phase behavior caused by non-additivity of symmetric mixtures, and by the difference in the interaction energies of the components with pore walls.

</details>


### [72] [II. Temperature trends in the properties of simple monohydric alcohols. Molecular dynamics simulations of united atom UAMI-EW model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20026)
*M. Aguilar,E. Núñez-Rojas,O. Pizio*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过等压-等温分子动力学模拟，探究了甲醇、乙醇和1-丙醇及其混合物的多种性质对温度的依赖性，评估了最新提出的联合原子非极化力场的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索一元醇（monohydric alcohols）的多种性质对温度的依赖性，并评估最近提出的联合原子非极化力场（united atom, non-polarizable force field）在预测这些性质方面的准确性。

Method: 采用等压-等温分子动力学计算机模拟（isobaric-isothermal molecular dynamics computer simulations），研究对象包括甲醇、乙醇和1-丙醇及其混合物，应用了最近提出的联合原子非极化力场。

Result: 通过比较模拟预测与实验数据（密度、介电常数、表面张力、自扩散系数），讨论了力场的准确性；通过研究甲醇-丙醇混合物的组成依赖性，获得了模型适用性的补充见解，阐明了该系统中物种混合的特殊性。

Conclusion: 研究最后对建模前景进行了评论，表明该力场能够有效预测一元醇及其混合物的多种性质，为相关系统的分子模拟提供了可靠工具。

Abstract: We explore the dependence of a wide set of properties of monohydric alcohols on temperature by using the isobaric-isothermal molecular dynamics computer simulations. Namely, methanol (MeOH), ethanol (EtOH) and 1-propanol (PrOH) alcohols are studied. The recently proposed united atom, non-polarizable force field for each of alcohols [V. García-Melgarejo et al., J. Mol. Liq., 2021, 323, 114576] is applied for this purpose. Accuracy of the force field is discussed comparing predictions from simulations and experimental data for density, dielectric constant, surface tension, and self-diffusion coefficient. Supplementary insights concerning applicability of the model are obtained by exploration of the composition dependence of various properties for MeOH-PrOH mixtures. Peculiarities of mixing of species in this system are elucidated in terms of density, excess mixing volume and excess mixing enthalpy. Static dielectric constant of the mixture and the corresponding excess are obtained. Perspectives of modelling are commented finally.

Accuracy of the force field is evaluated by comparing the simulation results and available experimental data from the literature. Specifically, the density of alcohols upon increasing pressure, the isothermal compressibility, the static dielectric constant and self-diffusion coefficient are investigated starting from 1 bar up to 3 kbar. ### [75] [How does ethane wet different substrates?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20043)
*Ł. Baran,D. Tarasewicz,W. Rżysko*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过计算机模拟（computer simulations）探究乙烷（ethane）在均质与非均质基底上的吸附机制（adsorption mechanisms）。研究发现，均质表面的相变（phase transitions）可通过调节表面势能（surface potential）强度实现从不完全润湿（incomplete wetting）到完全润湿（complete wetting）的转变，且分层转变温度（layering transition temperatures）与实验测量结果高度一致。相比之下，非均质基底虽均呈现预润湿转变（prewetting transition），但其吸附机制受条纹宽度（stripe width）显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过计算机模拟深入理解乙烷在不同类型基底上的吸附机制，特别是比较均质与条纹状非均质基底对吸附行为的影响差异。

Method: 采用计算机模拟方法，通过调节表面势能强度来研究均质基底上的吸附相变，同时考察不同条纹宽度的非均质基底对乙烷吸附过程的影响。

Result: 对于均质基底，通过调节表面势能可实现从完全润湿到不完全润湿的完整相变范围，且分层转变温度与乙烷在石墨上的实验测量结果高度吻合。对于非均质基底，所有系统均表现出预润湿转变，但吸附机制强烈依赖于条纹宽度。

Conclusion: 基底的非均质性对乙烷吸附机制具有显著影响，均质基底可通过表面势能调控实现完整的润湿相变，而非均质基底的吸附行为则受其微观结构特征（如条纹宽度）的强烈制约。

Abstract: Computer simulations are employed to investigate the adsorption mechanisms of ethane on both homogeneous and inhomogeneous substrates. For homogeneous surfaces, the full range of surface phase transitions - from incomplete to complete wetting - can be accessed by tuning the strength of the surface potential. The resulting layering transition temperatures show excellent agreement with experimental measurements of ethane on graphite. By contrast, although all inhomogeneous substrates exhibit a prewetting transition, the adsorption mechanisms are strongly influenced by the stripe width.

</details>


### [76] [The application of Kirkwood-Buff theory to study hydration properties of $α$-amino acids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20051)
*Z. Štefanič,B. Hribar-Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过测量七种α-氨基酸在水溶液中的密度，计算表观摩尔体积并通过线性外推获得标准摩尔体积，用于表征氨基酸水合特性。结合Ornstein-Zernike积分方程和粗粒化Lennard-Jones珠模型，成功重现了实验测得的标准摩尔体积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蛋白质构象稳定性和功能依赖于非共价相互作用，这些作用受周围环境强烈影响。氨基酸常被用作模型系统来探索蛋白质性质，本研究旨在通过分析氨基酸水合特性来理解这些相互作用。

Method: 在278.15 K至308.15 K温度范围内测定七种α-氨基酸水溶液的密度，计算表观摩尔体积并通过线性外推获得标准摩尔体积。采用Ornstein-Zernike积分方程与超网链闭合（hypernetted-chain closure）以及粗粒化Lennard-Jones珠模型（coarse-grained Lennard-Jones bead model）计算对相关函数和Kirkwood-Buff积分。

Result: 标准摩尔体积随温度升高而增加，表明氨基酸周围水的电致伸缩（electrostriction）减弱，这与高温下较低的水合数一致。相对于甘氨酸确定了侧链对标准摩尔体积的贡献，理论模型很好地重现了实验测得的标准摩尔体积。

Conclusion: 通过实验测量和理论计算相结合的方法，成功表征了氨基酸的水合特性，为理解蛋白质非共价相互作用提供了重要参考。模型与实验数据的高度一致性验证了理论方法的可靠性。

Abstract: Protein conformational stability and function depend on non-covalent interactions that are strongly influenced by the surrounding environment. To explore protein properties, amino acids are often utilized as model systems. In this study, we determined the densities of seven $α$-amino acids in aqueous solutions between 278.15 K and 308.15 K and calculated the apparent molar volumes. Linear extrapolation yielded standard molar volumes, which were analyzed to characterize amino-acid hydration. The contributions of side chains to the standard molar volume were determined relative to glycine. The standard molar volume increased with temperature, indicating reduced electrostriction of water around the amino acids, consistent with lower hydration numbers at higher temperatures. We employed the Ornstein-Zernike integral equation with hypernetted-chain closure and a coarse-grained Lennard-Jones bead model to calculate pair correlation functions and Kirkwood-Buff integrals, from which standard molar volumes were obtained. The model reproduced the experimental standard molar volumes very well.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究重点介绍了三维参考相互作用位点模型与Kovalenko-Hirata闭合（3D-RISM-KH）这一强大的分子溶剂化理论，该方法已成功应用于纳米化学和生物分子模拟领域，用于研究半纤维素水凝胶、半纤维素组成对初生细胞壁纳米尺度作用力的影响，以及木质素-木质素和木质素-半纤维素相互作用。

Abstract: This review examines multiscale modelling approaches for cellulose nanocrystals (CNCs) and lignocellulosic plant cell walls, with a focus on hemicellulose and lignin interactions in aqueous environments. The three-dimensional reference interaction site model with the Kovalenko-Hirata closure (3D-RISM-KH) is highlighted as a powerful molecular solvation theory applied in nanochemistry and biomolecular simulations. The method has been successfully employed to investigate hemicellulose hydrogels, the influence of hemicellulose composition on nanoscale forces in primary cell walls, and lignin-lignin and lignin-hemicellulose interactions. Findings indicate that these interactions are predominantly hydrophobic and entropy-driven, arising from water exclusion effects. Insights gained through this modeling framework deepen the understanding of molecular-scale forces in plant cell walls and inform strategies for biomass valorization, including genetic engineering and pretreatment technologies aimed at enhancing cellulose extraction and utilization.

### [78] [Mechanical response of a simple DNA nanostar hydrogel: symptoms of disorder and glassy emergence of solidity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20119)
*Hajar Ajiyel,Anthony J. Genot,Soo Hyeon Kim,Nicolas Schabanel,Hervé Guillou,Catherine Barentin,Mathieu Leocmach*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过系统方法分析DNA纳米星水凝胶（DNA nanostar hydrogel）的力学响应，揭示了无序性（disorder）在DNA材料中的重要作用，并发现了偏离麦克斯韦行为（Maxwell behaviour）和玻璃化转变（glass transition）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DNA自组装（DNA self-assembly）技术已能获得高度有序结构，但DNA水凝胶（DNA hydrogel）依赖无序组装达到宏观体积。为理解DNA块体材料（DNA bulk materials）的宏观性质如何从无序中产生，需要系统研究无序性对材料性能的影响。

Method: 采用系统方法研究简单DNA纳米星水凝胶的力学响应，结合块体流变学（bulk rheology）、动态光散射微流变学（dynamic light scattering microrheology）、力学建模（mechanical modeling）、热力学计算（thermodynamic calculation）以及DNA序列改变（DNA sequence alteration）。

Result: 低温下观察到系统偏离麦克斯韦行为，这是无序材料的典型特征；在远高于DNA网络渗流温度（percolation temperature）时，表征出令人惊讶的固体行为，归因于玻璃化转变。结果强调了无序性在DNA材料中的重要性。

Conclusion: 无序性对DNA材料性能具有关键影响，本文展示的系统方法可广泛应用于更复杂的DNA材料研究，为理解DNA块体材料的宏观性质提供了新视角。

Abstract: DNA self-assembly is a well-understood nanotechnology to obtain extremely ordered structures from the nanometer to up to the hundred of microns scale. By contrast, DNA hydrogels rely on the disordered assembly of DNA building blocks to reach macroscopic volumes. However, in order to hold the promise of DNA bulk materials, the sequence designer needs a systematic understanding of how macroscopic properties emerge from disorder. Here, we show a method to study systematically the mechanical response of a simple DNA nanostar hydrogel. This method mobilises bulk rheology, dynamic light scattering microrheology, mechanical modeling, as well as thermodynamic calculation and DNA sequence alteration. At low temperatures, we demonstrate a systematic deviation from Maxwell behaviour that is symptomatic of disordered materials. At temperatures much higher than the percolation of the DNA network, we characterise a surprising solid behaviour that we attribute to a glass transition. Our results show the importance of disorder in DNA materials. Furthermore, the method we showcase in this article can be widely applied to more complex DNA materials.

### [79] [Nonlinear iontronic signal processing with neuromorphic Spike Rate-Dependent Plasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20126)
*T. M. Kamsma,Y. Gu,D. Shi,C. Spitoni,M. Dijkstra,R. van Roij,Y. Xie*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在超越孤立组件，探索异质离子电子动力学如何解锁非线性时间序列处理能力，这对未来离子电子神经形态计算至关重要。研究动机源于将理论预测与实验实现相结合，开发能够处理复杂生物信号的物理系统。

Method: 方法基于集成离子电子忆阻器电路设计，该电路包含两个平行的忆阻膜，分别具有短和长的锥形忆阻通道且取向相反，从而产生异质内部时间尺度和不同的增强响应。实验测量受到理论模型的启发并与之一致。

Result: 电路展现出非线性频率响应：低频输入降低整体电导，而高频输入增加电导，从而模拟生物SRDP。该器件功能通过分离不同昆虫的编码声音信号（这些信号无法线性分离）得到验证，成功实现了自然听觉数据的分类。

Abstract: We present an integrated iontronic memristor circuit that reproduces biologically inspired Spike Rate-Dependent Plasticity (SRDP) and functions as a physical nonlinear frequency kernel, which we demonstrate can be used to classify natural auditory data. The fluidic circuit integrates two parallel memristive membranes containing short and long conical memristive channels with opposite orientations, giving rise to heterogeneous internal timescales and different potentiation responses. As a result, the circuit exhibits a nonlinear frequency response in which low-frequency inputs decrease the overall conductance, whereas higher-frequency inputs increase it, thereby emulating biological SRDP. Our experimental measurements are inspired by and consistent with predictions of a theoretical model. We demonstrate the functionality of the device by separating encoded sound signals from different insects that cannot be linearly separated. By unifying theoretical predictions with experimental realisation of coupled iontronic memristors, this work moves beyond isolated components and demonstrates how heterogeneous iontronic dynamics can unlock nonlinear time-series processing capabilities, essential for future iontronic neuromorphic computing.

### [80] [Binary colloidal mixtures in near-critical binary solvents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20137)
*Nima Farahmand Bafi,Robert Evans,Anna Maciolek*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究将单胶体在近临界溶剂中的相行为分析扩展至双胶体体系，通过三维晶格模型揭示了两种不同胶体相对体积分数变化时相图拓扑结构的显著改变，为温度可逆调控的胶体"合金"自组装过程提供了理论见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究受到近期实验的启发，旨在探究两种胶体类型（C1和C2）在接近其分层临界点的二元溶剂中的混合体系。单胶体在近临界溶剂中的相行为已知非常丰富，但双胶体体系的研究相对较少，需要扩展现有理论框架。

Method: 研究扩展了先前用于研究二维单胶体体系的平均场描述（mean-field description）晶格模型（lattice model），将其应用于三维双胶体情况。该模型将系统视为完整的四组分混合物，其中C1和C2被简化为具有相同半径但对溶剂中B组分具有不同亲和力的硬球（hard spheres）。

Result: 研究显示，C1与溶剂、C2与溶剂的耦合作用，以及溶剂-溶剂相互作用和硬球堆积之间的复杂相互作用，导致当两种不同胶体类型的相对体积分数（relative volume fractions）变化时，胶体相图（colloidal phase diagram）的拓扑结构发生显著改变。两条三相点线（lines of triple points）的行为尤为有趣。

Conclusion: 研究结果为通过近临界溶剂介导、温度可逆调控的胶体"合金"（colloidal 'alloys'）自组装过程（self-assembly process）的控制提供了一定的理论见解。该模型揭示了多组分胶体体系中相行为的复杂性及其潜在调控机制。

Abstract: The phase behavior of a single type of colloid C suspended in near-critical solvents is known to be very rich. Motivated in part by recent experiments we consider a mixture of two colloidal types C1 and C2 in a binary solvent close to its demixing critical point. We extend a mean-field description of a lattice model, previously used to investigate systems with a single type of colloid in two dimensions, to the binary colloid case in three dimensions. The model treats the system as a full four-component mixture. For simplicity we choose C1 and C2 to be hard spheres with the same radius but with different affinities for one species, B, of the AB binary solvent. We show that intricate interplay between couplings of C1 and solvent, C2 and solvent as well as solvent-solvent interactions and hard sphere packing drive significant changes in the topology of the colloidal phase diagram when the relative volume fractions of the two different colloid types change. The behavior of the two lines of triple points is particularly interesting. Our results can provide some insight into the control of the self-assembly process for colloidal 'alloys' mediated by a near-critical solvent and therefore controlled by temperature in a reversible manner

</details>

### [81] [A Concept of Next-Generation Atmospheric Cherenkov Telescope Array (NG-ACTA)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19622)
*Jiancheng Wang,Jirong Mao*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: NG-ACTA（下一代大气切伦科夫望远镜阵列）是一个由88台望远镜组成的混合孔径阵列，最大直径10公里，采用三阶配置（30米LST、12米MST、6米SST），覆盖20 GeV至100 TeV全能量波段，具备超低探测阈值、超高角分辨率、超大有效面积、极强宇宙线背景抑制和快速瞬变响应能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该阵列旨在解决现代天体物理学和粒子物理学中最前沿和变革性的基础科学问题，包括甚高能（VHE）伽马射线天文学、宇宙线起源、多信使天文学、暗物质以及新物理检验。

Method: NG-ACTA采用混合孔径阵列设计，包含三种尺寸的望远镜：30米大口径大型望远镜（LSTs）、12米中口径中型望远镜（MSTs）和6米小口径小型望远镜（SSTs），形成三阶配置，实现从20 GeV到100 TeV连续伽马射线探测。

Result: 与国际在建设施（如CTAO-North、CTAO-South）和中国设施（如LACT）的全面比较表明，NG-ACTA在低能阈值、基线长度、背景抑制和多信使快速响应能力方面处于世界领先地位。

Conclusion: NG-ACTA的科学目标涵盖粒子天体物理学、甚高能伽马射线天文学、宇宙线物理学、多信使天文学和新物理探索五个核心领域，具有从银河系到河外源、从稳态到瞬变天体、从常规天体到暗物质的六个层次化且相互支持的科学目标。

Abstract: The Next-Generation Atmospheric Cherenkov Telescope Array (NG-ACTA) is proposed as a prospective infrastructure for very high energy (VHE) gamma-ray astronomy, consisting of a mixed-aperture array of 88 telescopes with a maximum array diameter of 10 km. The array adopts a three-tier configuration of 30 m large-aperture Large Size Telescopes (LSTs), 12 m medium-aperture Medium Size Telescopes (MSTs), and 6 m small-aperture Small Size Telescopes (SSTs), enabling continuous gamma-ray detection across the full energy band from 20 GeV to 100 TeV. With core advantages of an ultra-low detection threshold ($\leq20$ GeV), ultra-high angular resolution ($\leq0.04^\circ$), ultra-large effective area ($\geq1\times10^5$ m$^2$), extreme cosmic ray background rejection (proton rejection efficiency $\geq99.99\%$), and rapid transient response ($\leq100$ ns trigger latency), NG-ACTA targets the most cutting-edge and transformative fundamental scientific topics in modern astrophysics and particle physics, including VHE gamma-ray astronomy, cosmic ray origin, multi-messenger astronomy, and dark matter as well as new physics tests.
  The array's scientific goals cover five core fields: particle astrophysics, VHE gamma-ray astronomy, cosmic ray physics, multi-messenger astronomy, and new physics exploration, with six hierarchical and mutually supportive scientific objectives from Galactic to extragalactic sources, steady to transient objects, and conventional objects to dark matter. A comprehensive comparison with international under-construction facilities (e.g., CTAO-North, CTAO-South) and Chinese facilities (e.g., LACT) demonstrates that NG-ACTA leads the world in low-energy threshold, baseline length, background suppression, and multi-messenger rapid response capabilities.

</details>


### [82] [Numerically stable equations for the orbital evolution of compact object binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20124)
*Max M. Briel,Jeff J. Andrews*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在ln空间中重写Peters方程的数值方法，用于计算致密双星系统的轨道演化，该方法提高了数值稳定性并减少了60%-70%的函数计算量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Peters和Mathews推导的致密双星系统引力波辐射轨道演化方程在引力波领域广泛应用，但缺乏闭合形式解，且标准数值方法在接近并合点时容易失效。虽然并合时间计算已有改进研究，但轨道演化本身未受到同等关注。

Method: 作者将Peters方程在ln空间中重写，使得常用数值求解器能够收敛。这种变换提供了更稳健的数值方法，用于计算引力波辐射导致的致密双星系统演化。

Result: 该方法显著提高了数值稳健性和计算效率，在测试中将函数计算量减少了60%到70%。ln空间重写使标准数值求解器能够处理接近并合点的演化过程。

Conclusion: 通过ln空间重写Peters方程，本文提供了一种更高效、更稳健的数值方法，用于计算致密双星系统（compact binary）的引力波驱动轨道演化，解决了传统方法在并合点附近失效的问题。

Abstract: The orbital and eccentricity evolution for compact object binaries through gravitational wave emission first derived by Peters and Mathews are used extensively throughout the gravitational wave community for calculating the orbital evolution and merger time of compact binaries. While improved calculations of the binary merger time have been the focus of several investigations since, the orbital evolution has not received the same attention. As the equations lack a closed form solution, a numerical integrator is required, but standard methods typically break when the point of merger is overstepped. We present a rewrite of Peters' equations in $\ln$-space, which allows common numerical solvers to converge. This leads to a more numerically robust and computationally efficient method for evolving compact binaries due to gravitational wave emission, reducing the number of function evaluations by 60\% to 70\% in our tests.

</details>

### [83] [A T-Duality-Protected Speed-of-Light Bounce in String Gas Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19334)
*Ali Nayeri*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了弦气体宇宙学（string gas cosmology）中由伸缩子（dilaton）控制的光速变化（varying-speed-of-light）阶段，发现指数形式的光速变化会产生光速反弹（speed-of-light bounce）现象，包括早期超光速相、交叉点以及接近自对偶（self-dual）区域时的光速坍缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索弦气体宇宙学框架下伸缩子驱动的光速变化阶段如何影响宇宙学因果结构。具体关注这种机制能否扩大因果视界（causal horizon）并抑制曲率，同时将剩余的障碍定位到自对偶匹配点。

Method: 采用指数形式的光速变化假设 $c(φ)=c_0\,e^{-αφ}$，在弦气体宇宙学的哈格多恩时代（Hagedorn era）背景下进行解析研究。通过计算共动视界（comoving horizon）和平坦度参数 $Ω-1\propto c^2/(a^2H^2)$ 来评估因果结构效应。

Result: 研究发现光速变化会产生光速反弹现象：早期超光速相（$c\gg c_0$），在 $t/t_0\approx 0.285$ 处交叉，接近自对偶区域时 $c$ 坍缩至零。对于 $α=1$ 和 $α=2$，共动视界增强因子分别为 $1.54$ 和 $3.44$，而平坦度参数在晚期哈格多恩相中被抑制 $10^{-4}$--$10^{-7}$ 倍。

Conclusion: 伸缩子驱动的光速变化阶段能够在弦气体宇宙学的受控区域内扩大因果视界并抑制曲率，同时将剩余的匹配问题定位到自对偶点 $R=\ell_s$，该点可作为 T-对偶（T-duality）锚点匹配到后期分支 $c=1$。

Abstract: We study a varying-speed-of-light (VSL) phase embedded in string gas cosmology (SGC), with the effective propagation speed controlled by the dilaton during the Hagedorn era. For the exponential ansatz $c(φ)=c_0\,e^{-αφ}$, the analytic Hagedorn background generates a speed-of-light bounce: an early superluminal phase ($c\gg c_0$), crossover at $t/t_0\approx 0.285$ for the branch studied here, and a collapse of $c$ toward zero as the self-dual regime is approached. The self-dual point at $R=\ell_s$ provides a T-duality anchor for matching onto the late-time branch with $c=1$. Evaluating the comoving horizon on this background, we find enhancement factors of $1.54$ and $3.44$ for $α=1$ and $α=2$, respectively, while the flatness parameter $Ω-1\propto c^2/(a^2H^2)$ is found numerically to be suppressed by $10^{-4}$--$10^{-7}$ over the late Hagedorn phase. These results show that a dilaton-driven VSL phase can enlarge the causal horizon and suppress curvature within the controlled regime of SGC, while localizing the remaining obstruction to the self-dual matching point.

</details>


### [84] [Integrable Systems for Generalized Toric Polygons and Higgsed 5d N=1 Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19353)
*Minsung Kho,Kimyeong Lee,Norton Lee,Rak-Kyeong Seong*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究将环面Calabi-Yau 3-折叠、二聚体可积系统与5维量子场论的框架扩展到广义环面多边形（GTPs），通过精炼双有理变换构建可积系统，并论证这些变换通过Hanany-Witten跃迁实现为与GTPs对偶的(p,q) 5-膜网。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环面Calabi-Yau 3-折叠、二聚体可积系统与5维量子场论之间的相互作用已被证明富有成果。本研究旨在将此框架扩展到广义环面多边形（generalized toric polygons, GTPs），探索其可积系统的构建及其在弦论中的实现。

Method: 通过精炼双有理变换（refined birational transformations）作用于已知二聚体可积系统的Casimir不变量、Hamilton量、Poisson结构及谱曲线，构建GTPs的可积系统。论证这些变换通过Hanany-Witten跃迁实现为与GTPs对偶的(p,q) 5-膜网。

Result: 证明所得5维N=1理论可通过Higgs机制从更高秩理论获得，该更高秩理论对应的环面Calabi-Yau的环面图与GTP具有相同形状。建立了GTPs、可积系统与5维场论之间的对应关系。

Conclusion: 成功将环面Calabi-Yau、二聚体可积系统与5维量子场论的框架扩展到广义环面多边形，揭示了精炼双有理变换、Hanany-Witten跃迁与Higgs机制在构建这些对应关系中的核心作用。

Abstract: The interplay between toric Calabi-Yau 3-folds, dimer integrable systems, and 5-dimensional quantum field theories has proved fruitful. We extend this framework to generalized toric polygons (GTPs) and show that their integrable systems arise from refined birational transformations of known dimer integrable systems acting on the Casimirs and Hamiltonians as well as the Poisson structure and spectral curves. We argue that these transformations are realized as Hanany-Witten transitions producing (p,q) 5-brane webs dual to GTPs. We show that the resulting 5d N=1 theory is obtained by Higgsing a higher-rank theory whose associated toric Calabi-Yau has a toric diagram of the same shape as the GTP.

### [85] [Confinement without symmetry breaking in chiral gauge theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19355)
*Haolin Li,Álvaro Pastor-Gutiérrez,Shahram Vatani*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究使用功能重整化群方法分析Bars-Yankielowicz类规范理论，发现存在两种不同相：小色数下的禁闭与对称性破缺共存相，以及大色数极限下仅禁闭而无对称性破缺的新奇相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性费米子规范理论的红外结构尚未得到充分探索。本研究旨在利用功能重整化群方法分析Bars-Yankielowicz类理论，基于最近在规范-费米子系统中的进展，这些进展为禁闭和动力学对称性破缺提供了明确判据。

Method: 采用功能重整化群（functional renormalisation group）方法研究Bars-Yankielowicz类规范理论。该方法建立在近期规范-费米子系统研究的基础上，这些研究为禁闭（confinement）和动力学对称性破缺（dynamical symmetry breaking）提供了清晰的分析框架。

Result: 研究发现存在两种不同的相：在小色数情况下，系统同时表现出禁闭和对称性破缺；而在大色数极限下，系统呈现仅禁闭而无对称性破缺的特征。后者实现了一种新奇区域，为研究奇异谱和现象提供了可能性。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了大色数极限下仅禁闭而无对称性破缺的新奇相，这一发现为研究奇异谱和现象开辟了新的可能性，并可在系统化框架内进行深入探索。

Abstract: The infrared structure of gauge theories with chiral fermions remains largely unexplored. In this work we investigate the Bars-Yankielowicz class using the functional renormalisation group, building on recent developments in gauge-fermion systems that provide clear criteria for confinement and dynamical symmetry breaking. We show that two distinct phases arise: one exhibiting both confinement and symmetry breaking at small numbers of colours, and another characterised by confinement without symmetry breaking in the large-colour limit. The latter realises a novel regime, opening the possibility of exotic spectra and phenomena that can now be studied within a systematic framework.

### [86] [Four Fermi Theory in Four Dimensions is Renormalisable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19357)
*Charlie Cresswell-Hogg,Daniel F. Litim*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了四维量子场论在大量费米子味数极限下的可重整性，使用Gross-Neveu型相互作用作为模板，展示了包含高阶导数相互作用的扩展四费米子理论是良好定义、可重整且具有预测性的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在证明四维量子场论中具有基本自相互作用狄拉克费米子的可重整性，特别是在大量费米子味数（large-$N_{\rm f}$）极限下。通过分析发散结构和Gross-Neveu型相互作用，探索扩展四费米子理论的良好定义性和预测能力。

Method: 从基本发散结构出发，以Gross-Neveu型相互作用为模板，研究包含高阶导数相互作用的扩展四费米子理论。在大量费米子味数极限下，计算耦合常数的精确领头阶beta函数，并分析量子标度维度、普适性和$1/N_{\rm f}$修正。

Result: 证明了扩展四费米子理论（包括高阶导数相互作用）是良好定义、可重整且具有预测性的，仅需少量自由参数。提供了耦合常数在大量费米子味数极限下的精确领头阶beta函数，并讨论了量子标度维度、普适性、$1/N_{\rm f}$修正以及向其他类型四费米子相互作用的扩展。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了四维量子场论在大量费米子味数极限下的可重整性，为有效理论和模型构建提供了理论基础。扩展四费米子理论展现出良好的可重整性和预测能力，仅需少量参数即可描述物理现象。

Abstract: We demonstrate the renormalisability of quantum field theories in four dimensions with elementary self-interacting Dirac fermions and to leading order in the limit of many fermion flavours $N_{\rm f}$. Starting from the underlying divergence structure and using Gross-Neveu-type interactions as a template, we explain why extended four-fermion theories including higher-derivative interactions are well-defined, renormalisable, and predictive with only a few free parameters. We also provide the exact large-$N_{\rm f}$ leading beta functions of couplings and discuss quantum scaling dimensions, universality, $1/N_{\rm f}$ corrections, and extensions to other types of four fermion interactions. Implications for effective theory and model building are indicated.
