### [87] [Towards a Refinement of Krylov Complexity: Scrambling, Classical Operator Growth and Replicas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19359)
*Hugo A. Camargo,Yichao Fu,Keun-Young Kim,Yeong Han Park*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出并测试了对数Krylov复杂度（logK-complexity），这是一种通过副本方法定义的算子增长度量，能够有效探测早期算子混洗（operator scrambling）且避免假阳性。该度量在有限维量子系统和可积量子系统中均表现出良好的区分能力，并能扩展到经典动力系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Krylov复杂度在探测早期算子混洗时可能产生假阳性，特别是在存在不稳定鞍点（unstable saddle）的情况下。需要一种新的算子增长度量来准确区分真正的混洗和鞍点主导的混洗。

Method: 提出对数Krylov复杂度（logK-complexity），通过副本方法（replica approach）定义。在有限维量子系统中测试Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick（LMG）模型和混沌点的混合场Ising模型；在可积量子系统中测试SYK₂模型和量子倒谐振子（quantum inverted harmonic oscillator）。通过修改Krylov扩散算子（Krylov spreading operator）并推广副本技巧（replica trick）中的解析延拓过程来精炼logK复杂度。

Result: 在有限维量子系统中，logK复杂度能够区分真正的混洗和鞍点主导的混洗，在前者中正确避免了不稳定鞍点的指数贡献，在后者中紧密跟踪传统Krylov复杂度。在可积量子系统中，通过修改Krylov扩散算子，logK复杂度能够捕捉理论的可积性质。经典版本的分析表明，经典相空间中不稳定鞍点引起的假阳性不存在。

Conclusion: 对数Krylov复杂度是一种可行的早期算子混洗探针，能够避免假阳性，并在量子系统和经典系统中均表现出良好的区分能力。该度量通过副本方法定义，能够有效区分不同类型的算子增长行为。

Abstract: We propose and test logarithmic Krylov (logK) complexity, an operator growth measure akin to Krylov complexity defined through a replica approach, as a viable probe of early-time operator scrambling without false positives. In finite-dimensional quantum systems, such as the Lipkin--Meshkov--Glick (LMG) model and the mixed-field Ising model at the chaotic point, we provide numerical evidence that logK-complexity discriminates between genuine and saddle-dominated scrambling at early times, correctly avoiding the exponential contribution coming from the unstable saddle in the former case, and closely tracking the conventional Krylov complexity in the latter. In integrable quantum systems admitting infinite-dimensional Krylov subspaces, such as the SYK$_{2}$ model and the quantum inverted harmonic oscillator, we show that by modifying the Krylov spreading operator, obtained through generalizing the analytic continuation procedure in the replica trick, the logK complexity can be refined to capture the integrable properties of the theories. We supplement these analyses by extending the Krylov formalism in classical dynamical systems and defining classical versions of these operator growth measures, showing that the false positives arising from unstable saddles in classical phase space are non-existent.

</details>


### [88] [Modular Properties of Symplectic Fermion Generalised Gibbs Ensemble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19383)
*Faisal Karimi,Gérard M. T. Watts*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究辛费米子（symplectic fermion）这一c=-2的非幺正共形场论，推导了柱面上的守恒荷表达式，构建了广义吉布斯系综（GGE），并计算了模S变换的精确表达式。研究还探讨了守恒荷子集与KdV和Boussinesq层次结构的关系，并将GGE识别为辛费米子场的平移不变纯传输缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 辛费米子作为c=-2的非幺正共形场论（non-unitary conformal field theory）包含无限族相互对易的守恒荷，研究其广义吉布斯系综（Generalised Gibbs Ensembles）的构建与性质具有理论意义。本文旨在推导守恒荷在柱面上的表达式，并研究其在W(1,2)三重态模型中的具体应用。

Method: 在W(1,2)三重态模型（triplet model）的特定情况下，推导柱面上的守恒荷表达式，并利用这些表达式构建广义吉布斯系综。计算辛费米子各扇区（以及整个GGE）的模S变换（modular S-transforms）精确表达式，并提取化学势趋近零时的渐近行为表达式。

Result: 对于与W_3代数的零模W_0对应的荷，获得的渐近行为与伴文[1]中的猜想精确一致；对于KdV子集，结果与单个自由费米子的情况完全对应。研究还将GGE识别为辛费米子场的平移不变且纯传输的缺陷（translation invariant and purely transmitting defect）。

Conclusion: 本文成功构建了辛费米子的广义吉布斯系综，获得了模S变换的精确表达式，验证了相关猜想，并建立了GGE与平移不变纯传输缺陷的对应关系。研究结果为进一步探讨W_n代数（W_n algebras）的关系提供了基础。

Abstract: The symplectic fermion is a much-studied non-unitary conformal field theory with $c=-2$ and is known to contain an infinite family of mutually commuting conserved charges. We derive expressions for the conserved charges on the cylinder and use these to construct Generalised Gibbs Ensembles (GGEs) in the particular case of the ${W}(1,2)$ triplet model. We derive exact expressions for the modular $S$-transforms in each sector of the symplectic fermion (and so of the whole GGE) and further extract the expressions in the asymptotic regime where the chemical potentials go to zero. Subsets of the conserved charges are known to reproduce the KdV and Boussinesq hierarchies. For the case in which the charge is identified with the zero mode $W_0$ of the $W_3$ algebra, we obtain asymptotic behaviour in precise agreement with the conjecture proposed in our companion paper [1]; for the KdV subset we obtain results which exactly mirror the case for a single free fermion. Finally we identify the GGE with a translation invariant and purely transmitting defect for the symplectic fermion fields, and make some comments on the relation to other $W_n$ algebras.

</details>


### [89] [Bound States in Scalar Theory with Fourth-order Derivative Term](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19478)
*Ichiro Oda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了含四阶导数项的标量理论中束缚态的形成问题。通过将理论重写为标准二阶导数标量理论，计算了由负范数（negative norm）的鬼粒子（ghost）和正范数（positive norm）的正常场（normal field）构成的复合算符关联函数。结果表明，在耦合常数较大时，标量场吸引作用会在两种场的关联函数中产生束缚态极点，但在对应于引力子的近无质量正常粒子的关联函数中则不会出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究含四阶导数项的标量理论中是否形成束缚态。该问题与二次引力理论（quadratic gravity）中的鬼粒子禁闭（confinement of massive ghost）和幺正性破坏（unitarity violation）问题密切相关，旨在为解决二次引力理论中的幺正性问题提供新视角。

Method: 方法是将含四阶导数项的标量理论重写为标准二阶导数标量理论。随后在梯状近似（ladder approximation）下，计算由负范数的大质量鬼粒子和正范数的大质量正常场构成的复合算符关联函数。

Result: 结果显示，当耦合常数较大时，标量场的吸引作用会在鬼粒子和正常场的关联函数中产生束缚态极点。然而，在对应于引力子的近无质量正常粒子的关联函数中，则不会出现此类束缚态。

Conclusion: 该模型为理解二次引力理论中大质量鬼粒子的禁闭机制提供了新思路，从而有望解决与鬼粒子相关的幺正性破坏问题。研究还指出了含四阶导数项的标量理论与二次引力理论之间的内在联系。

Abstract: We consider a problem whether bound states are made in a scalar theory with a fourth-order derivative term or not. After rewriting the theory to a standard scalar theory with second-order derivative terms, we calculate a correlation function of the composite operators made out of massive ghosts with negative norm and massive normal fields with positive norm in the ladder approximation. It is shown that there appears a pole of the bound state in the correlation function of the both fields by attraction due to scalar field when the coupling constant is large whereas there does not so in the correlation function of almost massless normal particles corresponding to the graviton. We also point out the relationship between the scalar theory with a fourth-order derivative term and quadratic gravity. Our model may shed some light on the confinement of massive ghost in quadratic gravity, thereby enabling us to solve the problem of unitarity violation associated with the massive ghost.

</details>


### [90] [Advances in the Worldline Approach to Quantum Field Theory: Strong Fields, Amplitudes and Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19726)
*Filippo Fecit*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文系统阐述了量子场论的第一量子化方法（即"世界线形式体系"），展示了其在广泛物理背景下的多功能性和计算效率，涵盖从标量粒子到自旋2粒子的不同场论体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在展示世界线形式体系（Worldline Formalism）在量子场论中的广泛应用潜力，特别是在处理强背景场相互作用、散射振幅计算和热核（heat kernel）微扰展开等基础物理问题时的优势。

Method: 采用第一量子化方法（first-quantized approach）研究量子场论，系统考察不同自旋粒子的场论体系：从标量粒子开始，经过阿贝尔（abelian）和非阿贝尔（non-abelian）情况下的自旋1粒子，最后到质量和无质量情况下的自旋2粒子。

Result: 研究展示了世界线形式体系在微扰和非微扰分析中的多功能性和计算效率，特别是在处理强背景场相互作用、散射振幅计算以及热核微扰展开等复杂物理情境时的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过一系列从标量到自旋2粒子的实例分析，论文证明了世界线形式体系在解决理论物理学中基本开放问题时的灵活性和计算能力，展示了该形式体系在日益复杂物理情境中的扩展潜力。

Abstract: This thesis is devoted to the first-quantized approach to quantum field theory, commonly known as the 'Worldline Formalism'. It collects most of the works completed by the author during the PhD, illustrating the versatility and efficiency of this formalism across a broad range of physical contexts. The applications discussed fall into two broad categories: perturbative and non-perturbative analyses. In particular, the thesis investigates how quantum particles interact with strong background fields, how scattering amplitudes can be efficiently computed, and how perturbative expansions of the heat kernel can be systematically performed. These studies highlight recent advances in extending the worldline approach to increasingly complex situations. Different field theories are examined from this first-quantized perspective and are organized according to the spin of the particle under consideration. The discussion begins with the seemingly simple scalar case, progresses through spin 1, both in the abelian and the non-abelian case, and concludes with spin-2 particles, both in the massless and in the massive realizations. Through this sequence of examples, the thesis aims to demonstrate the flexibility as well as the computational power of the Worldline Formalism in addressing fundamental open problems in theoretical physics.

</details>


### [91] [Phase Diagram and Finite Temperature Properties of Negative Coupling Scalar Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19877)
*Paul Romatschke*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨具有负四次自相互作用（negative quartic self-interaction）的标量场理论，其经典势能呈倒置形态。尽管缺乏经典稳定基态，该理论在量子力学处理下表现出稳定性和幺正时间演化，为连续介质中的相互作用标量场理论提供了有前景的候选方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索具有负四次自相互作用的标量场理论，其对应倒置经典势能（upside-down classical potential）。这类理论虽缺乏经典稳定基态，但在量子力学框架下却能表现出稳定性和幺正性，为构建连续介质中的相互作用标量场理论提供新途径。

Method: 研究方法采用两种不同的鞍点展开（saddle-point expansions）分析同一理论。通过该方法，作者讨论了欧几里得维度一至四（Euclidean dimensions one to four）中裸参数（bare parameters）的相图，并将其推广至有限温度情形。

Result: 研究结果表明，负耦合场论（negative coupling field theory）是连续介质中相互作用标量场理论的有力候选者。特别在四维情况下，该理论利用量子平庸性（quantum triviality）数学证明中的漏洞，暗示负耦合标量场理论可能为希格斯粒子（Higgs）提供紫外完备且相互作用的描述。

Conclusion: 结论指出，负耦合标量场理论在量子力学处理下表现出稳定性和幺正性，为构建连续介质中的相互作用标量场理论开辟了新路径。该理论尤其在四维情况下展现出规避量子平庸性证明的潜力，可能为希格斯物理提供紫外完备的理论框架。

Abstract: In this work, I consider scalar field theory with negative quartic self-interaction, corresponding to an upside-down classical potential. Despite not possessing a classically stable ground state, such potentials are known to behave properly when treated quantum mechanically, leading to stable and unitary time evolution. Using two different saddle-point expansions for the same theory, I discuss the phase diagram in terms of bare parameters in Euclidean dimensions one to four, as well as the generalization to finite temperature. Comparing to other methods where available, I find that negative coupling field theory is a promising candidate for an interacting scalar field theory in the continuum. In particular, in four dimensions it exploits a loophole in mathematical proofs of quantum triviality, suggesting that negative coupling scalar field theory could offer a UV-complete and interacting description of the Higgs.

### [92] [Gauss law constraint in A-theory branes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19878)
*Machiko Hatsuda,Ondrej Hulık,William D. Linch,Di Wang,Yu-Ping Wang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: A-理论通过将弦世界面扩展为更高维膜世界体来实现U-对偶对称性，其中高斯定律约束将时空坐标提升为规范场。该理论在D=3和4情况下仅存在一致的弦解，表明物理对称性为二维共形对称性，支持弦式量子化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: A-理论旨在实现U-对偶对称性（U-duality symmetry），通过将弦世界面（string worldsheet）扩展为更高维的膜世界体（brane worldvolume）。该理论中，世界体和时空属于例外群（exceptional group）的不同表示，需要解决高斯定律约束（Gauss law constraint）的处理问题以实现量子化。

Method: 采用高斯定律约束将时空坐标提升为规范场，并将弦世界面扩展为膜世界体。通过维拉索罗约束（Virasoro constraint）约化时空坐标，同时使用高斯定律约束约化世界体和时空坐标。特别关注D=3和4情况下高斯定律维数约化条件的一致解。

Result: 证明弦解（string solution）仅在D=3和4情况下是高斯定律维数约化条件的一致解。这一结果表明理论的物理对称性为二维共形对称性（two-dimensional conformal symmetry），暗示理论允许弦式量子化（string-like quantization）。进一步构建了在例外群对称性下协变的弦解。

Conclusion: A-理论通过膜世界体框架实现U-对偶对称性，其中高斯定律约束在量子化中起关键作用。弦解仅在特定维度下一致存在，支持理论的弦式量子化方案。构建的例外群协变弦解与例外σ-模型（exceptional σ-model）中的常数电荷参数存在关联。

Abstract: A-theory realizes U-duality symmetry by extending the string worldsheet to a higher dimensional brane worldvolume, in which the worldvolume and the spacetime belong to different representations of the exceptional group. The closure of the brane Virasoro algebra requires the Gauss law constraint. The Gauss law constraint promotes spacetime coordinates to gauge fields and extends the string worldsheet into the brane worldvolume. While the Virasoro constraint is used to reduce the spacetime coordinate, the Gauss law constraint is used to reduce both the worldvolume and the spacetime coordinates. As in conventional gauge theories, the treatment of the Gauss law constraint is a technically important aspect of the quantization of A-theory. We show that the string solution is only consistent solution of the Gauss law dimensional reduction condition for D=3 and 4 cases. This result implies that the physical symmetry of the theory is two-dimensional conformal symmetry, suggesting that the theory admits a string-like quantization. We further construct a string solution that is covariant under the exceptional group symmetry. The relation between this solution and the constant charge parameter appearing in the exceptional σ-model is also discussed.

</details>


### [93] [Some rigidity results for supergravity backgrounds in 11 dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19923)
*Emanuele Di Bella,Willem A. de Graaf,Andrea Santi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了11维超引力背景的"超对称间隙"问题，建立了当4-形式F的秩≤6且Killing旋量维度>26时，背景必须局部等距于最大超对称Minkowski时空或AdS₇×S⁴的刚性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决11维超引力背景的超对称间隙（supersymmetry gap）问题，研究对背景曲率的限制条件。通过分析超对称背景的几何结构，探索在何种条件下背景必须简化为已知的最大超对称解。

Method: 利用李超代数（Lie superalgebras）特定过滤形变空间与高度超对称超引力背景空间之间的双射对应关系。通过分析4-形式F的秩（rank）和Killing旋量（Killing spinors）的维度，结合洛伦兹群（Lorentz group）作用下4-形式的特定轨道分类。

Result: 建立了关键刚性定理：当4-形式F的秩rk(F)≤6、具有欧几里得支撑（Euclidean support），且Killing旋量空间维度dim𝔨₁>26时，背景(M,g,F)局部等距于最大超对称Minkowski时空或Freund-Rubin背景AdS₇×S⁴。对于特定类型的𝔨₁和洛伦兹群轨道，给出了更精细的维度估计。

Conclusion: 论文证明了在11维超引力中，当超对称性足够高（Killing旋量超过26个）且4-形式F的秩足够低时，背景几何受到严格限制，只能简化为已知的最大超对称解。这为超对称间隙问题提供了重要的理论约束。

Abstract: This paper is a contribution to the supersymmetry gap problem for supergravity backgrounds $(M,g,F)$ in $11$ dimensions. We study restrictions on the curvature of $(M,g,F)$ and, using the bijective correspondence between the space of certain filtered deformations of Lie superalgebras and the space of highly supersymmetric supergravity backgrounds, we establish the following general rigidity result: if the $4$-form $F$ has rank $\operatorname{rk}(F)\leq 6$, Euclidean support, and the space $\mathfrak{k}_{\bar 1}$ of Killing spinors has dimension $\dim\mathfrak{k}_{\bar 1}> 26$ then $(M,g,F)$ is locally isometric to the maximally supersymmetric Minkowski spacetime or Freund Rubin background $\mathrm{AdS}_7\times\mathrm{S}^4$. The same rigidity result but with finer estimates on $\dim\mathfrak{k}_{\bar 1}$ is provided for certain types of $\mathfrak k_{\bar 1}$ and specific orbits of the $4$-form under the action of the Lorentz group.

</details>


### [94] [Giant graviton integrated correlators at finite coupling and all orders in $1/N$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20083)
*Augustus Brown,Daniele Dorigoni,Congkao Wen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究分析了SU(N)和U(N) N=4超对称杨-米尔斯理论中巨引力子（giant graviton）积分关联子在有限复耦合τ下的性质。研究发现大N展开具有显著模不变性（modular invariance），展开系数由非全纯艾森斯坦级数（non-holomorphic Eisenstein series）组成，并包含指数抑制的模函数。研究获得了U(N)理论的闭形式表达式，并首次在有限N下计算了两圈阶巨引力子关联子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解SU(N) N=4超对称杨-米尔斯理论中巨引力子积分关联子在有限复耦合τ下的行为。尽管所考虑的算符具有重性（heavy nature）导致计算极其复杂，但大N展开却展现出显著的简化特性，这为深入研究非微扰效应提供了契机。

Method: 研究方法基于大N展开分析，利用积分关联子约束条件。通过研究展开系数与非全纯艾森斯坦级数的关系，捕捉了杨-米尔斯耦合中完整的微扰和非微扰效应谱。特别地，利用了模不变性这一关键性质来简化分析。

Result: 研究结果显示，大N展开在每个1/N阶上，展开系数都是非全纯艾森斯坦级数的线性组合。发现了指数抑制于N的附加模函数贡献。在't Hooft极限下，获得了任意耦合λ下1/N展开的全阶结果。对于U(N)理论，得到了对所有N和τ有效的闭形式表达式，并证明SU(N)和U(N)之间耦合依赖部分具有全阶普适性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功确定了有限N下两圈阶巨引力子关联子，这之前仅在平面极限下可计算。研究揭示了巨引力子积分关联子在大N展开中的模不变性结构，以及SU(N)和U(N)理论间耦合依赖部分的普适性，为理解N=4超对称杨-米尔斯理论中重算符的非微扰性质提供了新见解。

Abstract: We study the giant graviton integrated correlator in SU$(N)$ $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills at finite complexified coupling $τ$. Despite the formidable complexity arising from the heavy nature of the operators considered, the large-$N$ expansion simplifies dramatically and exhibits manifest modular invariance. At each order in $1/N$, the expansion coefficients are linear combinations of non-holomorphic Eisenstein series thus capturing the full spectrum of perturbative and non-perturbative effects in the Yang-Mills coupling. Furthermore, we find additional contributions which are modular functions exponentially suppressed in $N$. In the 't Hooft limit, this yields an all-orders result in the $1/N$ expansion at arbitrary coupling $λ$, extending beyond prior results of leading orders. For the U$(N)$ theory, we obtain a closed-form expression valid for all $N$ and $τ$, and show that the coupling-dependent sector of the large-$N$ expansion is universal between SU$(N)$ and U$(N)$ to all orders. Crucially, we exploit the integrated correlator constraints and determine the giant graviton correlator itself to two-loop order at finite $N$, previously only accessible in the planar limit.

</details>

### [95] [Survival of the most compact: the life and death of satellite halos in self-interacting dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19362)
*David Klemmer,Moritz S. Fischer,Kimberly K. Boddy,Manoj Kaplinghat,Laura Sagunski*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种计算高效的模拟框架，用于研究自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）模型中依赖于速度和角度的自相互作用截面下的子晕演化与引力热坍缩，强调了散射诱导的子晕-晕相互作用对子晕结构演化的重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）模型通过暗物质粒子间的短程相互作用，可能解释星系旋转曲线内区的多样性并产生独特的引力透镜特征。卫星星系和暗物质子晕为检验此类模型提供了重要场所。

Method: 开发了模拟框架，采用N体模拟，对主晕进行解析处理，并使用虚拟主晕粒子模拟散射诱导的子晕-晕相互作用过程。采用埃丁顿反演方法精确模拟晕内的局域速度分布，并考虑了潮汐剥离和潮汐加热效应。

Result: 环境效应，特别是散射诱导的子晕-晕相互作用，对子晕演化有强烈影响并驱动复杂的结构演化。与无碰撞暗物质相比，SIDM子晕具有更广的中心密度范围和密度轮廓斜率多样性。

Conclusion: 该计算高效的模拟框架使得在真实环境中模拟SIDM子晕成为可能。研究结果强调了精确模拟散射诱导的子晕-晕相互作用对于预测SIDM子晕密度轮廓的必要性，其增强的质量轮廓多样性将在强透镜系统和卫星星系中留下可观测印记。

Abstract: Self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) models feature short-range interactions between dark matter (DM) particles that lead to larger diversity in the inner parts of galactic rotation curves and potentially unique gravitational lensing signatures. Satellite galaxies and dark subhalos provide a valuable testing ground for such models. We develop a simulation framework to explore subhalo evolution and its gravothermal collapse for velocity- and angle-dependent self-interacting cross section in these SIDM models. Our results are essential for testing these models. We perform N-body simulations, treating the host halo analytically and modelling the scattering-induced subhalo-halo interaction process using virtual host particles, a central innovation of our work. We use the Eddington inversion method to accurately model the local velocity distribution in the halo. Our approach is significantly less computationally expensive than simulations with a fully resolved host, while incorporating tidal stripping and tidal heating. We test both isotropic and forward-dominated self-scattering, which represent limiting cases for the angular dependence of the self-interaction cross section. Environmental effects, especially the scattering-induced subhalo-halo interaction, have a strong impact on the subhalo evolution and drive a complex structural evolution. As a result, SIDM subhalos have a larger range of central densities and density profile slopes compared to collisionless DM. Our cost-efficient simulation framework enables modelling of SIDM subhalos in realistic environments. Our results highlight the necessity of accurately modelling the scattering-induced subhalo-halo interaction to predict SIDM subhalo density profiles. For the SIDM models we investigate, the enhanced diversity in the mass profiles of subhalos would leave an observable imprint on strong lensing systems and satellite galaxies.

</details>

### [96] [Analytically tractable model of synaptic crowding explains emergent small-world structure and network dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19320)
*Makoto Fukushima*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 该研究提出一个基于突触拥挤（synaptic crowding）的最小化布线规则模型，该模型仅需单个参数即可解释神经网络中连接度的对数增长、有界方差以及小世界特性等宏观组织特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络需要在局部连接约束与全局整合需求之间取得平衡。研究旨在探索局部发育约束如何影响宏观网络组织和动力学，特别是突触拥挤现象——即随着神经元积累输入连接，每个额外突触的形成难度逐渐增加。

Method: 引入一个受突触拥挤启发的单参数最小化布线规则模型。该模型考虑了候选连接按空间邻近顺序出现的情况，并结合了捷径重连（shortcut rewiring）机制。通过精确的有限尺寸解分析诱导入度分布，并研究其在阈值网络动力学中对吸引子盆地边界的影响。

Result: 模型产生简单标度律：平均连接度随网络规模仅呈对数增长，而方差保持有界，这与突触密度的稳态调节一致。拥挤规则在未规定任何显式距离依赖布线法则的情况下，产生了广泛的近似幂律连接长度分布；结合捷径重连可生成具有小世界特性的网络。诱导度统计主要决定阈值网络动力学中的吸引子盆地边界，而局部聚类主要调节这些边界附近长寿命非吸收结果的普遍性。

Conclusion: 该模型提供了可检验的预测，将局部发育约束与宏观网络组织和动力学联系起来，表明突触拥挤这一简单机制能够解释神经网络中观察到的多种统计和拓扑特征。

Abstract: Neural circuits must balance local connectivity constraints against the need for global integration. Here we introduce a minimal wiring rule motivated by synaptic crowding: as a neuron accumulates incoming connections, each additional synapse becomes progressively harder to form. This single-parameter model admits an exact finite-size solution for the induced in-degree distribution and yields simple scaling laws: mean connectivity grows only logarithmically with network size while variance remains bounded -- consistent with homeostatic regulation of synaptic density. When candidates are encountered in order of spatial proximity, the crowding rule produces a broad, approximately power-law distribution of connection lengths without prescribing any explicit distance-dependent wiring law; combined with shortcut rewiring, this yields networks with small-world characteristics. We further show that the induced degree statistics largely determine attractor basin boundaries in threshold network dynamics, while local clustering primarily modulates the prevalence of long-lived non-absorbing outcomes near these boundaries. The model provides testable predictions linking local developmental constraints to macroscopic network organization and dynamics.

</details>

### [97] [A Federated Many-to-One Hopfield model for associative Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19902)
*Andrea Alessandrelli,Fabrizio Durante,Andrea Ladiana,Andrea Lepre*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种联邦关联记忆框架，用于解决联邦学习中的客户端异构性和流式分布偏移问题。该方法通过学习共享原型（archetypes）来处理异构、持续的学习场景，避免遗忘并保持隐私保护。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习（federated learning）在客户端异构性和流式分布偏移（streaming distribution shifts）下存在收敛困难和遗忘问题。客户端数据独立但不一定平衡，且存在漂移（drift）和新数据（novel data）的挑战。

Method: 提出联邦关联记忆（federated associative-memory）框架，客户端将经验编码为低秩赫布算子（low-rank Hebbian operator）并发送到中央服务器。服务器通过聚合和因子分解（factorization）生成全局原型（global archetypes），将聚合建模为低秩加噪声谱推断问题（low-rank-plus-noise spectral inference problem），并采用基于熵的控制器（entropy-based controller）平衡稳定性和可塑性。

Result: 该方法在异构客户端、数据漂移和新数据场景下表现出改进的全局原型重构和关联检索（associative retrieval）能力。理论分析推导了可检测性（detectability）和检索鲁棒性的阈值，支持联邦整合的谱视角（spectral view）。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架能够保护隐私、避免集中式回放缓冲区（centralized replay buffers），并对小型、噪声或演化数据集具有鲁棒性。该方法为联邦学习中的异构持续学习问题提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Federated learning enables collaborative training without sharing raw data, but struggles under client heterogeneity and streaming distribution shifts, where drift and novel data can impair convergence and cause forgetting. We propose a federated associative-memory framework that learns shared archetypes in heterogeneous, continual settings, where client data are independent but not necessarily balanced. Each client encodes its experience as a low-rank Hebbian operator, sent to a central server for aggregation and factorization into global archetypes. This approach preserves privacy, avoids centralized replay buffers, and is robust to small, noisy, or evolving datasets. We cast aggregation as a low-rank-plus-noise spectral inference problem, deriving theoretical thresholds for detectability and retrieval robustness. An entropy-based controller balances stability and plasticity in streaming regimes. Experiments with heterogeneous clients, drift, and novelty show improved global archetype reconstruction and associative retrieval, supporting the spectral view of federated consolidation.

</details>


### [98] [Continuous Specialization Transition in the Soft Committee Machine with ReLU Activation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20010)
*Assem Afanah,Bernd Rosenow*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过副本方法分析具有修正线性单元（ReLU）激活函数的软委员会机，发现其表现出从非专门化对称相到专门化相的连续相变，与使用sigmoid激活函数的同类模型的一阶相变形成鲜明对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解激活函数对多层神经网络相结构和泛化行为的影响，特别是在可实现的师生设置中分析ReLU激活函数的软委员会机的典型泛化特性。

Method: 采用副本方法（replica method）分析ReLU激活的软委员会机，在副本对称假设下计算淬火自由能（quenched free energy），并通过鞍点方程求解宏观序参数。

Result: 系统表现出从非专门化对称相到专门化相的转变，其中隐藏单元间的置换对称性被破坏。确定了临界训练集大小与逆训练温度的函数关系，并推导了接近相变和大样本渐近区域的解析表达式。

Conclusion: 与sigmoid激活函数的一阶相变不同，ReLU软委员会机表现出连续专门化相变，这表明激活函数对多层网络的相结构和泛化行为具有决定性作用。

Abstract: We analyze the soft committee machine with Rectified Linear Unit (ReLU) activation by means of the replica method. In a realizable teacher--student setting, we compute the quenched free energy within a replica-symmetric ansatz and obtain the typical generalization behavior from the saddle-point equations for the macroscopic order parameters. The system exhibits a transition from an unspecialized symmetric phase to a specialized phase in which the permutation symmetry among hidden units is broken. We determine the critical training-set size as a function of the inverse training temperature and derive analytic expressions both near the transition and in the asymptotic large-sample regime. Unlike the corresponding model with sigmoidal activations, which undergoes a first-order transition, the ReLU soft committee machine shows a continuous specialization transition. These results show that the activation function plays a decisive role in the phase structure and generalization behavior of multilayer networks.

</details>

### [99] [Recursive Penrose processes in electrically charged black hole spacetimes: Backreaction and energy extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19354)
*Duarte Feiteira,José P. S. Lemos,Oleg B. Zaslavskii*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在反德西特（anti-de Sitter）渐近的Reissner-Nordström黑洞时空中，带电粒子衰变的递归彭罗斯过程（recursive Penrose process）及能量提取，考虑了黑洞质量和电荷的反作用（backreaction）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索在AdS时空中带电粒子的递归衰变过程，特别关注黑洞电荷和质量反作用对能量提取过程的影响。AdS时空的自然约束特性使得粒子能够被限制在有限区域内，为递归过程提供了理想环境。

Method: 采用递归彭罗斯过程方法，分析带电粒子在Reissner-Nordström-AdS黑洞中的衰变。通过追踪黑洞电荷Q_n随衰变次数n的变化，定义临界指数n_c，并区分整数和非整数n_c两种情况。考虑了两种约束机制：AdS的自然反射和有限半径处的镜像边界。

Result: 当n_c为整数时，黑洞电荷经过有限次衰变后精确降为零，但最后一个粒子会返回并被黑洞吸收，最终形成带电黑洞。当n_c为非整数时，黑洞电荷可无限减小但永不为零，过程在n=n_c⁻时终止。两种情况下系统都能获得有限能量增益，且反作用确保了能量提取的有限性。

Conclusion: 结论表明，在考虑反作用的情况下，递归彭罗斯过程能够提取有限能量，不会产生黑洞炸弹（black hole bomb）现象。系统最多作为能量工厂运作，过程会在违反宇宙监督假设（cosmic censorship）前自然终止。

Abstract: We study a recursive Penrose process and the energy extraction for the decay of electrically charged particles in a Reissner-Nordström black hole spacetime with anti-de Sitter (AdS) asymptotics, incorporating the backreaction on the black hole's mass and charge. A recursive process requires that the decay products are confined in a finite region so that the emitted particles bounce back for further decay. In AdS spacetimes, the confinement arises naturally. Outgoing particles encounter a turning point and are reflected. One may impose a mirror at finite radius, but in AdS, backreaction makes these two confinement methods equivalent. Let $Q_n$ be the black hole charge after $n$ decays, and define $n_{\rm c}$ as the index for which the black hole's charge is zero, $Q_{n_{\rm c}}=0$. For $n_{\rm c}$ integer the black hole's charge decreases and reaches exactly zero after a finite number of decays, terminating the process. However, the last particle turns back, and encountering zero charge, falls into the hole. The final state is a charged black hole whose charge equals the sum of the original black hole and the initial particle charges. For $n_{\rm c}$ noninteger, the black hole charge decreases and can be arbitrarily small, but is never zero. The last allowed decay occurs at $n=n_{c}^-$, where $n=n_{c}^-$ is the greatest integer less than $n_{\rm c}$. Any further decay invalidates the approximations, the particles would carry a charge comparable to the black hole mass, transforming the problem into a two-body problem. The would-be subsequent decay would violate cosmic censorship and the process terminates before any inconsistency arises. In the integer and noninteger cases, the system yields a finite energy gain. Backreaction ensures that the process extracts a finite amount of energy. No black hole bomb occurs, the system works at most as an energy factory.

</details>


### [100] [Cosmology and modified GW propagation from the BNS mass function at third-generation detector networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19377)
*Dounia Nanadoumgar-Lacroze,Niccolò Muttoni,Michele Maggiore,Michele Mancarella*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究利用双中子星质量函数信息，对第三代引力波探测器（爱因斯坦望远镜和宇宙探索者）进行哈勃参数H_0和修正引力波传播参数Xi_0的预测分析，评估了不同探测器配置对宇宙学参数的约束能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在评估第三代引力波探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜和宇宙探索者）在约束宇宙学参数方面的能力，特别是哈勃参数H_0和描述修正引力波传播的参数Xi_0。通过分析双中子星质量函数信息，为未来引力波宇宙学研究提供预测性评估。

Method: 研究采用全联合宇宙学-群体贝叶斯推断方法，基于双中子星质量函数信息进行预测。分析对象包括爱因斯坦望远镜的三角形和"2L"两种配置，以及由爱因斯坦望远镜与40公里宇宙探索者组成的探测器网络。研究限制在高信噪比（SNR>50）的双中子星事件，预计每年仍有约10^3个事件。

Result: 对于独立运行的爱因斯坦望远镜，三角形和2L配置对H_0的约束精度分别为12%和11%，对Xi_0的约束精度均为18%。当加入宇宙探索者组成网络时，H_0和Xi_0的约束精度分别提升至9%和6%。研究还发现，爱因斯坦望远镜单独运行时对H(z)的最佳约束精度在红移z=0.23和0.28处分别为10%和6%，加入宇宙探索者后，在z=0.37和0.38处的精度分别提升至4%和3%。

Conclusion: 第三代引力波探测器在约束宇宙学参数方面具有显著潜力，特别是当爱因斯坦望远镜与宇宙探索者组成网络时，约束精度得到显著提升。由于采用了高信噪比截断，这些结果应被视为对第三代探测器能力的保守估计。

Abstract: We perform forecasts for the Hubble parameter H_0 and for the parameter Xi_0 that describes modified gravitational-wave propagation, using information from the binary neutron star (BNS) mass function, for Einstein Telescope (ET), taken either in the triangle or in the ``2L'' configuration, as well as for detector network made by ET together with a 40-km Cosmic Explorer (CE). We restrict ourselves to BNSs with a large signal-to-noise ratio, SNR>50, which still give O(10^3) events yr-1, and we perform a full joint cosmology-population Bayesian inference. We find that, for ET in isolation, the two ET configurations perform comparably, yielding uncertainties of 12% and 11% on H_0 for the triangular and 2L designs, respectively, and 18% uncertainty on Xi_0 in both cases. For networks including ET and CE, we can constrain H_0 and Xi_0 to precisions of 9% and 6%, respectively. These results should be taken as a very conservative estimate of third-generation detectors' capabilities as a consequence of the high SNR cut. We project the constraints on the Lambda CDM expansion history and find that ET alone (triangular and 2L configurations) achieves its best precision on H(z) at z=0.23 and z=0.28, yielding a 10% and 6% precision, respectively. When CE is added to the network, the precision improves to 4% and 3% at z=0.37 and z=0.38, respectively.

</details>


### [101] [Ringdown modeling for effective-one-body waveforms in the test-mass limit for eccentric equatorial orbits around a Kerr black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19413)
*Simone Albanesi,Sebastiano Bernuzzi,Alessandro Nagar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一个完整的偏心旋进-合并-铃宕（inspiral-merger-ringdown）波形模型，适用于克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）中非自旋粒子的偏心平面旋进过程。模型从光环穿越（light-ring crossing）相关点开始建模，能够处理高自旋和高偏心率情况，并自然地扩展到动态捕获（dynamical capture）场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于详细分析克尔黑洞中非自旋粒子偏心平面旋进的坠入（plunge）和合并（merger）阶段。需要构建一个完整的波形模型，能够处理高自旋和高偏心率情况，并自然地扩展到动态捕获场景。

Method: 研究方法采用有效单体（effective-one-body）辐射反应驱动动力学，使用2+1时域代码Teukode求解Teukolsky方程获得数值波形。对合并-铃宕波形采用封闭形式（closed-form ansätze）进行建模，建模起点与光环穿越相关而非振幅峰值。

Result: 成功建模了所有m≥1直到ℓ=4的多极子模式，以及(2,0)、(5,5)、(5,4)、(5,3)模式，包含了球面-球面模态混合（spherical-spheroidal mode-mixing）和共转与反转准正则模态（quasi-normal modes）之间的拍频（beating）。构建了完整的有效单体旋进-坠入波形模型。

Conclusion: 该模型基于类椭圆配置（elliptic-like configurations）构建合并-铃宕阶段，自然地扩展到动态捕获场景而无需修改。研究还探讨了将该框架扩展到一般质量比（generic mass ratios）的可能性，提出与(2,2)波形频率拐点（inflection point）密切相关的时间点可作为铃宕建模的锚定点。

Abstract: We study the plunge and merger of a non-spinning particle falling into a Kerr black hole following an eccentric planar inspiral. The dynamics is driven by an effective-one-body radiation reaction, and the corresponding numerical inspiral-merger-ringdown waveforms are obtained by solving the Teukolsky equation with the 2+1 time-domain code Teukode. We then analyze in detail the plunge and merger phases, modeling the merger-ringdown waveform using closed-form ansätze. Crucially, our modeling starts from a point closely related to the light-ring crossing, rather than from the amplitude peaks. This choice allows us to neglect the impact of the relativistic anomaly at the separatrix-crossing, and to extend the modeling to high spins and high eccentricities. We model all the multipoles with $m\geq 1$ up to $\ell=4$, as well as the $(2,0)$, $(5,5)$, $(5,4)$, and $(5,3)$ modes, including spherical-spheroidal mode-mixing and the beating between co-rotating and counter-rotating quasi-normal modes. The post-merger waveform model is then employed to complete an effective-one-body inspiral-plunge waveform, thus providing a complete description. Our model, built using elliptic-like configurations for the merger-ringdown phase, naturally extends to dynamical capture scenarios without any further modification. Finally, we provide insights into the extension of this framework to generic mass ratios, arguing that a time closely related to the inflection point of the (2,2) waveform frequency could be used as anchoring point for the ringdown modeling.

</details>


### [102] [Observational imprints and quasi-Periodic oscillations of magnetically charged anti-de Sitter black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19458)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Mohsen Fathi,Ahmad Al-Badawi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了弦理论启发的欧拉-海森堡理论中磁荷反德西特黑洞的可观测特征，包括光子轨迹、黑洞阴影、粒子轨道运动及准周期振荡数据拟合，发现磁荷参数会显著影响这些特征但现有观测数据仅对其大小施加中等约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索弦理论启发的欧拉-海森堡理论中磁荷反德西特黑洞的可观测特征，分析磁荷参数如何影响黑洞周围的光传播和粒子运动，并将其理论预测与观测数据进行比较。

Method: 采用光子轨迹分析推导光子球和阴影半径，使用有效势方法研究中性及带电粒子运动并计算相应的回旋频率，通过二维Delta chi-square分析在(r, Q_m)参数空间拟合双峰准周期振荡数据。

Result: 磁荷参数Q_m增加导致光子球和阴影半径单调减小，最内稳定圆轨道半径发生偏移，径向、垂直和轨道频率明显偏离史瓦西情况；与准周期振荡数据的最佳拟合对应Q_m=0，但在置信水平内有限值仍被允许，1 sigma水平下获得上限Q_m/M小于约0.2。

Conclusion: 磁荷参数在理论上会产生可测量的偏差，显著影响黑洞周围的光传播和轨道结构，但目前的准周期振荡数据仅对其大小施加中等约束，表明需要更精确的观测数据来进一步限制磁荷参数。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate observable signatures of a magnetically charged Anti-de Sitter black hole in string-inspired Euler-Heisenberg theory. We analyze photon trajectories, the photon sphere, and the resulting black hole shadow. We derive the photon sphere and shadow radii and show that both deviate from the Schwarzschild and Schwarzschild-AdS cases. In particular, the radii decrease monotonically as the magnetic charge parameter $Q_m$ increases, indicating that magnetic charge modifies light propagation near the black hole. We also study neutral and charged particle motion and compute the corresponding epicyclic frequencies. Using the effective potential method, we obtain the specific energy and angular momentum for stable circular orbits and determine the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO). The presence of $Q_m$ shifts the ISCO radius and alters the orbital structure. The radial, vertical, and orbital frequencies show clear deviations from the Schwarzschild case. Finally, we confront the model with twin-peak quasi-periodic oscillation (QPO) data from stellar-mass, intermediate-mass, and supermassive black hole candidates. A two-dimensional Delta chi-square analysis in the ($r$, $Q_m$) space shows that the best fit corresponds to $Q_m=0$, although finite values remain allowed within confidence levels. At the 1 sigma level, we obtain an upper bound $Q_m/M$ less than about 0.2. These results indicate that while magnetic charge produces measurable theoretical deviations, current QPO data place only moderate constraints on its magnitude.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Dilatonic dyon black hole solution with gravitational radius $2 μ$ and two charges $Q_1$ and $Q_2$ (electric and magnetic ones) in the gravitational $4d$ model with one scalar field and one 2-form is considered. Dilatonic coupling constant $λ$ obeys $λ^2 = \frac{1}{2}$. The circular orbits for null geodesics are explored. The 3rd order polynomial master equation for radius
  $R_0$ of photon sphere is studied. It has only one solution which obeys $R_0 > 2 μ$.
  The circular null geodesics are shown to be unstable. The black hole shadow is studied
  and relations for shadow angle and critical impact parameter are obtained.

### [104] [On the Universal Cuspy Behavior in Black Hole Shadows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19576)
*Peng Cheng,Si-Jiang Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了致密天体阴影中尖点（cusp）形成的普适性，揭示了尖点出现伴随的三个相互关联现象：拓扑电荷转变、自相交结构的等面积定律以及普适临界标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索致密天体阴影中尖点形成的普适性特征，这些特征可能独立于具体的时空度规细节，为未来黑洞观测中识别非克尔（non-Kerr）特征提供模型无关的框架。

Method: 首先系统分析了具有跑动牛顿耦合（running Newton coupling）的克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole），然后扩展框架到旋转可穿越虫洞（rotating traversable wormholes），以验证普适行为在更一般致密天体中的持续性。

Result: 研究发现尖点形成伴随三个普适现象：拓扑电荷转变、自相交结构的等面积定律以及临界标度行为。这些现象源于阴影的全局形态学，因此独立于具体时空度规细节，在不同模型中均适用。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了尖点形成的普适性基础，为未来黑洞观测中识别非克尔特征提供了模型无关的框架，证实了这些普适行为在包括旋转可穿越虫洞在内的更一般致密天体中持续存在。

Abstract: This work investigates the universality of cusp formation in the shadows of compact objects. The emergence of cusps is accompanied by three interrelated phenomena: a topological charge transition, an equal-area law governing the self-intersecting structure, and universal critical scaling behavior. We demonstrate that, because these phenomena originate from the global morphology of the shadow, they are fundamentally independent of specific spacetime metric details and apply across diverse models. These features are systematically analyzed for the Kerr black hole endowed with a running Newton coupling. By extending our framework to rotating traversable wormholes, we confirm that the same universal behavior persists in more general compact objects. Our study uncovers the universality underlying cusp formation, offering a model-independent framework for identifying non-Kerr signatures in future black hole observations.

The innermost stable circular orbits (ISCOs) for both magnetized and electrically charged particles are examined in detail, revealing that the magnetic field parameter B exerts a considerable influence, leading to an increase in the ISCO radius. The orbital and epicyclic motion of test particles in Schwarzschild-BR black hole spacetime was analyzed, including both circular orbits and their oscillatory perturbations. Additionally, the trajectories of both magnetized and electrically charged particles are analyzed for various configurations of the magnetic parameter B. We also demonstrate how the magnetic field B, electric charge q, and magnetic moment μ influence the dynamics of charged particles, specifically affecting the chaotic behavior, Poincare' sections, oscillatory frequencies and power spectral density.

Abstract: We investigate a concrete realization of the Dark Dimension scenario, where a single large extra dimension is set at sub-millimeter scales. In this framework, the Casimir energy of bulk fields accounts for the observed dark energy. Working in a 5-dimensional setup with the Standard Model confined to a 4-dimensional brane, we derive the effective action for the radion. We demonstrate that a minimal model comprising only gravity and three right-handed bulk neutrinos typically yields a negative radion potential. To realize a positive vacuum energy, we consider some extensions with additional bulk degrees of freedom. These extensions generate a sufficiently flat positive potential that allows the radion to behave as a quintessence field, evolving slowly at the sub-eV scale. Finally, we analyze the evolution of the dark-energy equation-of-state parameter and show that our model is consistent with recent DESI BAO measurements, including the distance ratios $D_H/r_d$ and $D_M/r_d$.

### [108] [Modeling the merger-ringdown of an eccentric test-mass inspiral into a Kerr black hole using the effective-one-body framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19913)
*Guglielmo Faggioli,Alessandra Buonanno,Maarten van de Meent,Gaurav Khanna*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在刻画小质量致密天体从赤道偏心轨道坠入克尔黑洞并合过程中引力波并合-铃宕阶段的特征，并为偏心自旋对齐双黑洞波形模型SEOB-TMLE提供并合-铃宕模型，这是将接近并合时的残余偏心效应纳入自旋对齐有效单体（effective-one-body）模型的重要一步。

Method: 采用时域Teukolsky（Teukolsky）代码生成波形，其源轨迹由有效单体（effective-one-body）框架计算。参数空间涵盖克尔自旋a∈[-0.9, 0.9]、最稳定轨道（LSO）偏心率e_LSO∈[0,0.9]和相对论异常ξ_LSO∈[0,2π]。分析包括SEOBNR模型族通常包含的所有自旋权重球谐模（spin-weighted spherical harmonic modes）。

Result: 研究发现偏心率主要影响波形最后一个峰值的特征，而对铃宕信号影响较小；在最稳定轨道测量的相对论异常仅在参数空间有限部分影响最后一个峰值的形态，对铃宕部分无影响。研究为SEOB-TMLE模型引入了包含准正则模混合（quasinormal mode mixing）的并合-铃宕模型。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了偏心自旋对齐双黑洞在测试质量极限（test-mass limit）下的并合-铃宕模型，其特性可扩展至可比质量（comparable-mass）情形。这是将接近并合时的残余偏心效应纳入自旋对齐有效单体并合-铃宕模型的关键第一步。

Abstract: We characterize and phenomenologically model the merger-ringdown of gravitational waves emitted by a small compact object that plunges and merges into a Kerr black hole from equatorial-eccentric inspirals. The waveforms are generated employing a time-domain Teukolsky code sourced with trajectories computed using the effective-one-body framework. We span values of the Kerr spin $a\in[-0.9, 0.9] $, eccentricity at the last stable orbit (LSO) $ e_{\rm LSO} \in [0,0.9] $, and relativistic anomaly $ ξ_{\rm LSO} \in [0 , 2 π]$. We characterize the last peak of the waveform and ringdown features across the parameter space, finding that the eccentricity mainly affects the last peak features, while it has a smaller impact on the ringdown signal. In contrast, the relativistic anomaly measured at the LSO influences the morphology of the last peak in a restricted portion of the parameter space and has no impact on the ringdown part. We perform the analysis for all the spin-weighted spherical harmonic modes normally included in the \texttt{SEOBNR} family of models, $(\ell,m)\in\{ (2,2), (3,3), (4,4), (5,5), (2,1), (3,2), (4,3)\}$. Finally, we introduce a merger-ringdown model for \texttt{SEOB-TMLE}, a forthcoming inspiral-merger-ringdown waveform model for eccentric spin-aligned binary black holes in the test-mass limit, whose features can be extended to comparable-mass regimes. The model also accounts for quasinormal mode mixing during the ringdown. It provides a first step toward incorporating the impact of residual eccentricity close to merger into spin-aligned effective-one-body merger-ringdown models for binary black holes.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于广义相对论和后牛顿近似，在已有1.5PN解基础上，构建了2PN阶解析解，描述具有任意自旋和偏心率的双黑洞系统的相对分离矢量、单个黑洞自旋矢量及轨道角动量矢量的时间演化。

Conclusion: 本文从第一性原理出发，为同时具有自旋和偏心率的双黑洞系统引力波建模提供了改进的2PN阶解析解框架，相比经验性方法具有理论优势。

Abstract: Recent gravitational wave (GW) detections showing signatures of eccentricity and spin precession underscore the need to model binary black holes (BBHs) possessing these features simultaneously. Most efforts over the past fifteen years to model spinning BBHs and their corresponding GWs have relied on heuristically twisting waveforms from non-precessing systems. This approach is based on empirical observations rather than first principles. This article aims to model the GWs from spinning and eccentric BBHs from a first-principles approach within general relativity and post-Newtonian (PN) approximation. Building on the already-existing 1.5 PN solution, we construct an analytical solution for the time evolution of the relative separation vector, the individual black hole spin vectors, and the orbital angular momentum vector at 2PN order for BBHs with arbitrary spins and eccentricity. Such a solution is not fully 2PN accurate in that the tiny orbital timescale fluctuations in the solutions for the spins are only leading 1.5PN order accurate, instead of 2PN. However, it is shown that our new 2PN solution is still an order of magnitude improvement over the earlier 1.5PN solution, underlining the sub-dominant nature of the neglected next-to-leading-order oscillations in the spin solutions.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用有效作用量方法，推导了任意质量多极矩和电流多极矩（mass and current multipole）在角动量失败尾过程中的动力学方程，特别关注了质量八极矩和电流八极矩（mass and current octupoles）与相反宇称四极矩（quadrupoles of opposite parity）的混合贡献。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了角动量失败尾过程的一般理论框架，为理解致密双星系统高阶后牛顿动力学提供了重要基础，特别在六阶后牛顿阶的精度上明确了相关贡献项。

Abstract: We derive the effective action governing the dynamics of a compact binary system when gravitational radiation is emitted by any mass or current multipole, scattered by the quasi-static field associated with the binary's angular momentum, and then reabsorbed. Among such angular momentum failed-tail processes, the ones involving multipole moments up to mass and current octupoles, which mix also with quadrupoles of opposite parity, contribute to the system dynamics at sixth post-Newtonian order; we display these terms explicitly as a particular case of our general derivation. Additionally, we derive the radiative multipole moments associated to arbitrary angular momentum failed-tails in emission processes.

### [111] [On tt*-structures from $ADE$-type Stokes data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19871)
*Tadashi Udagawa*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 该研究为Cecotti和Vafa引入的拓扑反拓扑融合（tt*）方程提供了严格的解析框架，实现了ADE分类的严谨数学表述，揭示了Stokes矩阵、$\tilde{Br}_n$群作用与Cartan矩阵之间的深刻联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cecotti和Vafa引入的拓扑反拓扑融合（tt*）方程描述了超对称共形场论（supersymmetric conformal field theories）的大质量形变（massive deformations）。该研究旨在为tt*结构的ADE分类提供严格的解析表述（rigorous analytic formulation），澄清Stokes现象、$\tilde{Br}_n$对称性与Cartan型矩阵正定性之间的相互作用。

Method: 在自然结构假设下，$\mathbb{C}^*$上的tt*结构可通过具有上单位三角实Stokes矩阵（upper unitriangular real Stokes matrices）的等单值形变（isomonodromic deformations）描述。研究处理了两个核心问题：由重排操作生成的$\tilde{Br}_n$群作用所控制的Stokes矩阵模糊性，以及相关Riemann-Hilbert问题的可解性。

Result: 第一个主要结果表明分类可约化为模$\tilde{Br}_n$作用的容许Stokes矩阵，且Stokes矩阵的$\tilde{Br}_n$轨道决定了$\mathbb{C}^*$上的tt*结构。第二个主要结果证明，其对称化与$A_n, D_n, E_6, E_7, E_8$型Cartan矩阵一致的上单位三角矩阵可产生$\mathbb{C}^*$上的tt*结构。

Conclusion: 该研究为ADE分类提供了直接的解析实现（direct analytic realization），阐明了Stokes现象、$\tilde{Br}_n$对称性与Cartan型矩阵正定性之间的相互作用。这一框架将物理理论与严格的数学结构联系起来，深化了对tt*方程及其分类的理解。

Abstract: Cecotti and Vafa introduced the topological anti-topological fusion (tt*)-equation, whose solutions describe massive deformations of supersymmetric conformal field theories. We provide a rigorous analytic formulation of the $ADE$ classification of tt*-structures. Under natural structural assumptions, a tt*-structure over $\mathbb{C}^*$ can be described via isomonodromic deformations with upper unitriangular real Stokes matrices. Two fundamental issues arise: the ambiguities of Stokes matrices, governed by an action of a group $\tilde{Br}_n$, which is generated by reordering operations, and the solvability of the associated Riemann-Hilbert problem. Our first main result shows that the classification reduces to admissible Stokes matrices modulo $\tilde{Br}_n$-action, and that the $\tilde{Br}_n$-orbit of a Stokes matrix determines a tt*-structure over $\mathbb{C}^*$. Our second main result establishes that upper unitriangular matrices whose symmetrizations coincide with Cartan matrices of type $A_n, D_n, E_6, E_7,$ or $E_8$ give rise to tt*-structures over $\mathbb{C}^*$. This provides a direct analytic realization of the $ADE$ classification and clarifies the interplay between Stokes phenomena, $\tilde{Br}_n$-symmetry, and positivity of Cartan-type matrices.

### [112] [Transient Thermodynamic Efficiency of Adaptive Inference in Continuously Nonstationary Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19324)
*Aditya Gupta*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了非平稳环境中自适应系统的热力学学习过程，发现快速环境变化期间会出现瞬态学习效率峰值，表明最大热力学学习性能出现在瞬态而非稳态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自适应物理和生物系统持续处理来自环境的波动信息。当环境非平稳时，推断本身成为具有热力学成本的非平衡过程，需要研究这种自适应学习的热力学特性。

Method: 采用一个最小随机模型：处于自适应双阱势中的过阻尼粒子，其控制参数跟踪漂移的Ornstein-Uhlenbeck信号。使用随机热力学推导熵产生、互信息率和时变学习效率的显式表达式，并通过高精度Langevin模拟进行验证。

Result: 高精度Langevin模拟揭示了快速环境变化期间学习效率的瞬态峰值，这些峰值在稳态平均中不存在。结果表明瞬态自适应机制是信息到能量转换的最大时刻。

Conclusion: 最大热力学学习性能出现在瞬态而非稳态，突显了瞬态自适应机制在信息-能量转换中的重要性。环境被视为外部驱动的随机信号而非热力学子系统，其固有熵产生被排除在热力学核算之外。

Abstract: Adaptive physical and biological systems continually process fluctuating information from their environments. When the environment is nonstationary, inference itself becomes a nonequilibrium process with thermodynamic cost. We analyse a minimal stochastic model which is an overdamped particle in an adaptive double well potential whose control parameter tracks a drifting Ornstein Uhlenbeck signal. Using stochastic energetics, we derive explicit expressions for entropy production, mutual information rate, and a time dependent learning efficiency. High precision Langevin simulations reveal transient peaks in learning efficiency during rapid environmental shifts, absent in steady state averages. These results identify transient adaptive regimes as moments of maximal information to energy conversion, highlighting that maximal thermodynamic learning performance arises transiently rather than in steady state. Throughout this work, the environment is treated as an externally driven stochastic signal rather than a thermodynamic subsystem under control, and its intrinsic entropy production is therefore excluded from the thermodynamic accounting.

</details>


### [113] [Logarithmic growth of operator entanglement in a clean non-integrable circuit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19363)
*Mao Tian Tan,Tomaž Prosen*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了半遍历砖墙双幺正电路（semi-ergodic brickwork dual-unitary circuits）在有限大体积系统中的中长时间动力学行为。研究发现，尽管模型是非可积且无淬火无序的，但算符纠缠（operator entanglement）随时间呈对数增长，自相关函数（auto-correlation function）可用SO(3)矩阵乘积和描述，算符大小分布（operator size distribution）在某些时刻呈双峰分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨半遍历砖墙双幺正电路中，在无限体积极限下沿一条光锥（light ray）呈现遍历行为而沿另一条光锥呈现非遍历行为的系统，在有限大体积情况下的中长时间动力学特性。

Method: 研究方法包括分析有限大体积系统中的海森堡演化（Heisenberg evolution），将单迹零单点算符（single traceless single-site operator）的时间演化映射为单个qutrit与一系列qubit顺序散射的简化问题。

Result: 主要结果包括：算符纠缠随时间呈对数增长，与先前预期相反；自相关函数可表示为SO(3)矩阵乘积和，允许在晚时进行随机矩阵预测；算符大小分布在特定时刻呈现双峰分布，显示介于混沌系统和自由系统之间的中间行为。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，这种非可积且无淬火无序的模型表现出非典型的动力学行为：算符纠缠对数增长、自相关函数可用随机矩阵理论描述、算符大小分布呈现双峰特征，揭示了介于混沌和自由系统之间的中间动力学相。

Abstract: We study a so-called semi-ergodic brickwork dual-unitary circuits where, in the infinite volume limit, the two-point correlation functions of single-site operators exhibit ergodic behavior along one light ray and non-ergodic behavior along the other light ray. Here, however, we study intermediate and long-time dynamics of a system in a finite, large volume. Under such dynamics, the Heisenberg evolution of a single traceless single-site operator lies within a restricted subspace, and this time evolution can be mapped to a simpler problem of a single qutrit scattering with a bunch of qubits sequentially. Despite the model being non-integrable and free from any quenched disorder, the operator entanglement grows at most logarithmic in time, contrary to prior expectations. The auto-correlation function can be written in terms of a sum of products of $SO(3)$ matrices, allowing for a random matrix prediction for the auto-correlation function at late times. The operator size distribution also becomes bimodal at certain times, displaying intermediate behavior between chaotic and free systems.

</details>

Result: 研究结果表明，基于独立翻转自旋弦的可解随机模型能够正确描述转变点附近临界标度区域（critical scaling regime）内的弛豫行为以及弦长分布。广义标度形式（generalized scaling forms）能够捕捉更广泛磁单极子密度范围内的行为。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了翻转自旋弦的播种和生长机制能够描述经典自旋冰的动力学行为，并阐明了远离临界点时标度图像（scaling picture）的失效机制。

Abstract: We study dynamics in classical spin ice following a magnetic field quench to close to the Kasteleyn transition, using Monte Carlo simulations and dynamic scaling theory to characterize the relaxation of the magnetization and the density of magnetic monopoles. We have previously argued that this dynamics can be described in terms of seeding and growth of strings of flipped spins, and our results here demonstrate that a solvable stochastic model based on independent strings correctly describes the relaxation as well as the distribution of string lengths within the critical scaling regime near the transition. We also show how generalized scaling forms capture the behavior over a broader range of monopole densities and provide a clear understanding of the breakdown of the scaling picture further from the critical point.

### [115] [Operational Emergence of a Global Phase under Time-Dependent Coupling in Oscillator Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05668)
*Veronica Sanz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在时变耦合的振子网络中，全局相位何时能成为操作上明确定义的宏观坐标。研究者提出了基于相位滞后涨落的操作涌现判据，并分析了非自治耦合中斜坡时间尺度与弛豫的竞争关系，揭示了网络拓扑对同步过程的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 集体同步通常用复序参量 $R e^{iΨ}$ 描述，但全局相位 $Ψ$ 作为有意义的宏观坐标的操作明确定义性（operationally well-defined）在时变耦合网络中尚不明确。本研究旨在探究在耦合随时间变化的振子网络中，全局相位何时能成为操作上明确定义的宏观坐标。

Method: 研究采用阻尼（可选惯性）相振子模型，考虑时变耦合 $K(t)$ 的图结构，涵盖标准 Kuramoto 动力学作为极限情况。提出基于规范固定相位滞后涨落的操作涌现判据，利用拉普拉斯模态约化（Laplacian-mode reduction）在相干态附近进行分析，并通过数值模拟提取基于能量的跟踪诊断的操作冻结时间。

Result: 研究建立了由 $NR^2$ 控制的定量阈值，解释了为何 $Ψ$ 在非相干态中即使形式可定义也病态。非自治耦合引入的斜坡时间尺度与弛豫竞争，当 $K(t)λ_2$ 主导斜坡速率时排序跟踪协议，而更快斜坡导致冻结。在非空间网络中，冻结时的残余非相干性随谱协议参数 $λ_2τ$ 呈现坍缩现象，而在周期晶格中拓扑扇区和缺陷介导排序阻碍完全对齐。

Conclusion: 全局相位的操作明确定义性需要满足基于相位滞后涨落的定量涌现判据。时变耦合中的同步过程受斜坡时间尺度与弛豫竞争的影响，网络拓扑结构（特别是空间与非空间网络）对同步动力学产生系统性差异，导致协议依赖的长寿命部分同步态。

Abstract: Collective synchronization is often summarized by a complex order parameter $R e^{iΨ}$, implicitly treating the global phase $Ψ$ as a meaningful macroscopic coordinate. Here we ask when $Ψ$ becomes \emph{operationally well-defined} in oscillator networks whose coupling varies in time. We study damped (and optionally inertial) phase-oscillator models on graphs with time-dependent coupling $K(t)$, covering standard Kuramoto dynamics as a limit and including network and spatial topologies relevant to engineered settings.
  We propose an operational emergence criterion: a macroscopic phase is emergent only when it is robustly estimable, which we quantify via gauge-fixed phase-lag fluctuations under weak noise and finite sampling. This yields a quantitative threshold controlled by $NR^2$ and makes explicit why $Ψ$ is ill-posed in incoherent states even when formally definable. Nonautonomous coupling introduces a ramp timescale that competes with relaxation. Using a Laplacian-mode reduction near coherence, we derive a graph-spectral rate criterion: ordering tracks the protocol when $K(t)λ_2$ dominates the ramp rate, while faster ramps induce freeze-out. Numerically, we extract an operational freeze-out time from an energy-based tracking diagnostic and show that, for non-spatial networks, the residual incoherence at freeze-out collapses when plotted against the spectral protocol parameter $λ_2τ$ across Erdős--Rényi and small-world graph families. Finally, on periodic lattices we show that topological sectors and defect-mediated ordering obstruct complete alignment, leading to protocol-dependent, long-lived partially synchronized states and systematic deviations from spectral collapse.

### [116] [Level 2.5 large deviations and uncertainty relations for self-interacting jump processes: tilting constructions and the emergence of time-scale separation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19411)
*Francesco Coghi,Juan P. Garrahan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于指数倾斜构造（exponential tilting construction）推导了具有一般函数依赖性的SIJPs的"level-2.5"大偏差原理。该方法揭示了微观动力学的快速时间尺度与跃迁速率记忆驱动演化的慢时间尺度之间的分离，并通过指数折扣大偏差率泛函表达。

Result: 建立了经验占据测度（empirical occupation measure）与通量矩阵（flux matrix）联合涨落的变分框架。利用该框架推导出动力学和热力学不确定性关系（kinetic and thermodynamic uncertainty relations），将经典马尔可夫界限扩展到非马尔可夫系统。

Conclusion: 所发展的变分框架为分析具有记忆效应的非马尔可夫系统提供了理论基础，推导的不确定性关系在简单示例中展示了良好性能，扩展了经典马尔可夫理论在非马尔可夫动力学中的应用范围。

Abstract: Self-interacting jump processes (SIJPs) describe systems with non-Markovian stochastic dynamics in which transition rates depend on empirical observables of the process, which gives rise to long-range memory and feedback. We derive the ``level-2.5'' large deviation (LD) principle governing the joint fluctuations of empirical occupation measure and the flux matrix for a broad class of SIJPs with general functional dependence on an empirical observable. The derivation is based on an exponential tilting construction and reveals a separation between a faster timescale of the microscopic dynamics and a slower timescale of the memory-driven evolution of transition rates, which is expressed through an exponentially discounted LD rate functional. Using this variational framework, we derive kinetic and thermodynamic uncertainty relations that extend classical Markovian bounds to non-Markovian systems, and illustrate their performance with simple examples.

Abstract: Cellular metabolic networks exhibit scale-free topologies with power-law degree distributions across diverse organisms. We show that the metabolic-starvation transition observed under nutrient-poor conditions for homogeneous degree distributions disappears when the out-degree distribution is scale-free. ### [119] [Pareto fronts and trade-off relations from exact multi-objective optimization of thermal machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19885)
*José A. Almanza-Marrero,Édgar Roldán,Gonzalo Manzano*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热机性能通常由多个相互竞争的指标（如功率、效率、能量耗散和抗噪声能力）共同表征，需要多目标优化（multi-objective optimization）方法来研究不可逆线性响应（irreversible linear-response）区域内的最佳热机性能。

Method: 研究推导了热机性能指标（平均提取功率P、效率η、熵产Σ和功率波动幅度σ²_P）在任意权重分配下的最优帕累托前沿的精确解析参数化方法，并分析了内可逆热机的普适几何结构。

Result: 内可逆热机的帕累托前沿具有普适几何结构：二、三、四目标权衡遵循与热机物理参数无关的解析公式。这些普适热力学帕累托前沿也为非内可逆热机性能设定了定量基本极限。

Conclusion: 该研究的多目标优化框架不仅适用于线性响应区域，还能应用于不同物理尺度的实验数据，包括单原子引擎、胶体系统、宏观引擎和发电厂等系统。

Abstract: Thermal machines are physical systems that, when fueled by input energy, perform output tasks such as heat pumping or the production of work. Their performance is characterized with several, often competing quantities, such as power, efficiency, energy waste, and resilience to environmental noise. Multi-objective optimization provides a key tool to investigate the characterization of the best thermal machines operating in the irreversible linear-response regime. Here, we derive exact analytical parameterizations for the optimal (Pareto) fronts associated with any given choice of relative weights assigned to their mean extracted power $P$, efficiency $η$, entropy production $Σ$ and the amplitude of power fluctuations $σ^2_P$. The geometry of the front of endoreversible machines is universal: two-, three-, and four-objective trade-offs follow analytical formulae that do not depend on the value of any physical parameter of the machine. We show that such universal thermodynamic Pareto fronts also set quantitative fundamental limits for the performance of non-endoreversible machines. Furthermore, we demonstrate that our results apply to existing experimental data from different physical systems also beyond the linear regime, ranging from atomic to macroscopic scales, including single-atom engines, colloidal systems, macroscopic engines and power plants.

### [120] [Macroscopic Mpemba Effect from Cumulative-Heat-Enhanced Relaxation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19887)
*Yun-Qian Lin,Z. C. Tu,Yu-Han Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从线性不可逆热力学出发，提出了一个包含初始状态记忆的广义牛顿冷却定律，该理论能够解释姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect）等反常弛豫行为，并预测不完全热化现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect）——即较热的系统冷却更快——缺乏普适的宏观理论解释。本文旨在从线性不可逆热力学出发，建立能够解释此类反常弛豫行为的理论框架。

Method: 基于线性不可逆热力学，构建了一个广义牛顿冷却定律，其形式为 $\mathrm{d}ΔT/\mathrm{d}t = -[γ_0 + \mathcal{M}Q(t)][ΔT - \mathcal{I}Q(t)]$。其中 $γ_0$ 为裸弛豫率，累积热交换 $Q(t)$ 显式编码了初始状态记忆，系数 $\mathcal{M}$ 和 $\mathcal{I}$ 源于热流与结构演化的相互作用。

Result: 研究发现 $\mathcal{M} > 0$ 诱导姆潘巴效应，$\mathcal{M} < 0$ 诱导逆姆潘巴效应（inverse Mpemba effect），而 $\mathcal{I}$ 导致非零渐近温度差 $ΔT$，预测了不完全热化现象。该理论捕捉了记忆依赖弛豫的全谱行为。

Conclusion: 该理论框架将复杂系统中的动力学加速与结构冻结联系起来，为理解姆潘巴效应等反常热弛豫现象提供了普适的宏观理论解释。

Abstract: The counterintuitive Mpemba effect, wherein a hotter system cools faster, critically lacks a universal macroscopic theory. Here, starting from linear irreversible thermodynamics, we formulate a generalized Newton's cooling law for the system-reservoir temperature difference $ΔT$, given by $\mathrm{d}ΔT/\mathrm{d}t = -[γ_0 + \mathcal{M}Q(t)][ΔT - \mathcal{I}Q(t)]$, where $γ_0$ is the bare relaxation rate, and the cumulative heat exchange $Q(t)$ explicitly encodes initial-state memory. The coefficients $\mathcal{M}$ and $\mathcal{I}$, arising from the interplay between heat flux and structural evolution, govern diverse anomalous relaxation behaviors. Specifically, $\mathcal{M} > 0$ ($\mathcal{M} < 0$) induces the (inverse) Mpemba effect, while $\mathcal{I}$ imposes a non-vanishing asymptotic $ΔT$, predicting incomplete thermalization. Our findings capture the full spectrum of memory-dependent relaxation, bridging kinetic speedup with structural freezing in complex systems.

</details>


### [121] [Strong Violation of the Thermodynamic Uncertainty Relation in a Minimal Autonomous Heat Engine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20041)
*Enrique P. Cital,Viktor Holubec*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文展示了一个最小自主热机模型在长时间热力学不确定性关系（TUR）方面存在强烈违反，该模型由离散棘轮和欠阻尼谐振子组成，在时间尺度分离条件下可解析求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热力学不确定性关系（thermodynamic uncertainty relations, TURs）在自主稳态中对电流精度和熵产生施加了普遍权衡，限制了热机的功率、效率和恒定性。然而，该研究旨在探索TUR的违反情况。

Method: 构建了一个最小自主热机模型，包含离散棘轮（discrete ratchet）产生对抗恒定偏置的功，以及作为内部随机控制的欠阻尼谐振子（underdamped harmonic oscillator）。在时间尺度分离（time-scale separation）条件下，模型变得可精确求解。

Result: 在时间尺度分离条件下，获得了TUR比率的闭合解析表达式，其中连续自由度的影响完全由振荡器零交叉（oscillator zero crossings）的Fano因子（Fano factor）捕获。研究表明，随着内部控制变得越确定，TUR比率可任意接近零，而热机在接近最大电流和效率下运行。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了在最小自主热机模型中长时间TUR的强烈违反，在适当极限下模型可简化为Pietzonka的经典摆钟系统（pendulum-clock system），揭示了内部确定性控制如何驱动TUR比率趋近于零。

Abstract: Thermodynamic uncertainty relations (TURs) impose a universal trade-off between current precision and entropy production in autonomous steady states, constraining in particular the power, efficiency, and constancy of heat engines. We demonstrate strong violations of the long-time TUR in a minimal autonomous heat engine composed of a discrete ratchet generating work against a constant bias and an underdamped harmonic oscillator acting as an internal stochastic control. In the regime of time-scale separation, the model becomes exactly solvable and yields a closed analytical expression for the TUR ratio, where the influence of the continuous degree of freedom is fully captured by the Fano factor of oscillator zero crossings. We show that increasingly deterministic internal control drives the TUR ratio arbitrarily close to zero while the engine operates near maximal current and efficiency. In an appropriate limit, the model reduces to the classical pendulum-clock system of Pietzonka, Phys. Rev. Lett. 128, 130606 (2022).

</details>


### [122] [Edge Currents Shape Condensates in Chiral Active Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20064)
*Boyi Wang,Patrick Pietzonka,Frank Jülicher*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一个二维手性活性晶格气体模型，揭示了手性活性物质在低温下会凝聚成具有手性取向和晶面状形状的凝聚体，界面边缘存在持久、单向且角度依赖的电流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性活性物质（chiral active matter）在生物系统中普遍存在，它同时打破了宇称对称性（parity symmetry）和时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）。研究此类系统对于理解生物系统中的自组织现象具有重要意义。

Method: 首先引入了一个最小化的二维手性活性晶格气体模型（chiral active lattice gas），通过结合随机、有偏的局部旋转。随后提出了一个连续统理论（continuum theory），通过在Model B中添加一个活性手性边缘电流项（active chiral edge current term）。

Result: 在低温下，系统粗化成具有手性取向和晶面状晶体形状的凝聚体（condensates）。界面以特征角度相对于晶格轴排列，并表现出持久、单向且角度依赖的边缘电流（edge currents）。具有n重对称性的边缘电流产生形状类似于正n边形（regular n-sided polygons）的凝聚体。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了活性手性输运（active chiral transport）在相分离界面动力学中的关键作用。在薄界面极限（thin-interface limit）下构建的有效界面势（effective interface potential）能够从晶格模型和连续统描述中获得稳态凝聚体几何形状。

Abstract: Chiral active matter, which breaks both parity symmetry and time-reversal symmetry, is ubiquitous in living systems. Here, we introduce a minimal two-dimensional chiral active lattice gas by incorporating stochastic, biased local rotations. At low temperatures, the system coarsens into condensates with chiral orientations and faceted, crystal-like shapes. The interfaces align at characteristic angles with respect to the lattice axes and exhibit edge currents that are persistent, unidirectional, and angle-dependent. To generalise these findings, we propose a continuum theory by adding an active chiral edge current term to Model B, which reveals the essential role of active chiral transport in the interfacial dynamics of phase separation. Edge currents with $n$-fold symmetry produce condensates whose shapes resemble regular $n$-sided polygons. In the thin-interface limit, we construct an effective interface potential governing edge currents, from which the steady-state condensate geometry can be obtained, both in the lattice model and the continuum description.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法采用三维卷积神经网络自编码器（3D convolutional neural network autoencoder, CAE），仅使用零温度基态构型进行训练，然后将训练好的模型应用于宽温度范围和不同晶格尺寸的蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）构型。

Result: 结果显示均方重构误差对相变敏感，通过重构误差磁化率的峰值位置进行有限尺寸标度分析，得到临界温度Tc=4.5128(58)和关联长度临界指数ν=0.63(27)，与文献结果一致。

Abstract: We develop a one-class, deep-learning framework to detect the phase transition and recover critical behavior of the 3D Ising model. After training, the model is applied to Monte Carlo configurations across a wide temperature range and different lattice sizes. The mean-square reconstruction error is shown to be sensitive to the transition. Finite-size scaling of the peak location for the reconstruction error susceptibility yields the critical temperature $T_c=4.5128(58)$ and the correlation-length critical exponent $ν=0.63(27)$, consistent with results from the literature. Our results show that a one-class CAE, trained on zero-temperature configurations only, can recover nontrivial critical behavior of the 3D Ising model.

Abstract: We establish explicit means via which natural dilations of completely positive (CP) maps can be constructed à la Kraus's IInd representation theorem. To obtain this, we rely on the Choi-Jamiołkowski correspondence and develop a Cholesky algorithm for bi-partite systems. This enables a canonical construction of adjoint actions which recover the behaviour of the original CP-maps. Our results hold under separability assumptions and the requirement that the maps are completely bounded and preserve the subideal of finite rank operators.

### [125] [Physics-Informed Long-Range Coulomb Correction for Machine-learning Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20007)
*Yang Zhong,Xiwen Li,Xingao Gong,Hongjun Xiang*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 该研究开发了HamGNN-LR框架，通过结合变分分解的闭式长程哈密顿矩阵元与E(3)-等变消息传递，解决了机器学习电子哈密顿量中长程库仑相互作用的缺失问题，显著提升了极性晶体和异质结构中的物理预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器学习电子哈密顿量（machine-learning electronic Hamiltonians）虽然比密度泛函理论（density-functional theory）快几个数量级，但现有模型忽略了长程库仑相互作用（long-range Coulomb interactions），而这些相互作用在极性晶体和异质结构中起着关键作用。

Method: 通过静电能的变分分解（variational decomposition of the electrostatic energy），在非正交原子轨道基组中推导了闭式长程哈密顿矩阵元，建立了从电子密度矩阵到有效原子电荷的变分一致映射。该框架在HamGNN-LR中实现，采用双通道架构结合E(3)-等变消息传递（E(3)-equivariant message passing）与倒空间埃瓦尔德求和（reciprocal-space Ewald summation）。

Result: 基准测试表明，基于物理的长程修正至关重要：纯数据驱动的注意力机制无法捕捉宏观静电势。在极性ZnO板、CdSe/ZnS异质结构和GaN/AlN超晶格上的测试显示，误差降低了2-3倍，并且对远超出训练尺寸的系统具有鲁棒的可迁移性，消除了短程模型在内建电场中特有的阶梯状伪影（staircase artifacts）。

Conclusion: HamGNN-LR框架通过物理驱动的长程修正显著提升了机器学习电子哈密顿量在极性系统和异质结构中的预测精度和可迁移性，解决了现有短程模型的根本局限性。

Abstract: Machine-learning electronic Hamiltonians achieve orders-of-magnitude speedups over density-functional theory, yet current models omit long-range Coulomb interactions that govern physics in polar crystals and heterostructures. We derive closed-form long-range Hamiltonian matrix elements in a nonorthogonal atomic-orbital basis through variational decomposition of the electrostatic energy, deriving a variationally consistent mapping from the electron density matrix to effective atomic charges. We implement this framework in HamGNN-LR, a dual-channel architecture combining E(3)-equivariant message passing with reciprocal-space Ewald summation. Benchmarks demonstrate that physics-based long-range corrections are essential: purely data-driven attention mechanisms fail to capture macroscopic electrostatic potentials. Benchmarks on polar ZnO slabs, CdSe/ZnS heterostructures, and GaN/AlN superlattices show two- to threefold error reductions and robust transferability to systems far beyond training sizes, eliminating the characteristic staircase artifacts that plague short-range models in the presence of built-in electric fields.

### [126] [Cosmological forecast from the full-sky angular power spectrum and bispectrum of 21cm intensity mapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20160)

This represents the first forecast analysis using the full-sky relativistic bispectrum in redshift space for these surveys. Our results show that the second-order velocity contribution, often neglected under the Limber approximation, accounts for approximately $24\%$ of the total signal at low redshifts, indicating that it must be included for accurate modeling. Using these forecasts, we find that while the bispectrum provides constraints comparable to the angular power spectrum for $Λ$CDM and ${\rm w}$CDM models, it becomes a powerful probe of dynamical dark energy. Restricting the analysis to linear scales, we show that the inclusion of the bispectrum yields a substantial improvement in the determination of the Chevallier-Polarski-Linder (CPL) parameters. ### [128] [Crossover and Critical Behavior in the Layered XY Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19351)
*Roman Kracht,Andrea Trombettoni,Ilaria Maccari,Nicolò Defenu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过蒙特卡洛模拟三维经典XY模型，系统分析了各向异性耦合对层状超导体中二维与三维标度特征交叉的影响，揭示了拓扑标度特征在强各向异性条件下持续存在，直至系统尺寸超过交叉长度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于非常规层状超导体中观测到的二维与三维标度特征之间的相互作用。作者旨在通过系统研究各向异性耦合的三维经典XY模型，阐明从准二维拓扑标度到真正三维临界行为的交叉现象。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）方法研究三维经典XY模型，该模型包含面内耦合$J_\parallel$和面间耦合$J_\perp$的各向异性。研究特别关注了先前未探索的极小系统各向异性值$Δ=J_\perp /J_\parallel$，并重点表征从准二维拓扑标度到真正三维临界行为的交叉过程。

Result: 临界温度的数值结果明确揭示了与$Δ$的对数标度关系，这直接关联于二维极限下的拓扑标度。尽管层状XY临界性具有三维本质，但拓扑标度特征在系统尺寸达到交叉长度$\ell_J$时仍持续存在，而$\ell_J$在小$Δ$条件下以类似于Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）相变的标度行为发散。这表明真正的三维对称破缺行为仅在系统尺寸极大且各向异性极强时才显现。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，需要新的实验证据来阐明层状强关联材料中观测到的临界特征在多大程度上受到其显著各向异性的影响。拓扑标度特征在强各向异性条件下持续存在，直至系统尺寸超过交叉长度，这挑战了对这些材料临界行为的传统理解。

Abstract: Motivated by the interplay between 2D and 3D scaling signatures observed in unconventional layered superconductors, we present a systematic Monte Carlo study of the three-dimensional classical XY model with anisotropic in-plane $J_\parallel$ and inter-plane $J_\perp$ couplings. Our study includes very small values of the system anisotropy $Δ=J_\perp /J_\parallel$ not studied before, and focuses on characterizing the crossover from quasi-2D topological scaling to genuine 3D critical behavior. The numerical results for the critical temperature unambiguously reveal a logarithmic scaling with $Δ$, directly related to the topological scaling in the 2D limit. Despite the 3D nature of the layered XY criticality, topological scaling signatures survive up to system sizes comparable to the crossover length $\ell_J$, which diverges at small $Δ$ with a scaling behavior reminiscent of the Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless (BKT) transition. This shows that genuine 3D symmetry-breaking behavior emerges only at exceedingly large system sizes when the anisotropy is very strong. Our results indicate that new experimental evidence is required to clarify the extent to which the critical signatures observed in layered strongly correlated materials are shaped by their pronounced anisotropy.

</details>


### [129] [$Δ_T$ Noise, Quantum Shot Noise, and Thermoelectric Clues to the Pairing Puzzle in Iron Pnictides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20069)
*A Rajmohan Dora,Sachiraj Mishra,Colin Benjamin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究提出利用温度驱动噪声（Δ_T噪声）作为区分铁基超导体中S_{++}和S_{+-}配对对称性的新探针，结合热电电压、塞贝克系数和量子噪声测量，形成互补的探测手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子噪声（quantum noise）长期以来是介观结中量子输运的重要探针。最近，温度驱动噪声（Δ_T噪声）因其在无平均电荷电流时仍存在的特性而受到关注。铁基超导体中S_{++}和S_{+-}配对对称性的区分是重要研究课题。

Method: 研究采用正常金属-绝缘体-铁基超导体结（normal metal-insulator-iron-pnictide junction），系统分析热电电压（thermovoltage）、塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient）、零温量子散粒噪声（zero temperature quantum shot noise）、有限温量子噪声（finite temperature quantum noise）以及Δ_T噪声对不同配对对称性的响应特征。

Result: Δ_T噪声显示出显著的对称性依赖特征：S_{++}配对对称性呈现双峰结构（twin-peak structure），而S_{+-}态呈现单峰轮廓（single-peak profile）。类似地，零温量子散粒噪声和有限温量子噪声中，S_{++}态始终呈现双峰结构，S_{+-}态呈现单峰响应。热电电压和塞贝克系数对两种配对对称性显示符号反转（sign reversals），且在S_{++}和S_{+-}情况下呈现相反趋势。

Conclusion: 噪声测量与塞贝克系数、热电电压构成相互强化的探测组合，能够可靠识别铁基超导体中的超导能隙对称性。Δ_T噪声作为区分S_{++}和S_{+-}配对对称性的新型探针，提供了比电导测量更丰富的定性特征。

Abstract: Quantum noise has long served as a powerful probe of quantum transport in mesoscopic junctions. Recently, temperature-driven noise, or $Δ_T$ noise, has attracted growing interest due to its presence even in the absence of average charge current. In this work, we investigate a normal metal-insulator-iron-pnictide junction and demonstrate how thermovoltage, Seebeck coefficient, zero temperature quantum shot noise, finite temperature quantum noise, and $Δ_T$ noise can discriminate between $S_{++}$ and $S_{+-}$ pairing symmetries, which are relevant to iron-based superconductors. We introduce $Δ_T$ noise as a novel probe for distinguishing between the two pairing symmetries. In contrast to conductance, which exhibits a single peak for both $S_{++}$ and $S_{+-}$ states with only a difference in magnitude, the $Δ_T$ noise reveals qualitatively distinct features: a twin-peak structure for the $S_{++}$ pairing symmetry and a single-peak profile for the $S_{+-}$ state. A similar symmetry-dependent contrast is observed in both zero temperature quantum shot noise and finite temperature quantum noise, where the $S_{++}$ state consistently exhibits a twin-peak structure, while the $S_{+-}$ state shows a single-peak response. Furthermore, both the thermovoltage and the Seebeck coefficient display sign reversals for the two pairing symmetries, with opposite trends in the $S_{++}$ and $S_{+-}$ cases. Our results demonstrate that noise-based measurements, together with Seebeck coefficient and thermovoltage, form a mutually reinforcing set of probes that enables reliable identification of superconducting gap symmetry in Iron Pnictide superconductors.

</details>


### [130] [Lattice Dynamics of LiFeAs studied by Inelastic Neutron Scattering and Density Functional Theory calculations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19956)
*Akshay Tewari,Navid Qureshi,Rolf Heid,Andrea Piovano,Yvan Sidis,Luminita Harnagea,Sabine Wurmehl,Bernd Buchner,Markus Braden*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过非弹性中子散射实验和密度泛函理论计算，系统研究了非常规超导体LiFeAs的晶格动力学特性，揭示了其声子色散关系和电子-声子耦合强度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非常规超导体LiFeAs的晶格动力学特性，旨在通过实验和理论相结合的方法，全面了解其声子色散关系，并评估电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）在超导机制中的可能作用。

Method: 采用非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）实验和密度泛函理论（density-functional theory, DFT）计算相结合的方法，通过比较中子散射强度与晶格动力学模拟，识别主要对称方向上的所有模式的极化对称性。

Result: 实验与DFT计算结果总体上吻合良好，排除了被忽视的强电子-声子耦合的可能性；DFT计算显示平均电子-声子耦合常数较小；横向声学面内支在小的传播矢量下呈现正常色散，表明不存在向列不稳定性（nematic instability）；多个模式在冷却过程中表现出显著的硬化现象，可归因于LiFeAs晶格的各向异性收缩。

Conclusion: LiFeAs的晶格动力学特性不支持强电子-声子耦合机制，其超导性可能源于其他物理机制；实验观测到的模式硬化现象与晶格各向异性收缩相关，为进一步理解非常规超导体的微观机制提供了重要参考。

Abstract: We investigated the lattice dynamics of the unconventional superconductor LiFeAs using inelastic neutron scattering experiments and density-functional theory (DFT) calculations. By comparing the neutron scattering intensities with lattice-dynamics simulations we can identify the polarization symmetry of all modes along the main-symmetry directions yielding a complete experimental picture of the phonon dispersion. Overall there is good agreement between the experimental and DFT results, which renders an overlooked strong electron phonon coupling unlikely. Our DFT calculations reveal only a small averaged electron-phonon coupling constant. The transversal acoustic in-plane branches exhibit a normal dispersion for small propagation vectors indicating the absence of a nematic instability. Several modes exhibit considerable hardening upon cooling that can be attributed to the anisotropic shrinking of the LiFeAs lattice.

</details>


<div id='cs.DL'></div>

# cs.DL [[Back]](#toc)

### [131] [Benchmarking Cross-Scale Perception Ability of Large Multimodal Models in Material Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19327)
*Yuting Zheng,Zijian Chen,Qi Jia*

Main category: cs.DL

TL;DR: 本文提出了CSMBench数据集，用于评估大型多模态模型（LMMs）在材料科学中跨物理尺度（原子、微观、介观、宏观）的层次化推理能力，包含1,041个高质量图表，揭示了现有模型在不同尺度上的性能差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料科学的核心挑战是理解从微观到宏观的层次化结构-性能关系，但现有科学基准主要关注通用图表解释或孤立常识推理，未能捕捉跨复杂物理维度的推理能力。

Method: 研究者构建了CSMBench数据集，包含从顶级期刊（截至2025年9月）收集的1,041个高质量图表，按材料研究的定义严格分为原子、微观、介观和宏观四个尺度，通过开放式图表描述和多项选择标题匹配任务评估开源和闭源模型。

Result: 分析发现，由于不同物理尺度具有独特的视觉特征，模型性能在不同尺度上存在显著差异，突显了当前通用模型的局限性，并为材料研究中实现层次化和准确理解指明了关键方向。

Conclusion: CSMBench的发布填补了评估大型多模态模型跨物理尺度推理能力的空白，为材料科学中层次化理解的研究提供了重要基准，数据集已在Hugging Face平台公开。

Abstract: Unraveling the hierarchical structure-property relationships is the central challenge of materials science, necessitating the interpretation of data across vast physical scales from micro to macro. Despite the rapid integration of Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) into scientific workflows, existing scientific benchmarks primarily focus on general chart interpretation or isolated common-sense reasoning, failing to capture reasoning ability across intricate physical dimensions. To address this, we introduce CSMBench, a dataset comprising 1,041 high-quality figures curated from premier journals up to September 2025. CSMBench categorizes data into four scientifically distinct regimes: atomic, micro, meso, and macro scales, strictly aligning with the focus and definitions in materials study. Through open-ended figure description and multiple-choice caption matching tasks, we evaluate state-of-the-art open-source and closed-source models. Our analysis identifies that performance varies significantly across physical scales due to the distinct visual characteristics, highlighting the limitations of current generalist models and identifying critical directions for achieving hierarchical and accurate understanding in materials research. The CSMBench is publicly released at: https://huggingface.co/datasets/lututu/CSMBench.

</details>
